(The water ripples in the breeze as the seagulls fly overhead. The ubiqui-
tous windmills of this bright white world turn, their heavy creaking sound 
sailing on the air. Beneath the water, schools of fish swim in slow currents. 
High above the water, cable cars traverse over wires in the sunlight, 
clanging as they move along. At the world's central point, a grand tower 
stands. Inside the tower, the sun shines warmly on a pair of young boys 
seated at a table. The wall-length curtains ripple as the breeze wafts 
through the open window. On the table sits a game board with twenty playing 
pieces, thirteen black and seven white)

Boy in Black: Have you heard of the ancient Keyblade War?

Boy in White: Huh? Of course I have.

Boy in Black: Long ago, Keyblade wielders waged a war over the ownership 
of light.

(The Boy in Black moves one of his black pieces and takes one of the white 
pieces, as you would in a chess game)

Boy in White: Yeah, the Master's favorite story.

(The Boy in White takes a black piece with one of his white pieces)

Boy in Black: I wonder what they planned on doing with Kingdom Hearts after...
making it appear.

Boy in White: Who knows? I don't get why anyone would initiate a war.

(The boys keep playing)

Boy in Black: So...you know the "Lost Masters"?

Boy in White: Who?

Boy in Black: They're the ones who started the Keyblade War.

Boy in White: Never heard of 'em. Where'd you hear about that?

Boy in Black: Or...they're the ones for whom the war started.

Boy in White: I'm not following you.

Boy in Black: You can drop the facade.

Boy in White: Facade?

Boy in Black: "On that land shall darkness prevail and light expire." A 
prospective Keyblade Master should know this.

Boy in White: If you say so.

Boy in Black: The Gazing Eye sees the fate of the World.

(The Boy in Black looks up to a Keyblade on the wall with an eye set in 
its teeth)

The Boy in Black: The future--it's already been written.

Boy in White: Really? I'm not so sure about that.

(He picks up a white piece bearing a blank heart token)

Bow in White: Besides, who's to say I can't change it? And maybe light 
will prevail.

(The Boy in Black gives a small laugh)

Boy in Black: Pretty confident.

(He moves to claim another white piece)

Boy in Black: But things aren't in your favor.

Boy in White: Perhaps. But unlike darkness, there is more to light than 
meets the eye. You might be surprised.

(The Boy in Black smiles, peering at the other boy with his gray eyes)

Boy in Black: Oh, I hope so.

(Far into the future, Sora, Donald and Goofy meet at Yen Sid's Mysterious 
Tower. The trio stand at attention as the former Keyblade Master sits in 
his tall chair)

Yen Sid: In order to defeat Xehanort, there are allies we must gather, 
acting now to rouse them from their slumber. We have discussed this before, 
Sora.

(They nod)

Yen Sid: Your Mark of Mastery exam was conducted in the hopes you would 
acquire the power to wake them. However, the darkness nearly took control 
of you, and your grasp of your new abilities leaves much to be desired.

(Sora looks sad and Donald and Goofy share concerned faces)

Yen Sid: Furthermore, Xehanort nearly made you his vessel, and in the 
process stripped you of most of the power you had gained by then. I suspect 
you have already noticed this, correct? But first, you must regain all the 
strength you have lost. Perhaps it is foolish to expect a complete recovery, 
but it is absolutely vital you perfect one power--the power of waking, 
which you failed to master during your exam. There's someone who lost his

(Sora perks up and strikes various bodybuilding poses, to Donald's less-
than-amusement)

Yen Sid: Perhaps he can point you in the right direction.

Sora (saluting): Got it.

(The sorcerer nods)

Donald: Master Yen Sid...

Goofy: You can count on us to take care of Sora!

Yen Sid: I would have it no other way. I put Sora in your hands.

Goofy: Oh, this is gonna be lots of fun!

Sora: It's not a vacation!

(They stand at attention toward Yen Sid)

KINGDOM HEARTS II.9

Narrator: At long last, the time had come. The planets were edging into 
perfect alignment...and the plan Hades devised eighteen years ago was about 
to reach fruition. The Fates had predicted this very future--the day he 
would sieze control of Olympus and rule over all the cosmos. Hades' previous 
attempts--using Terra, Cloud, and Auron to advance his plans for conquest--
had failed. The hour was not yet right. But now the planets were aligned 
and nothing could possibly go wrong. A wave of darkness lanced down from 
their celestial rank, and one by one, Hades freed the Titans from their 
prison--some of them the same monstrosities that Sora and his friends had 
already fought and bested before. With both the Titans and his longing for 
vengeance against Zeus reinvigorated, Hades began his attack on Olympus.

Hades: Whoa, easy--what is this, Sparta? Kind of on a schedule. Don't

Hades (calling): Where are my Titans? Show me your power!

(The sky turns dark and the ground shakes. An enormous shadow looms over

Hades: Ahh! Love the breeze.

Hades: Sailing right to where I left...

One huge boulder strikes the cliff next to him, sending a rock slide 
over the edge, just a foot away. As they get closer, they enter the dark 
clouds and their view of the sun is obstructed. The Titan sees them 
getting nearer and stomps a foot against the precipice, causing a torrent 
of boulders in Sora's direction. With some quick footwork, he leaps 
from rock to rock, quickening his pace to the summit. A lit flame guides 
their way forward through a cave further ahead where they see flashes of 
light, proof that they have reached the thick of the storm clouds. 
Fighting Heartless in their path, the rain beats down in currents and 
lightning strikes the area around them. The Rock Titan, illuminated by 
the bolts in the air, hones in on the Keyblade wielder, sending a personal 
gift in his direction. It strikes just past his face, breaking the 
mountainside and blocking off the cave. For all the Titan's attempts, 
they succeed in reaching the Rock Titan. They strike at its feet, dodging 
when it tries to stomp them until cracks begin to show, causing the 
monster to fall against the mountain with a growl. With the Titan nearly 
motionless, they ascend their gigantic foe, striking at the two heads on 
its bulky body. Rain continues to pour as a power emerges from Sora in 
the shape of an illuminated train on magical roller coaster tracks. The 
trio ride in the train cars as sparks fly from the chimney of the Mountain 
Coaster. The Rock Titan attempts to punch the incoming train, but Sora 
sends a barrage of fireworks at the monster. The Titan howls and careens 
off the side of the mountain, tumbling all the way down. The three watch 
it fall)

Sora: Yes! That's one down!

Goofy: They're not so tough by themselves.

Donald: That one was dumb as a rock.

Sora: Okay! What's next?

(They follow the pathway ahead, following a cave to escape the storm. 
Bursting through a pile of rocks, they enter a bright light, finding a 
grand stairway into the clouds. Their spirits lightened, they rush up 
the stairs to a golden door and enter the Realm of the Gods)

Sora: Whoa! Is this...Olympus?

Goofy: Gawrsh, it's amazing!

(Trumpets sound suddenly, startling them)

Donald: The fanfare?

Sora: Nope!

(They summon their weapons as Heartless appear. Above the Cloud Ridge, 
Hercules demolishes Heartless aboard his trusty steed, flying toward 
the Apex. Hades has trapped Zeus, the king of the gods, in a cone of 
rock with the powers of the Ice and Lava Titans)

Zeus: I swear to you, Hades, when I get out of th--

(The lava reaches above Zeus's head and Hades summons a dark throne to 
sit and watch his handiwork)

Hades: No, I'm the one giving orders now, bolt boy.

(He sits back with a smirk)

Hercules (calling): Don't get too comfortable, Hades!

(Hades sits at alert and looks around)

Hades: Huh?

(Hercules flies in with his sword)

Sora: We're gonna stop you!

Hades: What?!

(He turns to the gates of the Apex, where Sora, Donald and Goofy brandish 
their weapons. Hercules looks down to see the other gods of Olympus in 
chains and swoops down, releasing them with his sword. Hades growls, 
bursting into red flames)

Hades (pointing): Get them!

(The Lava, Ice and Tornado Titans approach the trio)

Hercules: Sora, Donald, Goofy!

(Herc jumps down off of Pegasus and joins them)

Hercules: It's on!

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Yeah!

(They ascend the hardened lava cone to get a better vantage point of 
the Lava and Ice Titans while the Tornado Titan swirls in the wind 
around them. The Lava Titan sends out a barrage of molten liquid towards 
Sora, who dodges on the Ice Titan's side of the cone. After dealing the 
Ice Titan a blow to the face, it strikes back with a blizzard of icy 
breath in their direction. The Tornado Titan explodes in a gust of heavy 
wind, knocking the group back to the ground, making it hard to get back 
up. Combining their efforts, the Lava Titan glows red, spewing a rush of 
lava toward them as the Ice Titan focuses its energy into a beam of ice. 
Dodging upwards, they reascend the cone to continue their assault. Hercules 
grabs onto Sora's legs and spins him around like a top, using the Keyblade 
to strike at the two Titans until the Ice and Lava Titans collapse with 
exhaustion. The Tornado Titan moves in)

Sora: Just one Titan left!

(The Tornado Titan wiggles through the air, facing its vortex toward the 
group. Large pieces of debris from Thebes sail out in their direction. 
Sora dodges the flying rubble, sending spells at the whirlwind, until the 
Titan tries another approach. Branching out from its main funnel cloud, 
it aims two smaller vortices at the group, sending them high into the 
seemingly endless sky. As they fall from such a height, the Titan spits 
out more ruins toward them along with burning lava sludge and sharp ice 
crystals. Successfully dodging the barrage, Sora strikes right between 
the glowing red eyes of the Titan. Suddenly, the Rock Titan bursts through 
the clouds below with an enormous bellow. The group is surrounded, 
causing worry to grow on Donald and Goofy's faces) 

Goofy: Uh-oh! Now it's all four of them.

Sora: So what? There are four of us too.

Hercules: Actually, I think I can make it five.

(Hercules leaps to the top of the cone, attempting to pry open the 
hardened rock with his hands. With a great struggle and a burst of 
light, Zeus emerges from the open stone)

Hades: Nooo!

Zeus (smiling): Thank you, my boy.

Sora: Yeah!

(The trio rejoice and Zeus conjures a trove of lightning bolts)

Zeus (excitedly): Hah! Now, watch your old man work!

(He readies his arm and tosses a bolt at the Rock Titan, splintering 
rock from both of its heads. The Lava and Ice Titan start to head-tail 
with the other Titans following, one of the Rock Titan's heads covering 
its face. The Tornado Titan passes Hercules and he gets an idea. Running 
alongside the Titan, Herc manages to grab the tail end of the funnel. 
Spinning it, he swings the head of the vortex toward the other three 
Titans, who get sucked up into the cyclone. With a final hurl, Hercules 
sends the tornado flying into space causing a brilliant explosion. Zeus 
and Herc laugh and exchange a high-five.)

Goofy: We did it!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy share their own high-fives as Hades glares at them)

Hades: I can't believe it! I put eighteen years into that plan and you've 
blippin' ruined it! I REALLY don't like you.

(He points at them)

Sora: Just give it up already! You'll never beat Herc, no matter how many 
times you try.

Goofy: Yeah, stay in the Underworld where ya belong.

Donald: Go have the time of your afterlife.

(Hades trembles with anger)

Hades: Enough already! I did not come this far to be ridiculed by Zeusy 
high and mighty, his little sunspot, and a trio of clowns!

(He bursts into red flames)

Hades: You know what? I'll just go ahead and destroy you!

Hercules: Hades. 

(Hades stops, turning his head slowly toward Herc)

Hercules (motioning): The exit is that way.

(He looks back in the trio's direction and turns blue again with a sigh)

Hades: Oy vey... Geez Louise...

(He slowly starts walking toward the gate)

Hercules: Hold on. I almost forgot.

(Hades stops and turns back, before getting a knuckle sandwich in the face)

Hercules: That one's for trying to wreck Thebes.

(Hades clutching a hand to his face from his spot on the floor)

Hades: You'll pay for this! I have a very, VERY long memory!

(He summons a portal in the form of clouds of smoke)

Hades: I can still dunk your little Nut-Meg in a river of de--

(Zeus chucks a lightning bolt into the portal just as it closes. Later, the 
gates to the Realm of the Gods open and the trio and Hercules run out. Herc 
stops and takes a glance back)

Sora: Are you sure you want to leave all this behind?

Goofy: Isn't Olympus your home?

Donald: And your family.

Hercules: I can see my family anytime I want. If I stayed, I'd have to be 
apart from the person I love most... And that life would be empty.

(He looks at the base of the stairs where Meg is waiting)

Hercules: I finally know where I belong.

(He runs down the stairs)

Meg: Hercules...

(They share an embrace before the trio catches up)

Hercules: Sora, we never got back to your question. Can I help?

(Sora shakes his head)

Sora: Mmm, it's okay. I think I'm meant to figure it out for myself. I'll 
find my strength the way you found yours. Something to fight for...with all 
my heart. I guess you DID have the answer.

Hercules: Well, you've got heart, Sora. Just keep at it and I know you'll 
be stronger than ever.

Sora: Yeah, I might even end up stronger than YOU are.

(Sora strikes a hero pose. Goofy smiles and Donald's face drips with sarcasm)

Donald: There he goes again.

(They break into laughter. Meanwhile in the Gardens of Thebes, Pete has 
been busy digging through the ground while Maleficent oversees the job)

Pete: Are you sure this box with the Book of Prophecies is for reals? I 
think that dingbat in black was pulling your leg.

Maleficent: Be quiet and dig, you imbecile. I must find that Book of 
Prophecies and make it my own. His was the only clue we have. We cannot 
afford to dismiss it without a thorough investigation.

(Pete continues to dig)

Pete: I'm just sayin', a shot in the dark ain't gonna get us any closer to--

(He strikes something solid and looks down)

Pete: Whoa!

Maleficent: What is it? Have you found something? Show it to me at once, 
fool.

(Pete lifts a box from the ground)

Pete: Yes sir-eesy, this has gotta be that Pandora's Box Hades mentioned.

(Maleficent peers at it scornfully)

Maleficent: Leave it.

Pete: What? After all that diggin'?

Maleficent: That is not the box which I desire. We are finished with this 
world. Come.

(She walks away)

Pete: Awwwwww...

(He looks at the box sadly, before tossing it over his shoulder and 
running to catch up with Maleficent. Gazing down at them from above is Xigbar)

Xigbar: May your hear--

(Darkness. A world without light. King Mickey and Riku travel through the 
Realm of Darkness in search of Aqua. Riku stops and Mickey turns back)

Mickey: What's wrong, Riku? Are you tired? Do you need a break? We can stop.

Riku: No, just... I've been here. I should know this place. But that all 
seems like another life.

Mickey: Well, gee. Think of all you've seen! All the feelings you've felt. 
Why, you've done years of growin' in almost no time at all.

Riku: I remember my first time here. I was so scared. But now, my doubts 
and fears are gone. If anything, I feel exhilarated. And it's not because 
there's darkness in me--I know too well what that rush is like. This is 
different. And it's not adrenaline either. I know Aqua needs us...but 
I'm ready. I'm in control now. Maybe it's because you're with me this time.

(Mickey shakes his head)

Mickey: It's not me. I think it's because you've finally found inside you 
that special strength to protect what matters.

Riku: What?

Mickey: Sometimes you care so much for somebody that other feelings 
disappear. And then, there's no room for fear or doubt.

(Riku smiles, looking down at his hand)

Riku: Is that it?

(His thoughts drift to when he first held a Keyblade, when he met Terra 
at dusk on the Destiny Islands)

Riku: "Strength to protect what matters"... It reminds me of a promise 
I made.

Mickey: To who?

Riku: Just someone I once met. Can't tell.

Mickey: Sounds like a good memory.

Riku: Yeah... While we're reminicing--Mickey, does any of this look familiar?

Mickey (looking around): Sort of, but the realm of darkness has changed 
since I was here with Aqua.

Riku: Yeah, it's different from what I remember.

Mickey: Usually, I'd just follow my heart, and Aqua would show me the 
way. But the closer I get, the hazier our connection feels.

Riku: You mean...

Mickey: Maybe, but we can't give up hope.

Riku (nodding): Yeah.

(They continue on to the End of Sea, the Dark Margin, a beach in shadow. 
A light shines from far across the water)

Riku: This beach...

Mickey: It's gone...

Riku: Huh?

Mickey: I'm positive Aqua was here. But now...her trail's gone dim.

Riku: I've been here, too. With Sora.

Mickey: Really?

Riku: This is where we found our way back to the realm of light. Hey, 
maybe Aqua did, too!

(Mickey solemnly shakes his head)

Mickey: Aqua...has fallen into an even darker abyss--somewhere I can't 
see her. And I don't think we're equipped to dive any deeper than we 
already are.

Riku: So then...

(A horde of Shadow Heartless emerge from the dark sand)

Mickey: Oh no!

Riku: What?!

(They summon their Keyblades as the Shadows twitch hungrily)

Mickey: Riku...be careful. Even the least threatening Heartless are 
stronger in this realm.

Riku: I got it.

(The Heartless run past them, gathering into a huge solitary mass, the 
Demon Tower. The pillar of Shadows wriggles in the air and dives into 
the sand near them, scattering the cluster of Heartless across the 
sand. Riku and Mickey strike down several of them before they reform 
into the tower from beneath them, tossing them into the air. After a 
struggle, the tower disperses and the remaining Shadows encircle them)

Mickey: It's not over. Be careful!

(Surging from the ground, the spinning maw of the tower hones in on Riku)

Riku: Oh no!

(Riku holds an arm up to shield himself but is hit head on by the Demon Tower)

Mickey: Riku!

(The tower regains its vertical shape, spinning fiercely with no trace of 
Riku. He floats in darkness with a sensation like drowning, muffling his 
sight and his hearing)

????: Didn't expect to see you again.

Riku: What...?

????: Why did you even come here?

Riku: Because somebody needs me.

????: Do you want some help?

Riku: Who are you?

????: Me? I'm...

(Riku loses consciousness in the abyss. The next moment, he hears the 
sound of the waves)

Mickey: Riku... Wake up... Riku.

(Riku opens his eyes, seeing Mickey's sad face leaning over him. The King's 
eyes brighten into a smile)

Mickey: Are you okay?

(Riku sits up)

Riku: Where'd the Heartless go?

Mickey: I got more than half of 'em, and the rest vanished. But, they spit 
you out first.

(Riku stands, holding his head)

Riku: Thanks. I owe ya.

Mickey: I know ya feel invincible, but we're not.

Riku: Are YOU all right, Mickey?

Mickey: Yeah, thanks to the new gear. But...your Keyblade...

Riku: Oh.

(He look down at the Keyblade in his hand, which has been severed just below 
the winged teeth)

Mickey: The Heartless here are stronger than what we expected. I guess we 
probably should've powered up our Keyblades before we came in here, huh? I 
think we need to go back to Master Yen Sid's tower so we can regroup.

Riku (pausing): But Aqua's...still down here, alone. Facing enemies like 
that.

Mickey: I know...

(Riku walks to the edge of the water)

Riku: What if she's feeling as scared and alone...as I felt the first 
time I came here? How long are we supposed to keep her waiting in this 
awful place?

(Mickey walks up to him)

Mickey: But Aqua... She's like Sora.

Riku (stunned): Whaaat!?

Mickey: No no no... STRONG like Sora!

(Riku breathes a sigh of relief)

Riku: Okay... Good. Then I guess she's gonna be all right. Sora could 
fall into any darkness and swim his way out.

Mickey: Besides, we won't be long.

Riku: Right.

(Riku walks forward and plants his Keyblade into the sand)

Mickey: Huh?

Riku: Can't use THIS Keyblade anymore. Might as well leave it here...
for the other me.

Mickey: Wha...?

(Meanwhile, Sora, Donald, and Goofy revisit Master Yen Sid in his tower)

Yen Sid: I see... You could not regain your strength.

Sora: Aw, no biggie. I still learned a lot.

Yen Sid: Regardless, Sora, you will need the power of waking.

(Sora crosses his arms with a loud sigh)

Goofy: It can't be gone forever. Maybe something'll trigger it real soon.

Sora: Like, what exactly?

Donald: I know! How about a bonk on the head?

Sora: Hey!

(Sora and Donald have a staredown)

Yen Sid: Perhaps it could be something that is as simple as that.

Sora: Wait, YOU think so too?

Yen Sid: Whenever you are in need, magic happens. That is your greatest 
strength, Sora.

Sora: You make it sound like an accident.

(Sora slumps over and Donald and Goofy laugh, before they hear a knock 
at the door)

Sora: Huh?

Mickey: We're back, Master!

(The door opens and Mickey and Riku enter)

Sora (pointing): Whoa!

Mickey: Oh, wow. You guys are all here!

Sora: We were here before, but you didn't wait.

(Donald and Goofy each knock Sora aside to get to Mickey, causing him 
to fall over)

Donald & Goofy: Your Majesty!

Mickey: Hey there, fellas. So, what've you three been up to?

(Sora stands up, shaking off the fall and runs up)

Sora: We were visi--

(Donald and Goofy push him back to the floor)

Donald: We went to Olympus to visit Hercules!

Goofy: And to figure out how to get all of Sora's lost powers back.

Donald (whispering to Mickey): But...it was a big disappointment.

Mickey: Oh. What a shame. But, honestly...

Riku: We didn't fare any better.

Goofy: Did ya manage to figure out where Aqua is? 'Cause Master Yen Sid 
said that's why you fellas left.

Donald: Even a hint?

(Riku and Mickey enchange glances, before the King's face turns sad. Sora 
sits up on the floor)

Sora: Come on. Can I finally say something?

Riku: We know Master Aqua made it as far as the beach that Sora and I 
once visited, but that's where her trail ends.

(Sora stands back up and joins them)

Sora: Meaning...?

Mickey: All traces of her vanish into the great abyss...beneath the realm 
of darkness.

Donald: She's gone?

Riku: No. Sora was dragged into the abyss during his exam. And I went in 
after him. So, I think if we find someone who was really close to Aqua, 
and they make the dive, they could reach her down there.

(Mickey shakes his head sorrowfully)

Mickey: I'm not sure who's even left to ask. Ventus is hidden...and Aqua's 
the only one who knows where. Plus, nobody's seen Terra in ages. Aqua was 
the last.

Riku: So Aqua--she's gonna be the key to finding all three.

Yen Sid: Yes. Their teacher, Master Eraqus, would have been another 
possibility, had Xehanort not mercilessly struck him down.

(Yen Sid closes his eyes pensively and Sora places a hand over his heart)

Sora: I'll save her.

(Donald and Goofy jump in surprise)

Riku & Mickey: Huh?

Donald: You can't!

Goofy: But Sora, that's gonna be super hard since you don't have the 
power of waking.

Sora: Huh? Sorry... I have no idea why that just popped out.

Mickey: Well, it was pretty convincing.

Riku: Yeah, better not let us down.

(Sora nods)

Yen Sid: Sora, you must focus on regaining your lost power of waking. 
Mickey and Riku, I recall that Master Aqua journeyed to many worlds, 
and connected with others who could be the link we need.

Mickey: Good plan, sir. Riku and I will retrace her steps and see if 
we can find any sort of clues, but first...

(Mickey walks up to Yen Sid's desk)

Yen Sid: Hmm?

Mickey: We got hit pretty hard in the realm of darkness. My Keyblade was 
damaged, and the Heartless broke Riku's clean in half. So, we're gonna 
need to get replacements before we can continue.

Yen Sid: In that case, rendezvous with Kairi and Lea. They are 
continuing their training under the tutelage of the wizard Merlin.

(Mickey & Riku bow)

Mickey: Yes, sir.

Yen Sid: Also, I would like you to deliver these for me.

(He waves a hand over the table and two briefcases appear, one black & 
pink and one red)

Mickey: Are they...

Yen Sid: Yes, they are the same as the ones I gave you. Special 
vestments to shield Kairi and Lea from the darkness.

Mickey: We got 'em.

(Riku and Mickey take them in hand)

Sora (whining): What? No fair! What about my outfit, Master?

Donald: Sora, don't bug him like that. It's inconsiderate.

Yen Sid: Settle down. I have new clothes for you, too, Sora.

Sora (excitedly): Yeah?

Yen Sid: A gift from the good fairies.

(Sora laughs and Yen Sid appearifies a third briefcase)

Sora: I knew you'd come through for me. Thanks!

(Sora runs up to the table)

Yen Sid: Those are no ordinary garments, Sora.

(Sora picks it up, upside down)

Yen Sid: Like before, they have very special powers, so it took extra 
time to prepare them. In addition, there is a gift from Chip and Dale 
inside.

(Sora turns the case the right way and grabs the handle with glee)

Sora: Cool. Okay!

(He slings it over his shoulder)

Riku: Happy now?

Sora: Yup!

Yen Sid: Now, you are all ready to proceed.

(A small cricket in a top hat jumps onto the table, carrying the 
smallest of umbrellas)

Jiminy Cricket: Hey, wait! Don't forget about me!

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Jiminy!

Jiminy: Every journey worth goin' on needs a cricket to keep track of 
it. And I can't let ya start this one without ol' Jiminy Cricket by 
your side.

Goofy: The whole team's back!

Sora: Yeah.

Donald: Yeah!

Yen Sid: Good. Now, to mark the beginning of a new journey, I wish for 
you to have this, Sora.

(The sorcerer waves his hand and a purple crest appears in Sora's hand)

Sora: Okay?

Yen Sid: That is a Heartbinder. Think of it as a good luck charm made 
just for you. You have a gift, Sora, for connecting with others, and 
this makes that gift stronger.

(Sora holds the crest tight)

Mickey: It's time to go!

(The group of them stand at attention and bow)

Yen Sid (whispering): May your heart be your guiding key.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy huddle to themselves)

Goofy: See?

(Sora and Donald agree. Sora, Donald, Goofy & Jiminy leave the 
Mysterious Tower in their trusty Gummi Ship. Sora sits back in his chair 
as the ship chugs along)

Donald: Okay, where to?

Sora: Ummmmmm...

Donald: Oh, come on. Would you get serious?

Sora: Gimme a break, okay? I told you. These things take time.

Goofy: Gawrsh, is it just me, or is this turning into a routine?

(A quiet musical tune erupts inside the cockpit, surprising them)

Donald: Huh? What?

(They look around for the source of the noise. Jiminy holds a hand to his ear)

Jiminy: It's comin' from you, Sora!

Sora: Huh?

(He searches his pockets and pulls out a device with the King's symbol 
on it. The icon of a telephone ringing is displayed on the screen)

Sora: What's this?

(Donald and Goofy walk to Sora's chair to get a closer look)

Donald: Got me! Make it stop.

(Sora puts it to his ear and shakes it)

Sora: But, I don't know how. Maybe...this.

(He presses the green button on the screen and an video of Dale appears)

Dale: Hurray! He picked up.

Sora: Huh? Dale?

Dale (calling off-screen): Hey, Chipper, I finally got him! Hurry up, Chip!

(Chip runs into view)

Chip: Well, it's about time.

Sora: Chip?

Dale: Ya gotta answer the phone, Sora, or we can't give ya updates. We 
got lots and LOTS of important stuff we want to tell ya!

(Chip and Dale speak into their own phone situated on the desk in the 
Library of Disney Castle)

Chip: That's why we asked Master Yen Sid to make sure you got this 
Gummiphone we made ya. So we'd be able to stay in touch with you at all 
times.

(Dale nods, making a rectangle with his tiny fingers)

Dale: AND it takes pictures.

(Jiminy jumps onto Sora's shoulder)

Jiminy: Oh! You finally finished it. Say, with this Gummiphone, we can 
talk to each other across worlds. In fact, I might even try writing my 
journal on it.

Sora: Wow! Sounds like it's pretty handy, guys. So, what's so important?

Chip: This! Back when you and Riku quested through the Sleeping Worlds, 
Riku recovered some secret research data that Ansem the Wise hid inside you.

Dale: Ansem's Code!

Chip: Mm-hmm. We've been workin' our tails off tryin' to crack it and 
see what it says.

(The video switches to a young man in a lab coat with long gray hair 
obscuring half of his face)

?????: The data has been encrypted, so we've only deciphered some of it.

Sora: Huh?

(The man stands at the computer terminal inside Ansem's Study in Radiant 
Garden)

?????: Oh... I guess we haven't spoken since the castle. I'm Ienzo. 
Aeleus is here too.

(Aeleus walks behind Ienzo silently. He narrows his eyes and stops)
Ienzo: Aeleus, whatever's between you and Roxas, it's in the past.

(Aeleus continues walking and Ienzo sighs, turning back to the phone)

Ienzo: Sora, the reason we're here is because you and your friends 
defeated our Nobodies, thereby "recompleting" us. We cast off our hearts 
by choice, make no mistake, but we didn't know that Xemnas--or rather, 
Xehanort--was deceiving us.

Sora: Huh? Xemnas?

Goofy (hotly): Aw, he's with them!

Ienzo: Not anymore. Xemnas and Xehanort have no hold over us now. We're 
just students of the heart, exactly the same as we were before all of 
this began.

Donald: Yeah, right.

Goofy: Hmm... But ya know, now that I think about it, Axel's on our 
side now.

(Donald crosses his arms, his eyes narrowing)

Ienzo: We have friends we want to bring back to this world, just the 
same as you. To do that, we have to work together. In that spirit, Sora...

(He presses a key on the computer terminal)

Ienzo: ...we found some intriguing data in the bit of code we deciphered.

(A digital readout of Sora and his Keyblade appear on the D.T.D. screen)

Sora: Is it about me?

Ienzo: Yes. In order to piece your memories back together, our teacher, 
Ansem the Wise, look a close look at your heart. And what he found...

(Half of Sora's model on the screen flashes, bringing up red data windows)

Ienzo: ...is that your heart doesn't belong just to you.

Donald, Goofy & Jiminy: It doesn't?

Goofy: Gawrsh, you don't seem surprised.

Sora: Yeah. Honestly, I suspected as much. There's another heart inside 
mine. I think it's Roxas's. Just like Namin is still inside Kairi's.

Ienzo: Interesting... Well, no one knows your heart better than you.

(Ienzo taps his finger against the terminal)

Ienzo: To be honest, we still have a plethora of questions on our side, 
but...the idea has merit. It's incredible enough that you and your 
Nobody are able to coexist. If you share a heart...no wonder someone 
as remarkable as you caught Ansem the Wise's eye. We'll keep investigating 
based on your hypothesis. I'll be in touch.

(Ienzo ends his side of the call, and it switches back to Chip and Dale)

Dale: Okeydokey, we'll give you fellas a ring if there's anything else. 
Remember, me and Chip, the guys at Radiant Garden, and King Mickey and 
everybody are never far away.

Chip: And Jiminy, would ya do us a favor? Teach Sora how to use the 
Gummiphone.

Jiminy: Leave it to me.

(The call ends and Jiminy hops down)

Sora: I have to find Roxas and save him. The others are following Aqua's 
heart, so I'll follow Roxas's heart!

(Donald, Goofy & Jiminy nod)

Goofy: Trust the guidance that your heart gives ya, Sora. That's what 
Master Yen Sid said.

Donald: Where to?

Sora (smiling): Oh, that's easy.

(He holds out his hand and summons the Keyblade, aiming it out before 
him with a flash)

KINGDOM HEARTS III

(The group voyages across the Ocean Between and find their destination, 
a sleepy village of eternal sunset, Twilight Town. They walk casually 
down Market Street toward the Tram Common, passing clothing and 
accessory shops)

Goofy: Gawrsh, we forgot to fill Master Yen Sid in on what happened. 
Should we go back?

Donald: Typical Sora.

Sora: Hmm... You mean about Maleficent and Xigbar? No, the others 
have already got enough on their plates as it is. Why go stressing them 
out? The three of us know how to handle a couple of old adversaries, right?

Donald: Yeah, I guess...

Goofy: But doesn't that thing Pete said bother ya?

Donald: The black box?

Sora: Come on, we're talking about Pete. That means it's probably no big deal.

Goofy: I don't know...

(The tram passes in front of them, its trolley bell ringing)

Sora: Oh, cool. The trams are still here!

Donald: Sora, it hasn't been THAT long.

Sora: Feels like it.

Goofy: Maybe you're feeling what Roxas feels 'cause he misses home.

Sora: Mm-hmm. Actually, I ran into Roxas in the Sleeping Worlds. It was 
like...seeing into his heart for the first time.

Donald: And he was in the datascape, too.

Goofy: Uh-huh. It was a test to see if your data version was ready to 
face the hurt that ya carry inside.

Sora: Was I ready? I do know hurt. When I lost Riku and Kairi, and later 
when I lost the Keyblade, and you guys had to go on without me like that... 
Having no one to turn to was the worst kind of hurt. But that just shows 
how much you mean to me. Carrying around a little hurt can't be all that 
bad. Hurting is part of caring.

(Donald and Goofy share a glance)

Donald: He sounds like Data-Sora did.

Goofy: Of course. Any Sora's still Sora.

Sora: So wait... If Roxas feels something, then we're in the right place. 
Roxas, I'm gonna find you!

(Sora hears a voice, or rather, the words appear in his head)

????: Do you seek our liege?

Sora (stunned): Huh?

Donald: What is it?

(Three Dusk Nobodies appear behind Sora)

Goofy: Nobodies!

(Sora whirls around and summons the Keyblade as more appear. The fight 
the Dusks in the street until not a single one stands)

Sora: Hmm... What was that voice? I know I heard it.

Donald: I didn't hear it.

Goofy: You sure it wasn't the wind? Or somethin' else?

Sora: I'm pretty sure...

??????: Where'd they come from?!

??????: Get the ice cream later!

?????: What? Hold up!

Sora: See? Voices.

(Goofy scratches his head)

Sora: ...New ones?

(Sora spins around to see a familiar trio running in from around a corner)

Sora: What? Hayner? Pence! Olette!

(The three continue running as a monstrous wave of Shadow Heartless rushes 
in from behind them)

Goofy: What is THAT?!

(The wave gains ground on them as Hayner notices the group)

Hayner: Heeey! Sora!

(They run right past them as Sora watches)

Hayner: Hello, good-bye.

Sora: Go! We got this.

(The trio takes out their weapons as the wave spirals into the air as if 
facing them down. Sora provides several good hits on the flying swarm as 
Donald uses his magic spells, Goofy providing defense, until the Demon 
Tide flies off into the sky and away from them. Hayner, Pence, and Olette 
walk back over once the coast is clear)

Hayner: Nice fightin'! Thanks, Sora.

Sora: Hayner, Pence, Olette. It's been ages!

Hayner: What? It hasn't been THAT long.

Donald: Ya see?

Olette: Donald! Goofy! How are ya?

Donald: We're good.

Goofy (waving): Howdy there, Olette.

Pence: So does this mean that weird stuff's going down again?

Hayner (leaning in): You kidding, Pence? When have we ever seen a 
tornado of shadowy blobs before? It's not "weird." This is 
underprecedented.

Pence: Hmm, I guess it is. The creatures from the last time were bright 
white. These things must be new. Man, I can't wait to get to sleuthin'.

Olette: We're already done with the school project, silly. (to Sora) 
Whatever's going on, you wouldn't be here unless you had a good reason.

Hayner: Which is?

Sora: Well, actually, we're looking for Roxas.

Olette: Roxas?

(Hayner thinks)

Hayner: That's funny... I don't know any Roxas, but the name sounds 
familiar.

Pence: Maybe we bumped into him somewhere.

Donald: Uh, that's one way to put it.

Goofy: Actually, he mighta been friends with another version of ya.

(Goofy pulls out a photo of Hayner, Pence, Olette and Roxas standing 
in front of the Old Mansion, and hands it to Hayner)

Olette: This photograph...

Pence: Yeah. We've got the same one.

(Pence pulls out his photo, where Roxas is missing, and Hayner remembers)

Hayner: Oh yeah! The other Twilight Town!

(They compare the two)

Pence: It's like one of those "spot the differences" puzzles...except 
really easy. I guess in that town, we're friends with this "Roxas" person.

Hayner: Sora, let us help you track Roxas down.

Sora: Really?

Hayner: Sure, he seems like a pretty cool guy.

Sora (chuckling): Yeah. He is.

Pence: Great. Then let's all go ask around town. If alternate-us knew 
Roxas, then maybe alternate-other folks did too.

Olette: Mm-hmm. Sora, you three should go to the place in the photo. It's 
the old mansion. The three of us'll cover places in town.

Sora: Thanks. Oh yeah! I got this phone thingy that takes pictures.

(Sora pulls out the Gummiphone)

Sora: Want to snap a photo while we're all here?

Hayner: Sure!

Pence: That's a great idea!

(Everybody stands together in a pose)

Pence: Wait, who's taking it?

(Hayner, Sora & Donald share a bemused look. Hayner and Sora look at 
Donald. A moment later, Sora poses with Hayner, Pence and Olette while 
Donald holds the camera)

Donald: Aww! Why do I have to do it?

Sora: Hey, tough luck. You drew the short straw.

Goofy: It's okay. I'm sittin' outta the photo with ya, Donald.

Donald: Then YOU take the photograph!

(Donald shoves the phone into Goofy's hands and rejoins the group with 
a huff)

Goofy: Everybody smile. A-hyuck!

(Goofy snaps the photo and they see the result on the screen)

Pence: Wow, that came out great!

Olette: Oh! A lucky emblem.

(She points at a symbol made of the circles on the wall behind her in the 
photo)

Sora: Lucky emblem?

Olette: Oh yeah, they are HUGE right now. Supposedly, these things are 
hidden all over town. And if you get a picture of them, they'll bring 
you good luck.

(Sora, Donald & Goofy are impressed)

Sora: Cool! Wait. Look, guys! Is that...

(Sora points to the emblem, showing Donald and Goofy, whose eyes widen)

Goofy: You're right! I see it too.

Donald: Is it the King?

(Sora gives a small laugh)

Sora: I knew it.

Olette: Good luck, because they're not all this easy to find.

Hayner: Okay, we better start asking around. You start by checking 
the old mansion. We'll catch up.

Sora: Got it.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy make their way out of town through the woods. 
Walking down the beaten path, they come upon a trail of fruit)

Donald: What's that?

(Goofy looks up, seeing a small group of Powerwild Heartless in the trees)

Goofy: Heartless!

Sora: What do ya think they're up to?

(Goofy looks closer and sees a tiny rat trapped up in the tree)

Goofy (pointing): Look! On that branch. The Heartless have him surrounded!

Sora: Oh no!

Donald: Let's help!

Sora: Yeah!

(They summons their weapons and the Heartless jump down to fight. Once 
the Powerwilds are taken care of, the rat scurries down the tree toward them)

Sora: Well, take care.

(They start to walk away, leaving the rat alone with the multitude of 
fruit, some even bigger than himself. The rat sighs and runs in their 
direction. He latches onto Sora by his shoe and crawls up to his head. 
He grabs two tufts of Sora's hair and jerks them back towards the fruit. 
Sora spins uncontrollably and starts walking back the way they came, 
making very exaggerated movements)

Sora: Wh-what is--

(Donald and Goofy stop and watch)

Donald: Are you okay?

(Sora stops at an apple and the rat moves his hair downward, causing Sora 
to pick up the fruit)

Goofy: Lookie! That little feller's parked on your head.

(The rat turns Sora around)

Sora: Huuuh?

(He pulls Sora's hair upward...)

Sora: Would you cut that--

(...and then downward, picking up another apple)

Donald: Sora, you've been hijacked.

Goofy: Ya know, maybe he wants you to pick up the fruit for him.

(The rat nods, smiling)

Sora: Okay, that's fine. But I can do it by myself.

(The rat hops off Sora's head down to his hand, standing on the apple)

Sora: I just need to collect the fruit?

(The rat nods again)

Sora: Right, then.

(Moments later, the fruit is gathered into a nice big pile. Sora, Donald 
and Goofy kneel down to the rat's level)

Sora: So, what're you gonna do with all this, anyway?

(The rat makes a slicing, then swiping motion with his tiny, little arms)

Sora: Huh?

(The three exchange glances of confusion and the rat sighs)

Sora (standing): Well, okay. You be careful going home.

(They walk away)

Donald: Bye-bye!

Goofy: See ya 'round!

(The rat watches them leave, then turns back to his pile of fruit. After 
exiting the woods, the trio reach the Old Mansion. Sora looks up at the 
white curtains blowing in the window and gets a major surge of nostalgia. 
For a moment, it is not Sora looking up at the curtains, but Roxas. In 
the blink of an eye, Sora snaps out of it, feeling a sense of loss)

Sora: Whaddaya think, guys? This place is even creepier than I remember.

Goofy: Well, they do say that this mansion is haunted.

(If Donald's face wasn't already white, it would have turned it, and he 
gives off a shiver. They stare at the door, hesitant to enter when a hand 
reaches for Sora's shoulder)

??????: Hey, there.

(Sora knocks the hand away and screams, causing Donald and Goofy to jump in 
terror. Sora sees Hayner, Pence and Olette have joined them)

Sora: Thanks for the heart attack!

Hayner (smirking): Oh, what? Did I scare you?

Donald (trying to save face): Not a chance!

Olette: Our bad.

Sora: So how did it go? Did ya get any leads?

(Hayner looks toward Pence, who nods)

Pence: Nope, 'fraid not. The asking around thing was a total bust.

Hayner: Yup. This old mansion is our last hope.

(They look up at the mansion)

Olette: You guys ready?

Pence: Another Twilight Town awaits!

Sora: Yeah.

(They enter the mansion, making their way to the basement, where Pence 
spots a computer with numerous screens)

Pence: Here we go!

(He runs to the console and sits down)

Pence: The password was...uh..."sea-salt ice cream," right?

(He types the password into the computer and the D.T.D. screen appears)

Pence: Okay, I'm in. Let's get that transporter working...

(He types another command into the computer, or attempts to, when the 
screen flashes red)

Pence: Uhhh...

(He tries more keys, but only gets access errors and locked data)

Pence: Oh, man. The transporter's been protected.

Sora: Protected from what?

Pence: I guess from us? We can't use it to get to the other Twilight Town.

Hayner (loudly): Why not? It worked before! We sent Sora there!

Pence: Well that was then, and this is now.

Olette: And there's no other way?

Pence: None that I know.

Sora: Great.

(Sora's ringtone goes off in his pocket and he pulls out the Gummiphone. 
He answers the call and Ienzo appears on the screen)

Ienzo: Hello, Sora. You wouldn't happen to be in front of a computer?

Sora: Huh? Well...yeah. But how'd you know that?

Ienzo: I was tinkering with Ansem's computer--you know, to decrypt the 
Code that was left in it? And I noticed that someone had logged in from 
another terminal. I figured it might be you.

Sora (totally getting it): Oh! Yeah, the log terminal.

Donald: You don't know what he said.

Sora (to Donald): Oh, and what, you do?

(Ienzo laughs to himself)

Goofy: I know I haven't got a clue. A-hyuck!

Ienzo: Then, uhh...who was it that logged in?

Pence: Oh, hi there. This is Pence.

(Sora holds the phone up to him)

Pence: I'm the one who logged into the computer.

Ienzo: Good. As long as it's a user that we know we can trust.

Pence: Yup. But, I'm kind of stuck here.

(Hayner crosses his arms impatiently)

Pence: One of the programs is protected, so...I can't run it.

(Hayner sighs impatiently)

Ienzo: Which program?

Hayner (explodes): The transporter to the other Twilight Town!

(His outburst surprises Ienzo)

Hayner: It's the only way to find Roxas. You gotta help us.

Ienzo (processing this): Another Twilight Town? And a "transporter"? 
Okay... A virtual town inside the computer, made of data.

(Jiminy pops out of Sora's hood)

Jiminy: A datascape! Fellas...

Goofy: Mm-hmm, we've seen one. That's what we used once to investigate 
Jiminy's journal.

Ienzo: Maybe I can do something. Pence, let's get a network set up. My 
address here is...

(The time it takes to set up this network mixed with the inherent 
technobabble between Ienzo and Pence, Sora has fallen asleep holding the 
phone. The computer makes a sound through his snoring)

Ienzo: Okay, sharing is enabled.

(Sora awakes with a start)

Sora: Huh? Were you able to fix it?

Ienzo: Now that our two computers have been successfully networked 
together, I can take control of the terminal there and change the 
privileges...

Sora: And Roxas?

Ienzo: Yes. For the virtual world to be completely realized, Ansem the 
Wise would've included Roxas's full data in the construction. Meaning, 
somewhere on your machine there's a log of that data that--

(He pauses, thinking how to translate this into Sora-speak)

Ienzo: Uhh...basically, we can decipher Ansem's Code more quickly, AND 
we can analyze the virtual Twilight Town while we're at it.

Sora: Okay. Great! I can't computer so...do that.

Ienzo: Glad you're following along. Don't worry, we'll handle it. Chip 
and Dale will be helping me out here on this end. I'll call you back as 
soon as we know anything more.

Sora: Thanks.

Ienzo: Oh, before I forget--a bit of troubling news. It's about one of 
the Organization's former members. You knew him as Vexen--but to us he 
was Ansem's apprentice Even. He was recompleted like the rest of us, but 
hadn't regained consciousness yet. Then, sometime after Lea left, Even 
vanished. Aeleus and Dilan--the two you know as Lexaeus and Xaldin--they 
went out looking for him, but...he's just gone. And I'm starting to worry.

Sora: You think he's on THEIR side?

Ienzo: I think it's a real possibility. He's a devious researcher. You 
should be careful.

Sora: All right. Thanks.

(Sora hangs up and pockets the phone)

Hayner: Oh no! We got work! I totally forgot.

(Hayner starts to rush off)

Pence: Really? But what about all this?

Hayner: Hey, both are important. We're gonna need some cash to go to the 
beach. Also, don't forget the pretzels. Gotta buy four now.

(Pence thinks and counts on his fingers)

Pence: Ohh. I get it.

Olette (smiling): He's thinking ahead.

(Pence laughs)

Hayner: Later, Sora!

Sora: Yeah. See ya, Hayner!

(Hayner walks to the entrance and Olette follows)

Olette: Bye, Donald! Goofy!

Donald & Goofy (waving): Good-bye!

Pence: Oh, and since I'm manning the computer here, you guys're in charge 
of earning my share.

Hayner: No pretzel for Pence.

(Olette giggles and the two of them leave)

Pence: Hey!

(Pence sighs, making the trio chuckle. Sora, Donald and Goofy leave the 
mansion)

?????: So, you think you can bring Roxas back?

(Sora turns to see Ansem standing against the wall with his arms crossed, 
looking at them snidely)

Sora: Ansem!

(A corridor of darkness appears next to him and his Nobody persona emerges 
from its depths)

Sora: Xemnas!

Xemnas: Roxas should never have existed in the first place. What you seek 
is impossible.

Sora: Roxas does exist. His heart's inside my heart.

Xemnas: And in the unlikely event you did manage to separate the two, where 
is it you think you can put his heart?

Sora: Well...Roxas used to live in the other Twilight Town, right? So, I'm 
just gonna put him back there.

Ansem: Do you even realize what you are saying? The other Twilight Town is 
just data.

Sora: A heart can live anywhere. Even inside data. There are hearts all 
around us.

Goofy (pensively): Ansem and Xemnas used to be part of the same person, 
right? But look. Now, they exist separately just fine. If they can do it, 
then I don't see any reason why you and Roxas can't find a way.

Sora: Oh...yeah!

Donald: Yeah! You tell 'em, Captain Goofy!

(With newfound exhuberance, they face the two enemies)

Ansem: In that case, by all means.

Xemnas: Nothing would please us more than Roxas's return, of course.

Sora: You wish. He'll never answer to you again.

Xemnas: Still so blind. A Nobody is what's left behind when one gives 
his heart to darkness. There is only one way to bring Roxas back, which 
is for you to give your heart up as well. Sora, have you finally decided 
to call upon the darkness?

(He points directly at Sora)

Sora: What?

Ansem: Go on then. The shadows are never out of reach.

(Ansem smirks as a herd of Neoshadow Heartless appear behind them. Xemnas 
waves his hand and Dusk Nobodies join them. Sora glares at them)

Ansem & Xemnas: Now, set your heart free.

(The two disappear)

Sora: Wait!

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(The knight and the wizard face the creatures and Sora summons his Keyblade)

Sora: It's not darkness. Not if it helps him!

(Together, the three defeat the Heartless and Nobodies. Donald and Goofy 
regroup once the fighting is done, while Sora stands by himself, silently. 
The two give a sad sigh)

Sora: Herc said... He said, "With all my heart." Okay. Then all my heart 
it is. I'm getting Roxas out.

(He turns to the two of them)

Sora: Are you with me, Donald? Goofy?

Donald & Goofy (brightly): You betcha!

Sora: I don't know what Ansem and Xemnas want, but I think we'd better 
tell the others to watch out.

Donald (nodding): Yeah.

Goofy: Okay then. Let's head back to town.

(Sora nods and they run back through the woods to town, interrupted by 
a familiar voice)

???????: Well, bless my bagpipes! It was YOU laddies who rescued my chef.

(Donald and Goofy stop at the sound of the voice near a plaza where they 
see an elderly duck with a cane, top hat, and glasses. Tucked under one 
arm is a box)

Donald: It's Uncle Scrooge!

(Sora walks back)

Sora: Huh? Wait... Didn't he sell ice cream in Hollow Bastion?

Goofy: That's right. But Uncle Scrooge here's what you might call a world 
traveler.

Sora: Cool.

(Donald runs up to Scrooge McDuck with Sora and Goofy in tow)

Sora: How are ya, Uncle Scrooge?

Scrooge: Oh! Hello, Sora! You're lookin' hale and hearty. I heard ye were 
on another grand adventure with these two. I hope Donald isn't making a 
menace of himself.

(Donald shakes his head in embarassment)

Donald: Aw. Why did you have to say that?

Goofy: So, Uncle Scrooge, what's that you were sayin' about a chef?

Scrooge: Och! Right, right. The chef of me bistro here wanted to show ye 
his appreciation, so he baked this for ye.

(He holds out the box and Sora takes it)

Sora: What is it?

(He opens the box seeing a decadent dessert topped with fruit)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Wow, cake!

(Scrooge's top hat twitches, getting his attention)

Sora: The whole cake? It's for us?

(The hat twitches some more, puzzling Sora)

Scrooge: Aye, settle down... The chef wants ye to know it's not a cake, 
but a 'tarte aux fruits'.

Goofy: He does?

Scrooge: Why keep it under my hat? May I introduce...

(Scrooge takes off his top hat, revealing the gray rat from earlier, who 
hops down onto the crown of the hat)

Scrooge: Little Chef.

Sora: Oh! It's you!

Donald: Uncle Scrooge, you opened a bistro in Twilight Town?

Scrooge: Aye. It all started a little while ago, when I was enjoying one 
of the best meals of my life.

(Little Chef smiles and nods)

Scrooge: And when I asked to speak to the chef, I met this wee genius.

(Little Chef strikes a confident pose)

Scrooge: As it turns out, he wanted to expand his culinary horizons. So, 
I thought: that's an opportunity. And I financed the whole operation.

(Little Chef mimes cutting, preparing, and serving a dish)

Scrooge: Ooh, I think he wants to cook some more for ye.

(The happy rat smiles eagerly)

Scrooge: Fetch some ingredients. Especially anything unusual.

Goofy: That'll be fun! Kinda like a scavenger hunt.

Scrooge: An' the more the better. The mark of a truly great chef is 
creating masterpieces out of anything. Ye can start right here in town.

Sora: We'll do anything to try more of Little Chef's food.

Donald: Yeah!

(Little Chef scratches his head meekly)

Goofy: That tarte sure did look scrumptiously delicious.

Sora: Okay! The ingredient hunt is on.

(Donald and Goofy nod. After searching town for ingredients, the trio 
return to Le Grand Bistrot)

Hayner: Hey! Guys!

(They turn to see Hayner and Olette running towards them)

Sora: Hayner! Olette!

(Scrooge walks out from behind the three of them)

Hayner: Hey, boss. Done with the posters.

Scrooge: Aye, good work, kids.

Goofy: You guys work for Uncle Scrooge here at the bistro?

Hayner: Umm... Do we?

(He looks over at Olette, who pulls out a poster)

Olette: He gave us a short job putting up these special posters.

(She unravels the black-and-white poster which is titled "Mickey & Sora 
in 'GIANTLAND'" depicting a club-carrying bearded giant, holding up a 
rogue-dressed Mickey Mouse who looks ready to fight)

Olette: Mr. McDuck's hosting an open-air film festival in the courtyard. 
Cool, huh?

(The three gaze at the poster curiously)

Olette: Oh. Sora... Hold your phone up to the poster.

(Sora takes out the Gummiphone)

Sora: 'Kaaay...

(Olette gestures to the scrambled icon in the corner of the poster. Sora 
points the phone's camera at it and it scans the code with a bright sound. 
Olette rolls the poster back up)

Olette: There, you've just downloaded a promo game for the film. You can 
try it later.

(Donald turns to his rich uncle)

Donald: You did all this, Uncle Scrooge?

Scrooge: Of course, laddie. Provide a bit of entertainment, and then give 
folks a nice, cozy place to relax.

(He gestures to the restaurant, pointing at the logo with his cane)

Scrooge: Like me bistro here. They'll all be happy, an' hungry, an' eager 
to spend their money.

(He cackles to himself)

Donald: Uncle Scrooge...

Goofy: Gawrsh, he sure is canny. I always wondered how he keeps customers 
comin' into his businesses over and over.

Sora: Oh, yeah, I'm no business guy, but I sure wouldn't wanna be one of 
Uncle Scrooge's competitors.

Hayner: Seriously.

(Donald, Goofy and Olette laugh)

Sora: Oh! Right. I need to warn you guys.

Hayner: Why?

Sora: Well, those creepy-crawly things might come back for more, so stay 
on your toes.

Hayner: Sure. But don't we have you guys to take care of 'em for us?

(Olette catches on)

Olette: You have to leave AGAIN?

Sora (nodding): Mm-hmm.

Donald: It's our job.

Goofy: But we'll definitely be back.

Hayner: When ya gonna slow down?

Sora: Sorry. Just do me a favor...

Hayner: Well, what is it? Don't make it too tough.

Sora: I know how Roxas feels. To be lost. But Donald and Goofy...Kairi...
brought me back by wishing with all their hearts.

(Donald & Goofy nod)

Sora: So...I was hoping the three of you would do the same, and wish for 
Roxas.

Hayner: What? That's it? (chuckles) That's no favor. We'll all wish. I'm 
wishin'.

Olette: Yeah! Me and Pence too.

Sora (gladly): Thanks.

(On the roof of a nearby building, Ansem and Xemnas watch from above. From 
behind them, a dark portal opens and Xigbar struts out)

Xigbar: Aren't you making it a little too obvious?

Xemnas: We were instructed to guide him.

Ansem: Yes...just look at them. They wouldn't get far if we did not spell 
it out.

Xigbar: Fair enough. But let's not forget how many times Sora still managed 
to rain on our parade.

Ansem: If he wavers from the path we lay, we destroy him.

Xigbar: But in that case...we'll have to find ourselves another vessel.

Xemnas: That is why we never have just one iron in the fire.

(Later, Sora busts through the swinging doors into the kitchen of Le Grand 
Bistrot)

Sora: Is the food ready yet?

(He sees the kitchen empty)

Sora: Huh? He hasn't started?

(Little Chef runs in and crawls up Sora's leg)

Sora: Whoa! Hold on! Hey!

(He reaches Sora's head and grabs onto his hair, same as before. He pulls 
on one tuft of hair and Sora lurches in that direction)

Sora: Oh no!

(He grabs a frying pan in his left hand and a spatula in his right)

Sora: Would you--

(He spins around to face the stove)

Sora: You're gonna make ME cook?

(After a successful cooking experience with Little Chef at the helm, they 
leave Twilight Town hungry for more ingredients and also more worlds. In a 
Secret Forest, Kairi is writing a letter to Sora as the evening sun washes 
over her)

Kairi: I'm sorry I left without saying good-bye. Did Master Yen Sid tell 
you? I'm training to become a Keyblade wielder like you. That's right. No 
more waiting for you to come back from your adventures. I want to get out 
there and do my part to help. Merlin has used his magic to bring us to a 
place where time doesn't matter. We can take as long as we need to complete 
our training. He's an amazing wizard. Oh, and by "us," I mean me and Lea. 
He's really sorry for all the trouble he caused. I told him it's fine, but 
he won't stop apologizing. I'll admit I was a little scared of him at 
first, but I've gotten to know him better. All he ever wanted was to help 
his friend. Honestly, it's hard not to like him. Every now and then, I 
catch him staring at me. When I ask what's wrong, he says, "I'm not sure. 
I think I'm forgetting something. Don't know what." Sora, I think it may 
have something to do with you. Your journey is all about helping people: 
some that you've never met before, and some like Lea that you have. 
They're all counting on you. It won't be easy, but I hope you'll remain 
the happy and cheerful Sora I know. There's no heart your smile can't reach.

(She hears footsteps and look over to see Lea)

Kairi: What's wrong?

(He breaks his stare after a moment and tries to shrug it off, turning away)

Lea: Huh? Nothin', sorry.

Kairi (admonishingly): Lea.

Lea: What? I am.

(He scratches the back of his neck. She giggles, and he sits on a rock 
opposite her as she continues writing)

Lea: A letter?

Kairi: Yup.

Lea: To Sora?

Kairi: Mmm, technically yes. But I won't send it. It's more for me.

Lea: Ask Merlin. He'll deliver it for you.

Kairi: Yeah, but it's okay. I just like talking to Sora, even if it's 
on paper.

(She holds the notepad close)

Lea: Ohh... Okay.

(He remembers something)

Lea: Oh!

(Kairi tilts her head, puzzled. Lea pulls out two sea-salt ice cream bars)

Lea: Here.

Kairi: Ice cream? Really?

Lea: Yeah, I asked Merlin to pick these up.

(Kairi smiles)

Lea: Ya know, we did both summon Keyblades. Gotta celebrate.

(He hands a bar out to Kairi, who take it)

Kairi: You're sweet, Lea.

(Lea chuckles sheepishly)

Lea: Naw...

(Lea watches her take a bite, zoning out again)

Kairi: What?

(He averts his gaze)

Lea: N-nothing, I just...

Kairi: You're trying to remember what you forgot?

Lea: Well, I, uh... Yeah... Yeah.

(He looks out at the sunset as his words trail)

Kairi: So tomorrow--you and me in the ring. You ready?

(The sun starts to get into his eyes)

Lea: 'Course.

Kairi: Don't hold back, Lea. Promise?

(In the glare of the sun, Lea thinks he sees a different girl in Kairi's

cream with a smile. Lea's emerald eyes well up with tears and he drops his 
ice cream bar in shock. Unable to contain his feelings, the tears stream 
down his face)

Kairi: Huh? Are you okay? Lea!

(He quickly tries to wipe them away as Kairi gets closer to him)

Lea: Yeah... Sorry...

Kairi: You're crying. What's wrong?

(Lea sniffles)

Lea: Something in my eyes.

Kairi: Lea...

Lea: I'm...gonna go. Sorry.

Kairi: 'Kay, but stop apologizing.

Lea: Fine...on one condition.

Kairi: What?

Lea: Call me Axel from now on. Got it memorized?

(He points to his head)

Kairi: Yeah. Okay, Axel.

In the heart of Shibuya, a battle rages on between a group of fighters 
and the mechanical troopers known as Gigas. Atop a tall building a pink 
beam of light shoots into the sky. Racing through the rubble on the 
ground, a strong man with glasses tears through a Gigas with his large 
green sword, scattering the mechanical beast into disintegrating cubes. 
Running to catch up to him is another young man with silver hair who 
engages his red sword as more Gigas encroach on them. Swooping in on the 
silver-haired youth's left is a third young man wielding two thin blue 
swords, the wind whipping through his red hair. He aims a Blizzard spell 
at a (relatively) small Gigas in front of them. Several more Gigas close 
in on the source of the beam of light on the roof. The source is a young 
woman with long hair clutching at her necklace as the pink energy swirls 
around her. The beam is directed at a point in the sky which takes on a 
circular blue shape forming a kind of gate. The clouds whirl around it as 
the surrounding skyscrapers are torn asunder, pieces falling upwards toward 
the gate. The red-haired youth holds off a Gigas with one sword-hand, while 
sending a Thunder spell toward a second with his other hand, destroying the 
foe. The man with glasses summons a green Barrier to stop an incoming Gigas 
as the silver-haired youth takes one out behind him. Dodging several 
blaster shots, the silver-haired youth sends a red spell at a Gigas while 
eliminating another with a slice from his sword. He lands on the ground 
just as a red Gigas flies towards him. As it rushes him, the boy summons 
a spinning orb, sending shards of the tiled floor into the air. The boy 
leaps above the orb and strikes downward through it, tearing apart the 
bubble and the Gigas inside it. The energy surrounding the girl grows in 
volume as the boy freezes a Gigas in place with a Stop spell. The frozen 
Gigas soon caves in on itself by way of a Gravity spell, which the boy sends 
through two other Gigas, trapping them. He slices through the amalgamation 
and gives a defiant look through his red and blue eyes. The three young men 
reach the edge of an adjacent building in time to watch the skyscraper 
being torn apart by the pink energy, blue lightning bolts shooting out from 
the gate. The three fighters leap into the swirling vortex as numerous 
Gigas fly toward them. The silver-haired boy destroys one Gigas with his 
crossbow and slashes at another with his red sword. Catching him off-guard, 
he is soon piled on by several blue Gigas before a large Reflect spell 
surrounds him and his friends. The redhead summons another Blizzard spell 
and shoots it through the green barrier, providing a tunnel of ice for the 
silver-haired youth to fly through. He reaches out his hand to the girl 
drifting in the pink abyss, her star necklace floating freely around her 
neck. She opens her eyes as he reaches her and their hands nearly touch. 
Suddenly the maelstrom around them breaks and the girl is ensnared by the 
claw of a Gigas. The trio land on the building as the girl cries out from 
its clutches. An enormous Gigas, bigger than the rest rises to meet them on 
the edge of the skyscraper. It opens a giant claw, summoning a cerulean 
blast. The boy stands in its crosshairs and his weapon folds down, 
igniting the red sword once again. He swings it back as his other weapon 
raises the arms of his crossbow. He slices the air and sends a shot from the 
crossbow, with the energy claw reflecting firmly in his blue eye.
