Rex (excitedly): Hurray! Oh, that makes me so happy!

(He turns to Donald)

Rex: Were you watching too? Did you see what I did?

(Donald and Woody try to calm Rex down)

Donald: Yeah, good for you.

Woody: Listen, Rex.

Rex: I was going for fearsome...

Woody: Would ya--

Rex: ...but I think I might've actually achieved something close to 
terrifying!

Woody: Earth to Rex.

(Rex stops)

Sora: Do you know where the others were taken?

Rex: What do you mean? Did something bad happen?

Buzz: Back to square one.

Woody: Oh, great.

(Woody hears a clicking sound of plastic on metal and looks up to see 
the sergeant climbing down the vent near the ceiling)

Woody: Sarge! Have you got a status report?

Sarge (saluting): Sir! One of my men just located Hamm forward of our 
position, in Babies in Toddlers.

(The group smile with the good news)

Sarge: The corporal was debriefing him, but something must have gone 
wrong. All radio contact has been lost.

(The group sighs)

Buzz: Anything more specific we can go on?

Sarge: Right before I lost contact, I heard music with some sort of 
sonic interference.

Buzz: Music?

Goofy: Ya think it could be the Heartless?

Donald: What if it's another big monster?

Sora: Let's find out.

Woody: I agree.

(Woody and the group start walking ahead, while Rex stays put)

Rex: Actually...I think I'll head back and wait by the entrance. I'm 
sure those vents are gonna be much too narrow for my big dinosaur tail.

(Sora looks up at the vent)

Sora: Really? I'm sure you'd fit.

Buzz (interjecting): Rex is right. Besides, we need a lookout at th
e entrance. It's an important mission. Can you do it?

Rex: Yes, sir!

(Rex makes a determined fist with his little arm and Buzz salutes him. 
Sora and the rest chuckle and make their way up into the ventilation 
shaft. Using the vents to reach the third floor of Galaxy Toys they exit 
into the Dolls section of Babies & Toddlers)

Woody: This is Babies and Toddlers. Where do you guys think we should start?

(Goofy bends down to speak to the sergeant)

Goofy: Sarge, didn't you mention music?

(Sarge hops to face him)

Sarge: Affirmative, Goofy.

(Sora peers out through the vast toy section)

Sora: Hmm... All right. Why don't we look for things that make noise?

Goofy: Sure!

Donald: That's good thinking for you.

(Donald walks off, cackling)

Sora: Wha... What do you mean, for me?

(Donald breaks into a run)

Sora: Hey, where ya--

(Donald runs around Goofy)

Sora (laughing): Donald!

(They end up in a standoff around Goofy)

Woody: I think they really are good guys.

(Sora tries to grab Donald but he runs past him and shakes his tailfeather)

Sora: Hold still!

(Goofy chuckles and Sora runs after him)

Buzz: Well, you wouldn't have trusted them otherwise.

(Donald tries to run around Goofy again but Sora blocks him, prompting 
Donald to dive through Sora's legs. Goofy laughs harder)

Sora: What?

Donald: Missed me!

(He laughs, leaping back to his feet)

Sora: Don't!

Buzz: And I know that your trust is a hard-earned treasure.

(They continue playing cat and mouse)

Sora: No! Stop that!

Donald (laughing): Victor!

(Woody smiles softly at Buzz)

Buzz: Well...for all our sakes, let's hope you're right, cowboy. I'm 
willing to give 'em a chance at least for a little while longer. 
Especially if it means getting Andy and our friends back.

Woody: Agreed.

(They search through the store, taking out more Heartless-possessed 
toys, until they reach a large gramophone in the corner at a display 
labeled Musical Toads. Sora hops onto the turntable)

Sora: Is this it?

(He begins to run on the record and the symphony of toads on the display 
light up and begin playing)

Woody: Come on, Sora... You've never used a record player?

Sora: Huh?

(Sora slows down and the music stops as Woody leaps up onto the record as 
well)

Woody: Like this!

(He starts running along the record, throwing Sora off-balance. Sora 
returns to a run and laughs as the orchestra continues playing)

Goofy: It's workin'!

(One of the instruments plays a false note)

Buzz: Wait, did that sound off to you?

Donald: It did.

Sora: Huh?

(Distracted, Sora slows down and almost crashes into Woody)

Woody: Heeey!

(Sora speeds back up and Goofy calls up to him)

Goofy: Sora! There's some kinda strange noise comin' from the orchestra!

(Sora and Woody exchange glances)

Sora (waving): Got it! Woody, you keep the record going.

(Sora jumps down from the turntable)

Woody: Whoa-whoa-whoa!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy search the orchestra for the instrument that's 
playing off-rhythm and find that it's the tuba-playing toad. Woody 
struggles to catch his breath as he keeps the music playing while Goofy 
peers into the tuba)

Goofy: Hmm... Somethin' seems to be stuck in this tuba.

Sora: I'll get it out.

(Sora reaches into the tuba, feeling around for the obstruction. He finds 
it and struggles to get it unstuck)

Sora: Almost got it...

(With a loud pop, he pulls out...)

Sora: There!

(...the corporal. Sora places him gently on the table)

Sarge: Corporal!

(The sergeant hops down from a higher ledge and walks over to the 
corporal, placing a hand on his back)

Sarge: You all right, son?

Corporal: Yes, sir.

Buzz: That's the soldier Sarge lost contact with.

(Sarge gets the soldier to his feet and puts his arm around his shoulders, 
hoisting him up)

Sora: So you found Hamm?

Corporal: Yes. But...while I was radioing in, a giant hand grabbed me, 
and it stuffed me in there. They must have taken Hamm to another 
location. We have to hurry!

(The corporal tries to walk his injured self, but falls over)

Sarge: Wait, Corporal. You're not fit for action.

(Sarge helps him stand again)

Corporal: But Sarge...

Sarge: Your tour is over, son. And it's all right. Our trusted allies 
will take over.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy salute them and the corporal starts tearing up)

Sarge: I will move the corporal to a safer location.

Corporal (saluting): Good luck, gentlemen.

(The Green Army Men walk off as the music continues to play and Woody 
continues to run. They reach the edge of the orchestra ledge and give 
Woody a salute)

Woody: Huh...?

(They hop down the ledge)

Woody (running out of breath): Hey, hey, hey, hey! What is...going on?!

Sora: Oh, right!

Buzz: Woody! Mission complete!

(Woody leaps off the record player and the music slows to a stop)

Woody (winded): Why didn't...you tell me...a little sooner?

(Woody falls to his hands and knees, trying to catch his breath)

Buzz: Sorry, there's no time to rest. Hamm needs us.

(Buzz hops off the table and Woody gives an exhausted salute. They soon 
find a dollhouse that's rattling around in a window display. They struggle 
to get the side of the house open, but with everyone's help, it unlatches, 
and the five of them land in a pileup)

Hamm: Talk about cabin fever. Thanks for the save.

(Hamm walks out of the dollhouse much to their surprise)

Woody: You okay, Hamm?

Hamm: Yeah, aside from being locked in, the accomodations were fine.

(He nods over to the fully-furnished inside of the house, where Donald 
steps inside)

Donald: Aww. What a tiny little house.

(He walks by the window where a giant doll peers inside)

Donald: Huh?

(The doll brims with darkness and its sudden appearance causes Donald to 
thrash about the house)

Woody: Who was--

(Hamm shrieks in terror and backs away)

Buzz: What's wrong?

Hamm: She's back! That's the doll that pig-penned me!

(The doll's eyes glow orange, matching the glowing Heartless symbol on 
her left bunny ear)

Woody: Hamm, take cover.

Hamm: Uh, copy that. One stay in the dread-and-breakfast was enough for me!

(Hamm runs away)

Buzz: Not another possessed toy...

Sora: Guys, look alive!

(They fight the possessed Angelic Amber doll along with a horde of Bouncy 
Pets and Patchwork Animals also under the Marionette Heartless's control. 
The doll stops floating and its eyes return to their normal shade of blue. 
It slumps against the floor, lifeless)

Buzz: Wait... What if we end up just like her? Forgetting ourselves and...
attacking each other?

Sora: No way, Buzz. That won't happen.

Donald: No way!

Goofy: You guys are too strong.

Buzz (hotly): You can't be sure! What if I get taken over, then attack you?

(Woody places a hand on his shoulder)

Woody: Buzz, you're overthinking it.

Sora: Yeah. The Heartless--the darkness--can only creep in when our hearts 
falter. Trust me. You'll be fine if you don't lose heart.

Woody: Well, that's good. Because I know you, Buzz. You'll never lose heart 
when it comes to your friends.

(He flicks his hat upwards)

Buzz: True enough, cowboy.

(Buzz gives a small smile)

Buzz: Sorry to have worried you all.

Woody: No problem. Now, let's go find the others.

(They return to the window, Buzz helping Woody up to the windowsill, and 
meet back up with Hamm. Donald and Goofy spot something through the glass)

Donald: Look!

(A UFO with a crane claw sails past the window, a trail of darkness 
behind it)

Goofy: A flying saucer!

(Woody adjusts his hat)

Woody: I think I know who that might lead us to. C'mon, guys!

(They open the window right as the UFO passes by and Woody waves them 
through when the coast is clear)

Hamm: Hey, Woody. I'd just slow you down, with all the loose change I'm 
carrying. I'll hang by the entrance.

Woody: No problem. Be safe, Hamm.

(Woody leaps out the window)

Hamm: Hey, thanks, buddy. You just take care of your old self.

(Hamm leaves and Woody rejoins the group)

Woody: Now, let's follow that UFO!

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Right!

(They enter the Outdoor playplace of Babies & Toddlers where the UFO is 
flying through. The Aliens spot it with glee)

Little Green Man 1: They have come for us.

Little Green Man 2: The mystic portal awaits.

(The UFO stops over the three Aliens and the claw descends, sending the 
group running after them)

Buzz: Oh no!

Sora: Wait!

Woody: Stop!

(The Aliens are snatched up into the mothership)

Little Green Men: Farewell!

Buzz: It's getting away!

Sora: Don't go!

(Surrounded by Toy Trooper Heartless, Sora, Donald, Goofy, Woody & Buzz 
take down the possessed UFO. It drops the Aliens and falters in the air, 
eventually losing power and sinking to the floor)

Little Green Men: We are back!

(They start to run in different directions)

Little Green Man 1: Our ship is no more.

Little Green Man 2: Nirvana will not be reached.

(Sora picks one up with a squeak)

Sora: Sorry I trashed your ride.

Little Green Man 3: Fear not.

Little Green Man 1: We still have our new home.

Little Green Men: The Chamber of Andy.

Buzz: They're right.

(Sora sets the Alien down)

Buzz: This isn't where we belong. We've been in this toy store long enough. 
It's time for us to go home to Andy's room.

Sora: But...Xehanort told us that room isn't even his real room.

Buzz: Can you prove that any of that nonsense is true?

(Donald and Goofy sigh)

Buzz: And even if that Andy's room IS fake, it doesn't mean he's not 
somewhere in this world with us. I'm going home to wait for him. No more 
debate.

(He turns)

Buzz: You with me, Woody?

(The Aliens waddle to follow Buzz)

Woody: Hmm... Youre right, Buzz. Now that we're all accounted for, we 
should meet up at the entrance and go home. 

Sora: Okay. We could have used friends like you for the final showdown...

Goofy: But Organization XIII's our problem to solve.

(Sora nods and Donald hops in place)

Donald: Yeah, I can take 'em!

Sora: I'm not so sure about that...

(Goofy chuckles)

Donald: I'll show ya!

(Sora laughs and runs up to Woody and Buzz, Donald and Goofy following suit)

Sora: Guys, can we see you off?

Woody: That would be great.

(They return to the first floor)

Woody: Sarge, roll call.

(He points to the Green Army Man as he walks past him)

Sarge (saluting): Sir, yes sir! Roll call! All toys, fall in!

(The Army Men, Hamm, and the Aliens form a line as Buzz walks by them)

Buzz: Sarge... Army Men times four... Hamm... Aliens 1, 2, 3...

(The Army Men salute and each Alien squeaks as they raise their hands)

Buzz: Wait. Where's Rex?

Hamm: Aw, he took off. Said he wanted to prove to you you could trust Sora. 
He's up there by the video games.

(The pig points up to the third floor and Buzz sighs)

Buzz: Well, here we go again.

Sora: Huh? This is about us?

(He gives a worried look)

Sora: He's not safe. The Heartless are out there.

Woody: You're right. Sora, Donald, Goofy... Any chance you could help us 
one last time?

Sora: Sure!

Goofy: Of course!

Donald: You bet!

Woody (smiling): Thanks, guys.

(They return to the third floor and enter the video game store where they 
find Rex among the Verum Rex merchandise)

Rex: Hurray!

(He hops down and rushes over to Sora with the game in his hands)

Rex: Look! Look! I found it!

(He holds it almost too close to Sora's face, trying to show him the cover)

Rex: See, Sora?

(The cover shows an image of the silver-haired Yozora lazing on stone steps 
with his sword and crossbow)

Sora: Well, I never look THIS good. The clothes kinda match.

(Buzz and Woody walk further into the game store around a giant poster for 
Verum Rex, where they can see a much larger version of the game cover)

Woody: Whaddaya know! They ARE video game figures. See? I told ya, Buzz. 
They're toys, just like the rest of us.

(Buzz looks over to them as something catches Rex's eye)

Buzz: Well, I suppose.

(Sora leans over to speak privately with Donald)

Sora: Donald, I thought your magic decided how I look. Explain.

Donald: Simple. That's not you.

Goofy: Say, Riku would make a great action figure!

Donald: Must be him!

Sora: No! It's me. I've got the black clothes and, uh...

(He trails off slowly)

Donald: So what?

Buzz: All right, everyone. Now that we're back together, it's time to 
return to Andy's room.

(Rex is reading the back cover of a Play Plus strategy guide)

Rex: Now?

(He drops the book and searches through the shelf, tossing books aside)

Rex: But can't I at least check the strategy guides? I want to know how to 
beat Bahamut!

(He manages to find the Verum Rex guide)

Buzz: Next time. Right now, we need to go home.

(Buzz takes the book and tosses it away. Rex's face turns sad and Buzz 
consoles him with a tap him on the snout. Rex walks away hesitantly from 
the book, following Buzz back to the group. A figure with a pair of boots 
lands on the floor nearby)

Young Xehanort: Oh, but you needn't rush off.

(The voice catches their attention and they summon their weapons)

Sora: Xehanort!

Young Xehanort: I have more to observe. I can't let you leave yet.

Sora: It's us that you really want. Leave the others out of this.

(Xehanort smirks)

Young Xehanort: You WOULD say that, champion of light.

(A Marionette Heartless dangles behind them unknowingly)

Young Xehanort: Very well, let's skip to the final stage.

(It strolls up to Buzz and he gives a face of surprise before the 
Heartless disappears and his body goes quiet)

Rex: Buzz? What's the matter?

(Darkness emanates from Buzz Lightyear and he activates his laser, 
aiming it at Woody's head. Woody gasps before raising an eyebrow)

Woody: C'mon, Buzz. Quit fooling around.

Goofy: Look out!

(Buzz fires the laser just as Goofy leaps in front of Woody with his shield)

Woody: I can't believe it! Buzz has been taken over?

(Buzz fires a few more shots)

Sora: What did you do to him?!

(Sora attacks Xehanort, who phases away in the blink of an eye)

Young Xehanort: I thought I made it clear. I am testing the strength of 
their bonds.

(Young Xehanort walks around the room, phasing in and out as Sora tries 
to strike him down, but only slicing air)

Young Xehanort: In this world, toys have hearts. And those hearts come 
from a powerful bond.

(Sora looks around, seeing Xehanort on a high display case above a video 
screen)

Young Xehanort: So what happens when those bonds are stretched to their 
limit? When they are worlds apart, can cloth and plastic hold on to their 
hearts?

(Sora leaps to the top of the display with another failed attack)

Young Xehanort: All I needed was a wedge to widen the divide--someone like 
you to fill them with distrust and doubt.

(Sora finds him walking along the display and Xehanort dodges each of Sora's 
blows effortlessly)

Young Xehanort: And that chasm you created can be filled with a vast 
darkness.

(He appears on the floor and Sora leaps down at him, striking nothing)

Young Xehanort: Witness it for yourself.

Donald: Sora!

(Donald and Rex are trying to hold Buzz at bay, but he continues his laser 
blasts unflinching as Goofy stops them from hitting Woody)

Rex: Do somethiiing!

Sora: On my way!

(Sora tries to run to their aid, but Xehanort snatches him up)

Young Xehanort: Not this time!

(Xehanort summons a concentrated energy blast near Sora's waist, which then 
explodes, blasting him into the nearby video screen. He phases into it, 
sending a ripple through the screen. He lands on a metal surface of an 
enormous boat several miles from a nighttime city skyline)

Sora: Where am I?

Young Xehanort: Haven't you heard? In this world, you come from a video 
game. So now, you can watch my experiment from inside that screen. That 
is...if you manage to find a moment's rest.

(Young Xehanort teleports out of the store as Sora comes face to face with 
the Gigas inside Verum Rex)

Sora: There's got to be a way out. Buzz, Woody, hang on!

(After a few minutes, Sora leaps out of the television screen to the 
delighted faces of his friends)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

Woody: Y'all right, Sora?

Sora: Yeah, I'm just fine. And you?

(They don't know how to respond aside from worry)

Sora: Wait... Where's Buzz?

(Woody sighs)

Goofy: He disappeared into a dark corridor.

Sora: Oh...

Woody: Sora, how do we get him back?

Sora: I don't know. My power won't open those.

(Woody breathes a large sigh as the Green Army Men walk nearer)

Sarge: Sir, did I hear you say "dark corridor"?

Woody: That's right, Sarge. Any ideas?

Sarge: Well, it might be a long shot, but we've sighted a shadowy portal 
in the Kid Korral. We can infiltrate from a window inside Babies and 
Toddlers.

(Woody's disposition lightens)

Sarge: I'll head there and get it open.

(He kneels down close to the sergeant with a wide smile)

Woody: Sarge, you're a lifesaver!

(He turns back to Sora and the others)

Woody: You guys in?

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Yeah!

Rex: Please promise you'll bring Buzz home.

Hamm: With batteries included?

Little Green Man 1: Journey safely.

Little Green Man 2: Farewell!

Woody: Don't worry. WE'RE gonna get our friend back.

(They return to the Outdoor section of Babies & Toddlers)

Woody: Sora, look!

(High above on a windowed wall with the design of a house is a much 
smaller window)

Woody: That must be the window Sarge mentioned.

(They make their way up through the window and enter the Kid Korral, 
where Sora sees odd green cubes piled against the main door)

Sora: The entrance was blocked by BLOCKS?

Woody: Can you use the Gigas to move 'em?

Sora: Yeah, maybe. I'll try.

(Sora pilots a nearby blue Gigas, stretching its arm out. He activates 
the claw which sends magnetic bolts to the green blocks, causing them 
to glow and disperse, unbarring the door. They move further into the 
room where Donald spots something)

Donald: Up there!

(A stream of darkness emanates from the uppermost vent in the room, much 
too high to reach by normal means, especially at toy height)

Sora: How we gonna reach that?

Woody: Well, there ARE some more blocks here...

(Heartless appear as they reach another pile of green blocks, but they 
are quickly taken out. Sora uses a Gigas again to pile them closer to the 
vent)

Goofy: We'll need more than that.

(They find another pile in a room with multicolored blocks)

Donald: Getting closer.

(Once all the blocks have been gathered and piled up, three cones land on 
top of the green figure assembled and a fanfare plays. The figure, with a 
permanent surprised look on its face, leans over toward the wall, providing 
a path up to the vent)

Donald: Hey, is that...

Sora: A cactus?

(The vent cover falls open)

Goofy: Yep, and it's our way up to the dark corridor.

(The party makes their way to the vent and enters it, finding a corridor 
of darkness)

Sora: It looked like this?

Goofy: Yup.

Sora: Here goes.

(Sora and the group pass through the ominous portal, finding themselves 
in a hazy abyss. Buzz is hovering in the center, darkness coming off of 
him and spreading through the air. Young Xehanort waits for them, waves of 
dark energy covering the floor as pieces of toys are scattered about the 
abyss, floating on invisible strings)

Sora & Woody: Buzz!

Sora: Xehanort!

Woody: What do you want with my friend?

Young Xehanort: Look... Such tremendous darkness. All because he was ripped 
away from the boy who cares about him most.

(The waves punch upward)

Woody: Does that mean...we'll all be like Buzz...

(The waves coalesce around Woody)

Woody: ...if we don't...find Andy?

Sora: Wrong! Distance doesn't matter. Andy's part of their hearts, just 
like my friends are part of mine.

(Donald and Goofy nod in agreement, glaring at Xehanort)

Sora: You can't rip that apart!

(Woody looks at the bottom of his shoe where Andy had written his name 
years ago, and then at Buzz's, just the same. Buzz is carried higher by the 
waves as Xehanort raises an arm)

Young Xehanort: What? "Your friends are your power"? Ah... How very true. 
But if the light of friendship is a form of power...the darkness of being 
alone is a power...even greater. Darkness is the heart's true nature.

(Sora is stunned to silence, but Woody places a hand on his shoulder and 
walks past him)

Woody: Whatever you're talking about, I don't care. Put Buzz back the way 
he was, then get lost!

Young Xehanort: Or else what, toy?

Woody: Yeah, I am a toy. And a friend.

(Woody stamps down with his foot, breaking the waves of darkness slightly, 
revealing the floor underneath)

Woody: My guess is no one's ever loved you before. Because you know 
NOTHING about hearts and love.

(Sora joins him in their circle of light, both making steps forward)

Sora: There are hearts all around us, trying to connect. Your "loneliness" 
only made Woody and Buzz's connection stronger. THAT's the heart's true 
nature--to never, ever let go. Wherever they are, Andy and the other toys 
haven't let go either.

Woody: Yeah! You can't keep us from Andy. We're going home no matter what. 
And taking Buzz!

Sora: Xehanort, you're so caught up in finding the shadows, you forgot 
about the light that cast them.

(The force of light breaks through the dark waves, tearing apart the 
darkness holding Buzz in the air. As it reaches Buzz, it shines out with a 
brilliant light)

Young Xehanort: No!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy charge forward, forcing Xehanort to summon his 
Keyblade, blocking the three of them)

Sora: Woody, now!

(Woody leaps forward over them, tossing out the pullstring from his back. 
It latches onto a Lego floating in the air and Woody swings around, using 
the momentum to snatch Buzz from his tangled perch. Sora smiles as 
Xehanort scowls as the pullstring retracts back inside Woody with a message 
of "Giddy-up, partner! We gotta get this wagon train a-movin'!" Suddenly, 
Buzz opens his eyes, seeing Woody on top of him. Woody lifts his head and 
gazes back at his friend. He turns over and sits with Buzz, who holds his 
head)

Buzz: Woody... Wait, how did I get here?

Woody: Hmm. Oh, I don't know! (elbows him) Maybe somebody switched you 
into "dark and stormy" mode.

Buzz: But I don't have a--

(He realizes what Woody is saying. The cowboy extends a hand to him and 
Buzz smiles, taking it, getting to his feet)

Buzz: Thank you, Woody.

Woody: Good to have ya back, Buzz.

Donald: Hey, hurry up!

(The two of them look over to see the trio locked in combat with Xehanort)

Goofy: We can't hold him much longer!

Sora: Don't give up, guys!

(Young Xehanort knocks the three of them back)

Young Xehanort: So, even empty puppets can be given strong hearts. I am 
going to have to remember that.

(Buzz aims his laser beam at Young Xehanort)

Buzz: Remember this--our hearts will always be connected to Andy's. No 
matter what you do!

Woody: And that's something you'll never understand, because you're 
hollower than any toy.

Young Xehanort: But now I know a heart can be placed in the vessel of our 
choosing. For that, let me give you a parting gift to play with.

Sora: Wait!

(Sora runs at Xehanort and slashes right through him)

Young Xehanort (whispering): Find the hearts joined to yours.

Sora: Huh?

(Xehanort vanishes and Donald leaps up, pointing at the sky where the 
darkness has begun to break)

Buzz: There!

(The group rejoins as the darkness is swept up, forming a giant flying 
saucer Heartless, revealing the room as a toy-sized cityscape with a 
puzzle-piece road)

Woody: Careful!

Sora: Here goes.

(After a long battle with the King of Toys involving an electromagnetic 
tornado, they succeed in finishing off the Heartless and return to the 
first floor of Galaxy Toys. They regroup with their friends and begin 
walking toward the exit)

Goofy: So, Xehanort got away again.

Donald: Yeah, he's a big chicken.

(Sora hangs his head and stops walking)

Sora: I'm sorry!

(Woody, Buzz and the others turn back to him, confused)

Sora: I wanted to get you back to the real world.

(Woody and Buzz look at each other and smirk)

Buzz: It does seem that we're trapped here.

Rex: We'll never get home.

Hamm: Yeah, stuck like pigs.

Sarge: Our position appears fixed.

Little Green Men: Oh nooo.

(Donald and Goofy give a sad sigh)

Buzz: A shame we'll have to stay a little longer...with our new best 
friends.

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Huh?

(Woody walks up and leans on Sora's shoulder)

Woody: After all the adventures we've had, we're not quite ready to say, 
"So long."

(Sora laughs)

Sora: You guys...

(The space ranger extends a hand)

Buzz: I'm sorry that I was being so stubborn. Please forgive me.

(Sora shakes his head, smiling, and shakes Buzz's hand)

Sora: Hey, you were just looking out for your friends. No biggie.

Hamm: Yeah, somebody's gotta be the sensible one, especially since Woody's 
always gettin' in trouble.

Goofy: Gawrsh, that sounds a little like Sora, don't it?

(Sora and Woody exchange a look, pointing at themselves)

Donald: Yeah, and I'm the dependable one!

Rex: Like Buzz! ...Kinda.

(They all laugh)

Woody: Besides, if we do go back to the real world, we'll never see you 
again, right?

(Sora scratches his cheek)

Sora: But...what about Andy? You care about him so much.

(Buzz puts a hand on his shoulder)

Buzz: And he's still right here with us.

(He touches his heart, smiling. Woody puts an arm around Sora)

Woody: If we follow our hearts, we'll find him again.

Sora (grinning): Yeah!

(They continue walking to the exit)

Woody: So, Sora, are you goin' after the guy in the black coat?

Buzz: Something tells me we can't join you on that mission.

Woody: That's okay...because you've become part of our hearts.

(He points to Sora's heart)

Woody: So let us become a part of yours.

(The group extends joyous laughter and infectious smiles as Sora side-hugs 
Woody)

Sora: Thank you!

Buzz: Now, off you go. To infinity and beyond!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy leave the Toy Box and sail on again in the Gummi 
Ship. Sora sits in his chair with his hands behind his head and nowhere 
to go. Donald and Goofy walk to his chair)

Donald: Sora, what about the "power of waking"?

Sora: You HAD to remind me?

Goofy: Well, gawrsh, we just wanna help keep ya motivated.

Sora: I was thinking about Roxas. He's trapped here in my heart. But...
he needs a body to be himself again.

Goofy: Aw, don't worry. Ienzo's workin' on a way to get him free. I'll 
betcha he's got the perfect body all lined up.

(Jiminy Cricket hops out of Sora's hood)

Jiminy: You've got the Gummiphone, Sora. Why don't ya try givin' him a call?

Sora: Uhh, I guess so?

(He takes out the phone)

Sora: Yeah, why not.

(He dials and Mickey pops up on the screen)

Mickey: Oh! Hiya, Sora!

Donald & Goofy: Your Majesty!

(They shove themselves into the view of the camera)

Sora: Hey! Wha...? Wrong number?

Mickey: No, Riku and I are visiting Radiant Garden. Actually, we were 
just about to call you guys, but it looks like you beat us to the punch.

(Riku kneels down to Mickeys level as the King holds out the camera)

Riku: Sora, is something wrong?

Sora: I wanted to pick your brain. In order for us to recomplete Roxas, 
he needs a body, right?

Mickey: Yeah, to put his heart in.

(There is a moment of near silence among them while they think, the only 
sound from the water fountain at Radiant Garden. Riku gets an idea)

Riku: Replicas...

Sora: Huh?

Riku: Well, replicas are basically human.

Sora: Uh, what?

Riku: Oh, yeah... You wouldn't remember. The previous Organization XIII 
developed "replicas": realistic vessels to place hearts in. They're so 
real, in fact, that you'd actually mistake them for people. And with 
hearts, the replicas will BECOME people.

Sora: Cool, but if we get our hands on a replica, will Roxas look like 
himself when he's recompleted?

Riku: Yup. The replica takes the form of the heart inside it.

(He remembers his doppelganger from the events at Castle Oblivion)

Sora: That's perfect!

Mickey: I'll talk to Ienzo. He was in the Organization back then, so he 
might know more.

Sora: Great. Thanks. Wait... (to Donald & Goofy) Do you guys think THEY'RE 
after replicas too?

Goofy: No, they definitely said "a black box."

Riku: Who's that?

Sora: The Organization and Maleficent.

(They look slightly ashamed)

Donald: I guess we forgot to mention it.

Mickey: Aw, it's okay. But there's something you guys should know about 
one of their members.

Sora: Huh?

(They explain what they discovered about Terra)

Mickey: So, let the rest of us worry about Roxas and Namin for now. You 
journey on, and keep an eye out for Terra.

(Donald and Goofy block Sora again)

Donald & Goofy: Yes, Your Majesty!

Sora: Stop that!

(They hang on as Mickey and Riku chuckle)

Mickey: They don't change, do they?

(Riku stands)

Riku: Nope, that's their best quality.

Mickey: Welp, we gave Merlin the vestments for Kairi and Axel. Let's go 
stop by Ansem the Wise's study.

Riku: Right.

(Sora pilots the Gummi Ship to a new world with a tall tower in the 
middle of a deep forest, the Kingdom of Corona)

????????: Why can't I go outside?

??????: The outside world is a dangerous place. You must stay here, where 
you're safe. Do you understand, flower?

(A girl sits at the window of a tower gazing at night sky, her unusually 
long hair trailing to the floor behind her. Her lonely look changes upon 
seeing the floating lights in the sky)

Rapunzel: Those lights appear every year on my birthday--only on my 
birthday. And I can't help but feel like they're...they're meant for me. 
I need to see them. And not just from my window... In person. I have to 
know what they are.

(Some time later, Sora, Donald and Goofy walk through a picturesque 
forest. Goofy puts his hand up to block the sun)

Goofy: It sure is a pretty day.

(Sora stretches)

Sora: Yeah, the weather is great. It'd be perfect for a picnic.

Donald: Why do you think we came HERE?

Sora: Got me, Donald.

Goofy: We'll figure it out as we go.

Donald (sighing): Okay.

Sora: I'm sure we were brought to this world for SOME good reason, but 
can't we sweat it later?

Donald: Fine with me, as long as there's no Heartless.

(They hear a scream and stop in their tracks, looking around for the 
source of it. Then with grunting and a final slide, a man falls down the 
hill behind them. He groans, massaging his back, then looks back where he 
came from, where a troop of Heartless fly down after him. The man gets up 
and scampers away, the satchel on his hip flapping with every step. He runs 
toward the trio with the Heartless on his tail, flailing his arms wildly)

?????: Make way! Make way! Make way!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy part so he can pass them, then summon their weapons)

Sora: Heartless!

(The man finds a rock to hide behind, catching his breath and peering out 
at the group)

Sora: You see? Soon as you mention 'em, they show up!

Goofy: There goes our picnic.

Donald: I didn't do it!

Sora: S'okay. Let's send these guys packing.

?????: Say, since you three seem to know what you're doing, mind if I 
leave this one to you?

Sora: Yup. We'll take care of them. Go on, skedaddle!

?????: You have my thanks.

(The dashing man gives off a sigh)

?????: The horse was enough. Don't need any monsters on my trail.

Donald: The WHAT was enough?

?????: Oh, nothing, nothing. Name's Flynn. Flynn Rider. (pointing) Ohh! 
Watch out, they look mad!

(Donald turns around again and Flynn starts creeping away)

Flynn: Slowly... Slowly... Outta here!

(He dashes away as fast as he can while Sora, Donald and Goofy take out 
the multitude of Heartless. After the fight, they see no sign of Flynn Rider)

Sora: Huh? Where'd Flynn go?

Donald: He skedaddled.

Goofy: I think I saw him go thataway.

(He points toward a spot between the trees that veers into a small clearing 
with rocky hills on each side)

Sora: Huh? But "thataway" is...just a dead end.

Goofy: Yeah. That's puzzling.

Donald: Well, did he?

(Goofy crosses his arms, thinking)

Sora: I say we investigate.

(They search the area for Flynn and approach the rocky hillside ahead)

Donald: He couldn't have come this way.

(Sora sees no exit nearby and turns to face Donald & Goofy, his back to 
a patch of leafy vines)

Sora: Well, at least he got away safe. Right?

(He tries to lean against the vines, but stumbles right through them. Goofy 
turns at the rustling sound, but Sora has disappeared)

Goofy: Hey! Now Sora's gone, too!

(Goofy walks over to the vines and hears Sora's voice through them)

Sora: This way, guys! It's a secret passage!

(Sora stands up as Goofy and Donald pull the vines apart to find a small 
hollow in the mountain. They run through the cave until emerging into a 
small valley with a lone tower standing in its center. Made mostly of 
brick, the tower has vines running along its side indicating it must have 
been there for years. Behind the tower, a waterfall runs over the 
mountainside into a small pond that glistens in the sunlight. Inside 
the tower, Flynn wakes up tied to a green chair by yards and yards of 
golden hair. He struggles to get free and raises an eyebrow as Rapunzel 
steps from the shadows wielding a frying pan. Flynn takes the opportunity 
and gives her the smolder)

Flynn (suave): How you doing? The name's Flynn Rider. How's your day 
going? Huh?

(Rapunzel is unfazed and decides to brandish the frying pan, making Flynn 
wince)

Rapunzel: Who else knows my location, Flynn Rider?

Flynn: All right, hang on, Blondie.

Rapunzel: Rapunzel.

Flynn: Gesundheit. Here's the deal. I was in a situation, gallivanting 
through the forest when I stumbled upon a--

(His eyes go wide)

Flynn: Oh! Oh no no! No no no! Where is my satchel?

(He looks frantically around the room from his position in the chair)

Rapunzel: I've hidden it. Somewhere you'll never find it.

(She continues to threaten him with the culinary club)

Rapunzel: So, what do you want with my hair? To cut it? Sell it?

(She walks around the chair, her hair twisting over Flynn's legs)

Rapunzel: Sell it?

Flynn: No!

Rapunzel: Wait. You DON'T want my hair?

Flynn: Why on earth would I want your hair? Look, I was being chased, I 
saw a tower, I climbed it, okay? End of story.

(Rapunzel looks him over hesitantly before a tiny green chameleon emerges 
onto her shoulder, narrowing his eyes at the sight of Flynn. The chameleon 
looks back at Rapunzel, uncurling his tail and motioning with it, points 
toward the door to her right. She walks over, and Flynn again struggles 
to escape. After convening with her chameleon, Rapunzel places him back 
onto her shoulder)

Rapunzel: Okay, Flynn Rider. I'm prepared to offer you a deal.

Flynn (stops): A deal?

Rapunzel: Look this way.

(She pulls on the chair, twirling him around, and steps onto the fireplace, 
toppling him and the chair over)

Rapunzel: Do you know what these are?

(She pulls apart a red curtain where a mural of the floating lights has 
been painted on the wall. Flynn looks up from his squished position on 
the floor)

Flynn: You mean the lantern thing they do for the princess?

Rapunzel: Lanterns? I knew they weren't stars. Well, tomorrow evening they 
will light the night sky with these "lanterns."

(She points at him with the frying pan)

Rapunzel: YOU will act as my guide, take me to these lanterns, and return 
me home safely. Then, and only then, will I return your satchel to you. That 
is my deal.

Flynn: Yeah... No can do. Unfortunately...

(He lifts himself up with his hands and flips the chair onto its side)

Flynn: ...the Kingdom and I aren't exactly "simpatico" at the moment,

(He includes the air quotes)

Flynn: ...so I won't be taking you anywhere.

(The chameleon appears again and locks eyes with Rapunzel, making a 
punching motion with his front legs. She puts down the frying pan and 
jumps from the fireplace, gathering the strand of hair attached to the 
chair into her arms)

Rapunzel: Something brought you here, Flynn Rider. 

(She tugs on the chair, getting it to stand up)

Rapunzel: Call it what you will: fate, destiny...

(She walks forward, gripping at her hair with each step closer)

Rapunzel: So I have made the decision to trust you.

Flynn (sarcastically): A horrible decision, really.

Rapunzel: I am serious.

(She pulls again, the chair leaning forward, and catches it, her face 
inches from his. He pauses, clearing his throat)

Flynn: Let me get this straight. I take you to see the lanterns, bring you 
back home...then you'll give me back my satchel?

Rapunzel: I promise.

(His eyes narrow slightly)

Rapunzel: And when I promise something, I never, ever break that promise.

(He raises an eyebrow)

Rapunzel: Ever.

(She stares at him intensely)

Flynn (thinking): Oh, what to do? I cannot let her find that tiara. Okay, 
just think... I need the satchel and Blondie has it. There might be more 
monsters out there... I've got it! The three guys in the funny outfits. 
They looked tough enough to come in handy.

(He smirks)

Flynn: All right fine, I'll take you.

(She smiles brightly)

Flynn: But on one condition: my three sidekicks come along.

(He turns his head with a smile. Meanwhile, Sora, Donald and Goofy admire 
the tower in the glade)

Sora: Look at that. A tower! Let's check it out!

(As they near the base of the tower, they see Flynn climbing down the 
stones on the outside with a pair of arrows. He pauses, resting for a 
moment, when Rapunzel flings her hair down out the window, rappelling 
herself down the tower. She stops before she hits the ground and slowly 
extends a bare foot to the warm grass beneath. She takes in the feeling 
of her first taste of earth and kneels down, feeling the ground under her 
hands)

Rapunzel: It's so soft!

(Several dandelion seeds fly into the wind before her and she stands)

Rapunzel: I'm free... I'm really free!

(She starts running, not even noticing the trio as she passes them. Sora, 
Donald and Goofy run over to Flynn as he reaches the bottom of the tower)

Sora: Flynn, good to see you in one piece!

Flynn: Guys! You're here, and just in time.

(Rapunzel steps into the pond, laughing as she steps over the small stones 
lining the bottom)

Sora: Oh... Who's she?

Flynn: Uh, that would be Rapunzel.

(She takes a handful of water and splashes it upwards with a shout of 
glee and loud laughter)

Flynn: Something tells me this could be her first time outdoors. Give her 
a few minutes to get used to it.

Sora (wide-eyed): First time EVER?

(The sun beats down on her golden hair as she takes in her decision. She 
grabs her face)

Rapunzel (happily): I can't believe I did this!

(She grabs her head)

Rapunzel (shocked): I can't believe I did this.

(She spins around)

Rapunzel (excited): I can't believe I DID this!

(She gasps)

Rapunzel (worried): Mother would be so furious if she knew I disobeyed her 
and left the tower...

(She sits on a rock holding a flower)

Rapunzel (carefree): But that's okay--I mean, what she doesn't know won't 
kill her... Right? 

(She cries in the hollow cave)

Rapunzel (sadly): Oh my gosh. This would kill her.

(She runs through the grass, kicking up leaves. Donald laughs while Flynn 
rolls his eyes)

Rapunzel (shouting): This is so fuuuuuun!

(She leans her head against a tree)

Rapunzel (devastated): I am a horrible daughter. I'm going back.

(She does cartwheels through the flowers, wrapping herself in her hair)

Rapunzel (exhuberantly): I am never going back!

(She lies facedown on the ground)

Rapunzel (grief): I am a despicable human being.

(She swings around a large tree by her hair where Flynn and Sora wait for 
her to even out)

Rapunzel (exhilarated): Best. Day. Ever!

(She sobs into her hands at the base of the tree. Flynn walks over to her, 
with the trio following)

Flynn: I notice you seem a little at war with yourself here.

Goofy: A little MORE than a little.

Donald: More like a lot.

Sora: Yeah...

(She stops crying and turns to see them. She gasps and holds out the frying 
pan toward Sora, Donald and Goofy)

Rapunzel: Stop right there! Who are you?

(Flynn steps in-between them)

Flynn: I told you before: my sidekicks.

Sora: Sidekicks?

Flynn: May I introduce, ehh...

Sora: Oh, uh... My name's Sora.

Donald: Donald!

Goofy: And I'm Goofy. Pleasure, ma'am.

(The chameleon appears from under her hair, skeptical of them)

Rapunzel: Sora, Donald, and...Goofy.

(She lowers the frying pan)

Rapunzel: It's...nice to meet you, too. I'm Rapunzel.

Flynn: Yep. My sidekicks.

(Sora grabs Flynn's arm and spins him around)

Sora (whispering): Since when is THAT?

Flynn (whispering back): Look, she really wants to see the lantern show 
tomorrow night. Now, I'm a nice guy, so I've decided to help her. Only 
problem is those monsters might show up again. I can get her to the 
Kingdom--but you guys are clearly more cut out for combat.

Donald: That's cause we're heroes!

Flynn: Uh-huh!

Goofy: And we're Heartless experts.

Flynn: Yeah, yeah!

(They pose together and Sora gives a small laugh)

Sora: Just leave it to us!

Flynn: Done.

(Flynn motions to Rapunzel and leads her forward)

Donald: Rapunzel is interesting...

(The trio walks behind them as Rapunzel admires her surroundings)

Goofy: Yeah, her heart's pulling her all kinda ways.

Sora: The outside world must seem so big and scary. I know how she feels. 
Lucky for me you two came along at just the right time--and the rest has 
been unforgettable.

Donald: Awww...

(Sora realizes he's getting sentimental)

Sora: Yep, unforgettable...just like your face!

(He points at Donald, smiling)

Donald: Oh yeah?!

(Sora laughs as Donald bursts out in anger. Sora runs to catch up to 
Rapunzel and Flynn, putting his hands behind his head. Goofy chuckles 
as Donald seethes)

Goofy: C'mon, now.

(Goofy runs after Sora, and Donald follows)

Sora: All for one, and one for all.

(Soon, they reach a patch of wildflowers and something catches Rapunzel's 
attention)

Rapunzel: Oh, look. What is that? It's so fluffy!

(She runs up to the ball of fluff and inspects it, her fingers grazing 
the surface. Into the air sprout multiple tufts of fluff that, when the 
reach the ground, burst into Puffball Heartless. The Chief Puff itself 
pulls out of the ground and stares at her with its glowing yellow eyes, 
scaring her)

Sora: Heartless!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy run ahead of her and summon their weapons)

Sora: Rapunzel, take cover!

(She runs back to Flynn, throwing her arms around him and using him as a 
shield. At first he is surprised, but smirks soon after, seeing an out)

Flynn: All right, I hate to say it, but I'm lettin' you outta this deal.

(She loosens her grip on him)

Rapunzel: What?

Flynn: It's way too scary out here. Let's just turn around and take you home.

(He tries to get her to walk back, but she whirls around and punches him 
in the chest)

Rapunzel: No. I am seeing those lanterns.

(Rapunzel bravely gathers her hair in her arms and runs back to Sora and 
company)

Flynn: Oh, come on!

Sora: Rapunzel?

Rapunzel: It's okay. I'm not afraid to face them.

(They engage the plant-like Heartless and take them down. Meanwhile back 
at the tower, Mother Gothel has returned to find Rapunzel missing. She 
scrambles through the house in desperation)

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel?

(She runs into her room)

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel!

(She frantically tears down the curtain covering the window, but finds 
no one there. She clutches her face in terror before a glint of light 
catches her eye from beneath the stairs. She opens the bottom step and 
pulls out a satchel. Reaching into the satchel, she removes a sparkling 
tiara and at the sight of it, drops it in fear. Terrified, she looks 
further in the bag, taking out a Wanted poster for one Flynn Rider)

????????: Missing someone?

(She whirls around)

Mother Gothel: Who's there?

(Stepping out from a portal is a man in a black coat with long rose-colored 
hair. The abrupt entrance causes the frightened woman to drop the poster 
as Marluxia steps closer)

Marluxia: She's such a precious gift. Allow me to assist you in getting 
her back.

(Mother Gothel's eyes slowly turn pink. As Sora, Donald, Goofy, Rapunzel 
and Flynn continue their trek to the Kingdom, they find a large field of...)

Rapunzel: Dandelions!

(She runs ahead into the patch of flowers)

Rapunzel: Look! Watch.

(She kneels down and blows on a few of them, sending their seeds into the air)

Rapunzel: Oh yeah, I thought that might work. But I wish there was a way 
to make more fly at once.

(Sora summons an Aero spell, wafting the large patch of them into the air. 
The float past Rapunzel's wide-eyed stare)

Rapunzel: They're just like the floating lights.

(They continue along the path)

Rapunzel: Rabbits!

(They find a trio of rabbits)

Sora: Heartless!

(The rabbits run into the brush at the Heartless's appearance)

Rapunzel: Oh, no, you're not picking on these rabbits.

(After a brief brawl with the Heartless, the rabbits hop back out)

Rapunzel: Don't worry. It's safe now.

(They dash away)
Rapunzel: Oh, maybe they want to show us something. Let's follow them!

(They follow the rabbits to a chest hidden through a path in the trees)

Rapunzel: I think they want us to have this.

(The rabbits hop away)

Rapunzel: Thank you.

(Further through the forest, the group finds a small lake)

Rapunzel: Look at all this water!

(She dashes into the lake)

Rapunzel: It's so refreshing! You have to come in.

(Sora follows her into the lake, where she gives him a little splash)

Rapunzel: See? It feels nice.

Sora: My turn.

(He splashes her back)

Rapunzel: Sora!

(She splashes him again and he covers his face)

Sora: Okay. You're in for it!

(He summons the Keyblade and splashes the water into the air. The water 
droplets sparkle in the clear sun creating a band of colors)

Sora & Rapunzel: Whoa!

Rapunzel: A rainbow!

(They leave the lake and continue through the forest, Rapunzel's long hair 
trailing behind her as they come upon a strange plant stuck in the ground 
in a clearing alone)

Flynn: Okay. That's suspicious.

Sora: Rapunzel...

Rapunzel: Don't worry. I know to be careful around flowers now.

(She winks at him)

Sora: Whatever it is, it's not normal. I'll take a look.

(Sora walks closer)

Donald: Watch it.

(Sora approaches the odd vegetation and examines it while everyone waits 
with bated breath. After seeing no imminent threat from the flower, he 
turns to the group)

Sora: We're all clear.

(They sigh with relief, but too late, as the flower's petals open, folding 
downward as its form changes to that of a creature holding a scythe with 
a familiar symbol on its face)

Donald (alarmed): Sora!

(He points behind Sora, who turns just in time as the pink and white 
creature swings its immense scythe at him. Sora dodges away and summons 
his Keyblade with gritted teeth, joined by Donald and Goofy)

Sora: These guys?

(More of them appear)

Goofy: They're Nobodies!

Rapunzel: Mother said the outside world would be full of ruffians and thugs.

Donald: Those aren't ruffians. Those are...uhh, I dunno...

Sora: Rapunzel, Flynn, stay back!

Rapunzel: No. I want to help you fight.

Sora: I know. But I'm afraid you can't hurt these guys with a frying pan. 
Trust me on this. Flynn, could you explain?

Flynn: No problem. Knowing when to flee is one of my specialties.

(He rushes to Rapunzel)

Flynn: C'mon, Rapunzel. Gotta go.

Rapunzel: But--

Flynn: Look, I wanna stay and slug it out too, but my sidekicks have it 
covered.

(Sora nods with a smile)

Rapunzel: All right. Please be careful, Sora.

(They nod and leave them to it. Sora, Donald and Goofy take out all the 
Reaper Nobodies and regroup)

Goofy: You know who uses Nobodies...

Donald: The Organization!

Sora: Yeah. I'm surprised we haven't seen 'em. (calling out) I know you're 
there! Come out, you has-beens!

(They look around and a corridor of darkness appears behind them)

????????: "Has-beens"? Now why would you say that?

(A tall man with long pink hair emerges from the portal, peering at them 
through yellow eyes)

Sora: Because, bossing around Nobodies? That's the old Organization. 
(chuckling) Why? Are you in the "real" one too? Good for you.

????????: My name is Marluxia, and yes, that is correct. How interesting 
it is to see you again, Sora.

Sora: "Again"?

(He turns to Donald & Goofy)

Sora: YOU know 'im?

(Donald and Goofy shake their heads)

Marluxia: A shame you've no memory of me, because I remember you 
exceedingly well. Although...it's THOSE memories I'd soon erase.

Sora: I don't know what you're saying.

Marluxia: Nor should you. Nor will you ever, for that matter.

(They glance at him with confused faces)

Marluxia: Now, if you'll permit me, I've come to ask a favor.

Sora: Favor? You have got to be kidding me.

(Donald & Goofy nod in agreement)

Marluxia: Please hear what I have to say. I'm sure you've noticed...

(He muses on this for a moment and Sora raises his eyebrows for him to 
continue)

Marluxia: Well, perhaps not. But you should know that maiden with you, 
Rapunzel, is the very light of this world. I would see you guard her 
from its dark horrors.

Sora, Donald & Goofy (surprised): Huh? 

(They take defensive stances)

Sora: Starting with you, right?

Marluxia: All the Organization seeks is balance. You must understand, 
our ultimate objective is not to clash with the light. We seek to 
complement it. Use that Keyblade...to keep Rapunzel safe.

(He vanishes in a corridor of darkness)

Sora: Rapunzel's light...

(Goofy scratches his face and Sora looks around)

Sora: Hey. Where did they go?

Goofy: I guess they musta run on ahead.

Sora: Then we'd better go find them.

(They continue through the forest in search of Flynn and Rapunzel)

Donald: This might be a good spot to find some ingredients.

(Soon the forest turns into marshland and the fog obscures their view 
ahead. Still no sign of them, Sora sighs)

Sora: I wonder where they went.

Goofy: Don't worry. They couldn't have gotten too far.

(A hooded figure quickly hides behind a tree)

Donald: You just had to stop and talk.

(Mother Gothel peers at them from beneath her cloak)

Sora: Hey! Blame the has-been, not me.

Goofy: I think you mean Marluxia. I bet that's the name the has-been 
would prefer.

(Mother Gothel averts her gaze and begins to leave)

Sora (calling): Hellooo? Rapunzel? Flynn?

(She stops at Rapunzel's name and turns back, lowering her hood)

Mother Gothel: Excuse me, good travelers. Do you know Rapunzel?

(They turn to her as she walks toward them and exchange glances)

Sora: Uh, yeah... Sort of.

Donald: Why?

Mother Gothel: My apologies. I'm Rapunzel's mother. The poor child left 
home without a word, and I've just been worried sick. Please tell me: 
where is my dear, sweet girl?

Goofy: We'd tell ya, but we lost her.

Donald: By accident.

Sora: We could look together.

Mother Gothel: Lost her? (scoffs) You're of no use to me.

(She waves them off and continues walking)

Mother Gothel: I'll find her myself.

Donald: She ran away from home?

Sora: What if Marluxia was onto something back there?

Donald: You trust Organization XIII?

Sora: What? No! Of course not. But...what if?

Goofy: I agree. Why is Rapunzel in danger, and what darkness is after her?

Sora: Well, guys, the first step is to find her.

(They search for Rapunzel and Flynn, eventually exiting the marshland 
into more bright forest. Soon, they hear a voice)

Rapunzel: Wh-wh-whoa! Whoa, whoa, whoa, whoa. Easy, boy, easy! Settle 
down. Whoa, whoa!

Sora: That voice!

Goofy: It's Rapunzel!

(Ahead, a terrified Flynn has his back pressed against a rock while 
Rapunzel attempts to calm down a large white horse. The angry-looking 
horse peers at the chameleon atop Rapunzel's head. Pascal motions with 
his three-toed front feet to settle down. The horse, wide-eyed, raises 
an ear and sets his rump down on the ground with a dispirited whinny)

Rapunzel: You are such a good boy! Yes you are.

(She pets the bridge of his nose and his tail starts to wag)

Rapunzel: Are you all tired from chasing this bad man all over the place?

(The horse nods sadly)

Flynn: Excuse me?

Rapunzel: Nobody appreciates you, do they?

(Rapunzel moves closer to give him a hug)

Rapunzel: Do they?

(The horse shakes his head)

Flynn: Oh, come on. He's a bad horse!

Rapunzel: Ohhh. He's nothing but a big sweetheart.

(The horse nuzzles against her)

Rapunzel: Isn't that right...

(She scratches under his chin and peers at the name on his collar)

Rapunzel: Maximus?

(Maximus stamps his foot and whinnies at the attentive petting as Flynn 
gripes on the forest floor)

Flynn: Wha... You've got to be kidding me.

(Maximus glares at him)

Rapunzel: Look, today is kind of the biggest day of my life, and the thing 
is, I need you NOT to get him arrested.

(Rapunzel helps Flynn up and Maximus narrows his eyes at her)

Rapunzel: Just for twenty-four hours, and then you can chase each other 
to your hearts' content. Okay?

(Flynn begrudgingly offers a hand, but Maximus refuses, looking away)

Rapunzel: And it's also my birthday. Just so you know.

(Maximus grumbles softly and offers his hoof. They shake, their scowls 
unbroken. Rapunzel looks ahead, seeing the trio running toward them)

Sora: Rapunzel!

Rapunzel: You're here. And you're okay!

(Behind Rapunzel's back, Maximus punches Flynn in the side and smirks)

Sora: Yeah! You too.

Rapunzel: And look! I made a friend.

(The horse walks over)

Rapunzel: Meet Maximus. You could say Flynn introduced us. And where one 
goes, the other follows.

(Maximus inspects them dubiously)

Rapunzel: This is Sora, Goofy, and Donald. They've been helping me.

(He nods. Flynn gets up, clutching his side and pointing onward)

Flynn (grunting): Come on, the Kingdom's not far.

(They make their way through the wetlands and rocky cliffs where they 
find a clearing with an odd looking tower on wheels. A Powerwild Heartless 
smacks its monkey-butt at them summoning a multitude of Powerwilds. The 
tower shoots cannonballs at them as they attempt to dispose of the 
surrounding Heartless. Once the Powerwilds are gone, the tower's three 
sections topple to the ground and a horse-like Heartless bursts from 
one of the windows, effectively becoming a carriage)

Sora: Whoa, what? It transformed!

Flynn: What is it with me and horses?

(They defeat the Chaos Carriage and enter the Wildflower Clearing)

Rapunzel: Oh, look! I see some birds! This way!

(She runs up to them, but they flutter away)

Rapunzel: Wait! Come back! I must have startled them.

(Sora approaches the birds carefully and guides them to Rapunzel. One of 
the bluebirds sits on his hand and he shows it to her)

Rapunzel: I've never seen a bird like you.

(They gather around Rapunzel and chirp out a song)

Rapunzel: Listen. They're singing for us!

(She smiles and they watch the birds fly off. After sliding down a giant 
hill of flowers, they reach the edge of the Kingdom in full view of the 
castle)

Rapunzel: I just knew the outside world would be full of amazing things!

(Sora walks over)

Rapunzel: And you...you helped me find them. Thank you.

(They cross the bridge and enter the castle town, Rapunzel giggling to 
herself all the way)

Sora: Rapunzel sure looks happy.

Donald: She does.

Goofy: Well, her dream's gonna come true. They're sendin' the lanterns 
up after dark.

Sora: Cool! We don't wanna miss that!

(They enter the Thoroughfare, where Rapunzel has her hair braided and 
adorned with wildflowers. She spots a large tiled mural of the king and 
queen holding their baby daughter. She peers down where a girl is placing 
a flower at its base)

Girl: It's for the lost princess.

(Rapunzel looks up at the baby on the mural, who has green eyes and 
flowing blonde hair just like her. Music starts suddenly, distracting 
her, and she gleefully begins dancing in the street. A crowd of people 
gather around and join in and Flynn stands watching her)

Rapunzel: C'mon, everyone! Come dance with us!

(Sora joins in dancing with the townsfolk)

Rapunzel: This is so fun!

(They dance around the sun-shaped circle of stones on the ground. Maximus 
notices Flynn leaning against him and knocks him forward into the crowd)

Flynn: Hey!

(Flynn scowls at Maximus as Sora grabs his hand, the horse laughing. 
Everyone joins in the sunwheel dance and Sora gives Rapunzel a high-five. 
Flynn and Rapunzel spin into each other's arms as the music stops. They 
pause for a moment looking into the other's eyes)

Citizen: To the boats!

(They break apart at the distraction with soft surprise. The sun sets 
and the trio watch from one of the docks, Maximus from another, as Rapunzel 
and Flynn take a boat to the middle of the lake. They gaze up at the castle 
against the darkly lit sky)

Rapunzel: I've been looking out a window for eighteen years, dreaming 
about what it might feel like when those lights rise in the sky. What if 
it's not everything I dreamed it would be?

Flynn (calmly): It will be.

Rapunzel: And what if it is? What do I do then?

Flynn: Well, that's the good part, I guess. You get to go find a new dream.

(They look up as a solitary lantern peeks out from behind the castle, 
floating slowly up into the sky. Rapunzel hastily stands up, rocking the 
boat and grasping at the stern, as multitudes of floating lanterns pool 
out of the castle gates. Soon the entire kingdom is enveloped in a flock 
of lights floating softly into the air. Rapunzel leans her head on the 
wood as she gazes longingly at the magical sight. She turns back to Flynn 
holding two of his own in his hands. She happily sits back down)

Rapunzel: I have something for you, too.

(She pulls out his satchel and he stares at it)

Rapunzel: I should have given it to you before, but I was just scared. And 
the thing is, I'm not scared anymore. You know what I mean?

(He places a hand on the satchel and moves for her to put it down)

Flynn: I'm starting to.

(They set free their lanterns and they join the swirling bunch in the sky. 
Flynn gazes at Rapunzel, seeing the happiness on her face, then looks 
toward the satchel, thinking to himself. When the festival dies down, 
they dock the boat on the edge of the lake and Flynn gets out)

Flynn: I'm sorry. Everything is fine. There's...just something I have to 
take care of.

(He grabs the satchel and she looks back and forth between it and him)

Rapunzel: Okay.

(Backing away slowly)

Flynn: I'll be right back.

(He turns to leave and Pascal climbs onto her shoulder)

Rapunzel: It's all right, Pascal.

(They both sadly watch him go. From Sora's place at the dock, they watch 
the lights in the sky)

Sora (gasping): Wow!

(They sense a disturbance from behind as Reaper Nobodies appear on the 
wharf. They get up and turn around, irked)

Sora: Could you guys have possibly picked a worse time?

Goofy: I don't think they appreciate the moment, Sora.

Donald: Not one bit!

Sora: It's time for these wet blankets to go!

(They summon their weapons)

Donald & Goofy: Yeah!

(They take care of the Nobodies plaguing the wharf as Rapunzel waits 
by the shore with Pascal. Out of the fog over the water emerges a small 
sailboat)

Rapunzel: Eugene?

(From shore, she sees what looks like Flynn steering the sailboat with 
the stolen tiara in his hand)

Rapunzel: Eugene!

(Unknown to Rapunzel, he is out cold and tied to the mast and helm)

Marluxia: Oh dear... He's run off with the crown and forgotten you.

(Marluxia appears behind her)

Rapunzel: No. He wouldn't. Who are you?

(He doesn't answer and she looks back at the boat, still drifting away)

Marluxia: Forget Flynn Rider. You know where you belong, and it's not with 
him. Now...

(He motions with his hand and two Reaper Nobodies appear in front of 
Rapunzel. She runs away in fear and Marluxia smiles. She runs toward an 
opening between two large rocks, trying not to stumble when her braided 
hair catches on a fallen log. She pulls on it, trying to free it from 
the branch, when she hears a voice)

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel!

Rapunzel: Mother?

(Rapunzel walks back to the shoreline, where the Nobodies have dis-
integrated and Mother Gothel stands with a tree branch in her arms, 
out of breath. She perks up at the sight of Rapunzel)

Mother Gothel: Oh, my precious girl!

Rapunzel: Mother...

(She runs into Mother Gothel's arms)

Mother Gothel: Are you all right? Are you hurt?

(She touches Rapunzel's face)

Rapunzel: M-Mother, how did you--

Mother Gothel: I was so worried about you, dear. So I followed you. And 
I saw them attack you, and--

(She hugs her tightly)

Mother Gothel: Oh my. Let's go. Let's go, before they come to.

(Rapunzel stops and looks back at the boat on the lake. She slowly turns 
back to Mother Gothel, holding a green lantern in her hand. Rapunzel 
pauses as Mother Gothel sets the lantern down and opens her arms, 
beckoning her. Rapunzel's lip quivers and she starts to cry, running 
into her mother's embrace. Mother Gothel strokes her hair as she sobs. 
Sora, Donald and Goofy enter and see the two leaving)

Sora: Hey, isn't that Rapunzel?

(He cups his hands to his face)

Sora (shouting): Wait! Rapunz--

(Marluxia appears in front of them)

Marluxia: Show some decorum.

Donald: You again!

Sora: Marluxia!

Marluxia: The girl has found her dear mother. You should let them be.

Sora: And why is that?

Marluxia: Because Rapunzel is far too important. Atop her tower, she must 
remain out of sight, and live out her days with Mother Gothel.

Goofy: And never see anyone else?

Sora: But that's like...locking her in some prison!

Marluxia: That is EXACTLY what it's like. Rapunzel's hair holds the 
powerful magic of healing. And yes, Mother Gothel wants it for herself. As 
do others. And, if Mother Gothel's actions will protect Rapunzel, preserve 
her...then she is doing the Organization a favor.

Sora: What favor?

Marluxia: Let's say she's keeping Rapunzel on the shelf for us. An extra 
pawn in case you fail to find the remaining guardians of light, and we have 
occasion to call on other hearts of light instead. A New Seven Hearts to 
fill out the ranks.

Sora: "New Seven Hearts"?

Marluxia: Yes. Seven who inherited the princesses' light after their role 
was fulfilled.

Sora: So, you don't care about her. You guys just want Rapunzel for your 
own purposes! Well, you're done here!

(He summons his Keyblade)

Marluxia: Hmph. I just knew you would go and make a scene. Very well, then 
it's lights out for you.

(Marluxia extends a hand, blowing a pink wind toward Sora. He drops the 
Keyblade, his eyes drooping)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(They run towards him as his vision gets hazy, his ears muffled)

Marluxia: You always were such a sound sleeper.

(Sora falls to the ground. Meanwhile, Rapunzel lay in bed, her hair flowing 
throughout the floor. She clutches a purple cloth while Pascal looks on. She 
stares up at her ceiling where many of her paintings are. Her eyes grow 
wider and she holds up the cloth where a golden sun is stitched into the 
fabric. Rapunzel looks back and forth from the cloth to the ceiling. She 
sits up to get a closer look, her eyes widening, and she gasps as she 
sees the exact same symbol etched into the paintings on the wall. Over 
and over and over again. They shine down at her, now impossible to miss. She 
sees it in her eye, the symbol of the royal family. Her mind flies to 
the mural in the city plaza with the baby with the golden hair. She 
imagines placing the tiara on her head, her crown as the lost princess of 
Corona. This realization hits her like a cannonball and she falls into the 
vanity in her room, knocking over the stool. The loud thud alerts Mother 
Gothel, who begins ascending the stairs. Rapunzel tries to catch her breath 
as Mother Gothel approaches her room. Rapunzel pulls apart the curtains to 
the stairway)

Rapunzel (softly): I am the lost princess.

Mother Gothel (scoffing): Please speak up, Rapunzel. You know how I hate 
the mumbling.

Rapunzel (louder): I am the lost princess. Aren't I?

(She glares at Mother Gothel, whose eyes grow wide)

Rapunzel: Did I mumble, Mother? Or should I even call you that?

Mother Gothel (dismissively): Oh, Rapunzel. Do you even hear yourself?

(She walks closer)

Mother Gothel: Why would you ask such a ridiculous question?

(She smiles, chuckling it off. She opens her arms only for Rapunzel to 
push her away)

Rapunzel: It was you! It was ALL you!

(Mother Gothel's eyes narrow)

Mother Gothel: Everything I did was to protect YOU.

(Rapunzel pushes past her and rushes down the stairs)

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel...

(She goes after Rapunzel)

Rapunzel: I've spent my entire life hiding from people who would use me 
for my power...

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel!

Rapunzel: When I should have been hiding from you!

Mother Gothel: Where will you go? He won't be there for you.

Rapunzel: What did you do to him?

(Mother Gothel smirks evilly)

Mother Gothel: That criminal's to be hanged for his crimes.

Rapunzel (worried): No...

(Mother Gothel slithers around Rapunzel)

Mother Gothel: Now, now, it's all right. Listen to me. All of this is as 
it should be.

(She goes to pat Rapunzel on the head, but Rapunzel grabs her hand)

Rapunzel: No! You were wrong about the world. And you were wrong about me.

(Mother Gothel struggles in Rapunzel's grip)

Rapunzel: And I will NEVER let you use my hair again!

(Mother Gothel tugs against Rapunzel, the effort causing her to step back 
into the full-length mirror behind her, shattering it into pieces on the 
rug. Her breath comes quick and she looks back at Rapunzel, who walks away 
from her. Mother Gothel seeths with a dark aura)

Mother Gothel: You want me to be the bad guy? Fine. Now I'm the bad guy.

(Meanwhile, a recently escaped Flynn dashes on Maximus over the bridge 
away from the city. The morning sun brightens the sky as he rides toward 
the forest, encountering Donald and Goofy hovering over a still-sleeping 
Sora)

Flynn: Whoa, Max! Whoa, boy.

(They slide just short of them)

Goofy: Flynn!

Flynn: Is Sora okay?

Donald: We don't know.

Goofy: We keep callin' his name and shakin' him, but he won't open his eyes.

Donald: Sora!

Goofy: Wake up!

Flynn: Hmm... Unresponsive sidekick... Wait a minute. I know how to fix 
this! Max, give him a wash!

(Maximus licks Sora's face with his long tongue, rousing him from his 
sleep. Sora opens his eyes seeing Flynn and Maximus looking down at him. 
Donald and Goofy peek into view)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(Sora sits up)

Flynn: Well, that did the trick. Nice work, Max!

(Maximus smiles haughtily. Sora stands and holds his head)

Sora: Huh? How did I end up...

(The events come back to him)

Sora: Oh no! Flynn, Rapunzel's being held prisoner!

(Donald and Goofy nod)

Flynn: That's right. In her mother's tower.

(They trot forward)

Flynn: This calls for a rescue.

(He smiles down at Sora and extends a hand)

Flynn: Are you with me?

(Sora gives a small laugh)

Sora: Yeah.

(Flynn pulls Sora up onto the horse with a proud cackle. Donald jumps 
up onto Sora's shoulders and Goofy tags along on Maximus. Suddenly, they 
lose height)

Goofy: Uh-oh!

(Maximus's legs buckle, struggling to hold them up, but his face 
changes to one of determination. He lets out a whinny and stands straight up)

Flynn: Let's go, Max.

(Maximus rears back and charges forward. They race through the forest in 
the direction of the tower, when they are intercepted by a group of Nobodies)

Flynn: Whoa, whoa, whoa, whoa, whoa, Max!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy nod to each other and jump off Maximus, summoning 
their weapons)

Sora: We'll take it from here, Flynn. Go help Rapunzel.

Flynn: Thanks!

(He takes off with Maximus, leaving the Nobodies to them. As they follow 
along through the forest, their path is filled with Heartless. They defeat 
each wave in turn. By the time they arrive, Flynn has climbed up and 
entered the tower)

Flynn: Rapunzel! I thought I'd never see you again.

(He looks up, seeing Rapunzel chained and gagged. Her eyes widen as Mother 
Gothel sneaks behind him, striking a hidden dagger into his side. Rapunzel 
struggles to get free, crying out as Flynn falls over onto the floor. 
Mother Gothel looks down at him, squirming in pain on the stone floor. She 
tugs on Rapunzel's chains trying to lead her deeper into the tower, the 
girl desperate to get free)

Mother Gothel: Rapunzel, really! Enough already! Stop fighting me!

(Rapunzel, pulling back, loses her balance and falls over, the gag slipping 
from her mouth)

Rapunzel: No! I won't stop! For every minute of the rest of my life, I will 
fight! I will never stop trying to get away from you! But...if you let me 
save him, I will go with you.

(Mother Gothel raises an eyebrow)

Flynn (grunting): No! No, Rapunzel...

(Flynn attempts to crawl on the floor but the pain is too great. Pascal 
looks on helplessly)

Rapunzel: I'll never run... I'll never try to escape. Just let me heal 
him...and you and I will be together--forever, just like you want. Every-
thing will be the way it was. I promise. Just like you want. Just...let 
me heal him.

(Mother Gothel releases Rapunzel and shackles Flynn)

Mother Gothel (to Flynn): In case you get any ideas about following us.

(Rapunzel rushes to Flynn's side)

Rapunzel: Eu...Eugene!

(She brushes the hair out of his eyes and he clutches his side, struggling 
to sit up against the wall. She checks at his wound, obviously bleeding)

Rapunzel: Oh, I'm so sorry. Everything is gonna be okay, though.

(She gathers her hair into her arms)

Flynn: No...Rapunzel...

Rapunzel: I promise. You have to trust me.

(She places the hair over his wound)

Flynn: No! I can't let you do this.

(They stare into each other's eyes)

Rapunzel: And I can't let you die.

Flynn: But if you do this...

(She touches his face)

Flynn: ...but if you do this, then you will die.

Rapunzel (whispering): Hey. It's gonna be all right.

(He gives the very smallest of smiles)

Flynn: Rapunzel... Wait.

(He begins to stroke her hair, his face moving closer to hers, and with 
a swift motion cuts off her hair with a shard of the broken mirror. His 
hand falls to the floor, dropping the glass, as her hair turns brown, its 
healing ability lost. She looks down at him in shock)

Rapunzel: Eugene, what--

(Absolute terror erupts from Mother Gothel's face)

Mother Gothel (screaming): No!

(From the strand in Rapunzel's hands, the once golden locks of hair turn 
a deep brown. Mother Gothel tries to gather them up in her arms before 
the magic is lost)

Mother Gothel: Oh no. No...

(Unable to stop the transformation, she grabs her hand, watching it become 
wrinkled and withered)

Mother Gothel: What have you done? What have you DONE?!

(The aging spreads across her body like a weed, her skin turning pale and 
her hair a pallid gray. She screams out in sudden shrieks, her body moving 
feebly, as she covers her decrepit face with her hood. She writhes about 
the room, crossing closer to the window, where Pascal pulls on the long 
bunch of hair, causing her to spill out of the tower. She screams as she 
falls, aging out of existence, the shroud flying downward through the air 
as Sora, Donald and Goofy reach the base of the tower. Marluxia watches 
from the hill)

Marluxia: Fallen to darkness... We can't allow her near our pure light now. 
Her presence would only cast a pall over it.

(He motions with his arm, suspending the cloak in midair surrounded by 
petals of pink. An orb of darkness bursts forth and branch-like limbs 
erupt from within, followed by a tail. Another set of limbs, and the 
creature crashes to the ground, the darkness pulling back, revealing a 
large tree-like Heartless, the Grim Guardianess. It growls down at Sora, 
Donald and Goofy, who summon their weapons)

Sora: What happened up there?

Donald: I don't know, but we have to stop that Heartless.

(The Grim Guardianess flies toward them, its tail moving like a serpent, 
as its large mane of leaves crashes to the ground, sending pollen 
everywhere. Donald and Goofy are sent into a sneezing fit as thorns 
surround Sora. He struggles to get free of the thorns' grip before the 
Heartless slithers around the tower, spiraling to the top. Sora breaks 
free from the thorny tether as cherries fall from the sky. Sora, Donald 
and Goofy race across the hill avoiding the cages of vines that block 
their way, as the cherry bombs explode on impact with the ground. Dodging 
the torrent of bombs, Sora reaches the tower and runs up its stone 
exterior. The Heartless is soon no match for Sora and his Keyblade and is 
knocked from the tower. Inside, Rapunzel clutches Flynn)

Rapunzel: Don't go. Stay with me, Eugene.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy ascend the tower, seeing Rapunzel over Flynn's 
body. She grabs his arm and places it against her hair)

Rapunzel (singing through tears): Flower, gleam and glow. Let your power 
shine. Make the clock reverse.

Flynn: Rapunzel.

(Flynn opens his eyes)

Rapunzel (singing): Bring back what once was mine.

(He touches her face)

Flynn: Hey. Rapunzel.

(She holds his hand)

Rapunzel: What?

Flynn: Rapunzel... You were my new dream.

(The tears well up in her eyes)

Rapunzel: And you were mine.

(Flynn blinks once more and his eyes close, his body falling limp. The 
trio look on sadly as she moves her hand toward his face)

Rapunzel (singing): Heal what has been hurt. Change the Fates' design. 
Save what has been lost. Bring back what once was mine.

(She moves her hand over his heart and leans in closer, her face nearly 
touching his, her song nearly a whisper)

Rapunzel: What once was mine.

(She sobs, a tear falling onto the rogue's skin. It settles there, 
glowing into the shape of a flower. A light bursts forth from Flynn's 
wound, wresting Rapunzel from her sorrow. Sora, Donald and Goofy stare 
open-mouthed at this sight. The healing magic swirls into the air like 
strands of hair, wisping around Rapunzel, her eyes wide. A six-pointed 
flower magically blooms from the wound, before the light disappears inside 
of him. She moves closer to his face, brushing the hair out of her eyes 
as Flynn slowly takes a breath and opens his eyes)

Flynn: Rapunzel...

(She gasps)

Rapunzel: Eugene.

Flynn: Did I ever tell you...I've got a thing for brunettes?

(He smiles and Rapunzel is overcome by joy)

Rapunzel: Eugene!

(She throws her arms around him and he leans on his side to embrace her. 
Sora, Donald and Goofy smile with glee and Sora throws his arms around 
the other two, grinning from ear to ear and Flynn tightens his hold on 
Rapunzel. Later, they all stand at the base of the tower, the warm 
sunlight bathing over them)

Sora: Wow, Rapunzel! You're finally gonna get to see your real home.

Rapunzel: I know! I mean...I can't believe it. I can finally be with my 
real family! I couldn't have done it without your help.

Donald: You're welcome.

(She giggles)

Flynn: Well, from where I'm standing, the Kingdom couldn't ask for a 
better princess. And I couldn't have asked for better sidekicks!

(Sora brushes a knuckle across his nose)

Flynn: Thanks.

Rapunzel: Yes, thank you so much.

Donald: Happily ever after.

(Sora crosses his arms)

Sora: Mm-hmm.

Goofy: Now, Flynn, you and Maximus play nice.

(Maximus and Flynn exchange glances)

Flynn: Huh?

(Maximus whinnies with laughter)

Flynn (smiling): Fine.

(Rapunzel takes Flynn's hand and they stare into each other's eyes)

Sora: You're gonna be great.

Rapunzel & Flynn: Huh?

Sora: We haven't seen the guy controlling the monsters in a while, so 
that's one less worry.

Goofy: But there's still a chance that he might be around here somewhere.

Sora: Well, if he comes back and tries to bother Rapunzel again, then 
Flynn will keep her safe. And we three wont be far behind.

Donald: Come on. Rapunzel's the tough one, if you ask me.

Flynn: True. But nevertheless, I won't let her out of my sight.

Rapunzel (smiling): Oh... Eugene.

Sora: "Eugene"?

Flynn (chuckling): Oh! That's my real name. Eugene Fitzherbert. That's 
right. I never told you guys.

Donald: That's different.

Goofy: I think it's a great name!

Sora: Me too. Nice to re-meet you, Eugene.

Rapunzel (to Eugene): Hey! I thought I was the only one you were going to 
tell.

Eugene (to Rapunzel): Don't worry. I've saved plenty of Fitzherbert-y 
secrets just for you.

Rapunzel (to Eugene): Really?

Sora (pointing): Hey! What are you two lovebirds talking about?

Eugene: Nothing!

(Rapunzel giggles)

Rapunzel: Nothing.

Donald: Hey, you can tell us!

Goofy: Yeah, it's not nice to keep secrets.

Eugene: This one is none of your business.

(Sora chuckles)

Sora: Maximus, get him!

Eugene: Huh?

(Maximus glares at Eugene, an inch from his face, and Eugene stops, 
unsure of what to anticipate. Pascal crawls onto Rapunzel's shoulder 
with a determined look and jumps over to Eugene's, sending his long 
sticky tongue into his ear. Eugene reels back and clutches his ear, 
Pascal jumping off with a squeal of glee)

Eugene: You have got to be kidding me!

(Rapunzel and the rest burst out laughing. Maximus smiles at Eugene, 
waggling his eyebrows as Pascal chills on Eugene's head. Soon after, 
the trio leaves the Kingdom of Corona. Meanwhile, Maleficent and Pete 
look over the sun-lit valley)

Pete: ANOTHER world where we got doodly-squat.

Maleficent: Hmph.

Pete: You sure this box thingy's even real?

Maleficent: Yes.

Pete: Yeah, and just how do you know that?

Maleficent: It is etched.

(She turns away from him)

Pete: It's what?

(She opens a corridor of darkness before her)

Maleficent: Come with me.

Pete: Where to? Those bozos ain't gonna help us. Sora's sure not lookin' 
for the box.

Maleficent: Who said anything about following them?

(She enters the portal and Pete gives a muffled whimper before following

Mickey: What? We're too late?

(Aeleus says nothing, simply shaking his head)

Mickey: That's not good.

Ienzo: Unfortunately, his work on the replicas was incomplete. There may

(He motions to the computer beside him)

Ienzo: There's no place that he could go now that he's human. He has no

(Riku realizes something)

Riku: To fill out their ranks.

(Ienzo and Aeleus exchange glances)

Mickey: We'd better go tell Master Yen Sid. And Sora, and the others, too!

(Riku nods. In the Badlands on the outskirts of the Keyblade Graveyard,

(He lifts a finger to the rat, who high-fives it confidently. Later, Sora,

Goofy: Well, ya both scared me.
