Sora: Wonder what kind of weirdos live here...

Goofy (to Donald): Who'da thunk he'd get so creeped out?

??????: Weeee!

???: Boo.

(Mike rushes over to a giant control panel)

Mike: Yup! This is the central control unit for the whole factory! Now 
whaddaya say we get outta here?

(Sora runs over to the control panel, Donald following behind)

Sora: Let me.

(Mike throws his hands up with anxiety)

Donald: I'll do it!

Mike: Hey, hey! Show a little finesse!

(Mike runs over and Sora & Donald get out of his way. He presses a few 
buttons and then slams his fist on the control board)

Mike: Rats! Randall must have messed this up. Nothin' works!

(More buttons, but the result is the same)

Donald: We can't get out?

Goofy: Maybe it would be faster to just break it.

Sora: That's brilliant!

(He summons his Keyblade to a shocked Mike, raising it over his head)

Sulley: Hang on!

(He runs over holding Boo)

Sulley: Think I've got a better idea. If we can just short it out, the lock 
will disengage. And, lucky for us, Boo is a walking energy generator.

(Mike ponders)

Mike: That might work!

Sora: You're our MVP, Boo.

(Boo giggles and Sulley places her atop his head. He starts to laugh, 
playfully running around the room, and she screams excitedly. Mike and 
Sora run after them, but soon take a spill. Sora knocks Mike into the 
air with the Keyblade, but loses his grip and falls over. Mike lands 
upright on his knees with a triumphant "Yeehaw" before the Keyblade 
falls on top of him, causing him to see stars. He holds his head while 
everyone laughs, causing the control panel to whirr to life. Boo whimpers 
as multiple Unversed appear in the room)

Mike: Hide her!

Sulley: I'm on it.

(Mike readies his fighting stance as the other three summon their weapons 
once again. They defeat the ones that appeared, but more surround Sulley 
as he guards Boo from her hiding spot. The group performs a scream strike 
on the creatures before Sora uses Mike as a bowling ball again. Soon, the 
battle is over and the control panel is surging with energy, but the doors 
still aren't open)

Mike: It's no use. We need a bigger burst of laughter.

Sulley: Would you care to do the honors?

(Mike aims his fingerguns at Boo)

Mike: I'd love to.

(He waves his hands, getting ready, then smacks himself in the face, 
sending his eyeball in various directions with each smack, mimicking a 
bouncing ball. It bounces faster and faster until he gives a final "Tada!")

Mike: 40 - 0. Game and set!

(Sulley looks down at Boo, but she makes no reaction. Mike sighs)

Mike: I'm not cut out for this racket.

(Still no reaction. He clears his throat)

Mike: Come on. It's a tennis joke.

(Sora looks at Goofy)

Mike: Should I've gone with ping-pong?

Sora (to Goofy): Nothin' could've saved THAT one.

Mike (screaming): Wait! Nobody move!

(The trio react in alarm and Mike falls on all fours)

Mike: I dropped my contact!

(He searches the floor while Sulley scratches his face)

Sulley: I don't think Boo's gonna get it, Mike.

(Mike crosses his arms a Sora walks over to Sulley)

Sora (to Sulley): Do YOU get it?

Sulley (to Sora): Yeah, it's 'cause his eye's so big. The joke is you 
can't lose a contact the size of a dinner plate.

(Boo mimics Mike's arm crossing)

Mike (whirling around): Oh, fine!

(Boo roars)

Donald: Aren't you supposed to be good at this?

Mike: I AM once I'm warmed up.

Goofy: Sora, do the Funny Face Special.

Sora: Huh? Whaaat?

(He scratches his head)

Sora: Ugh, if you insist.

(He crouches to Boo's level and drops his head. After a moment of 
anticipation, he perks up his head with the goofiest smile, causing Boo 
to laugh)

Sora: Everybody join in!

(Sora repeats it and everyone makes a different silly face for Boo. The 
control panel goes wild and the shutter unlocks. Sulley chuckles)

Sulley: Sora's aimin' for your job.

(Mike crosses his arms in a huff. They start to walk toward the door when 
Randall slithers up behind them)

Randall: You boys aren't gonna leave without saying good-bye?

Mike: Give it a rest, Randall. You're not gonna get away with this.

Sulley: We'll stop anything you throw at us.

Sora: Yeah!

(Sora summons his Keyblade)

Randall: Maybe you will. Or then again, maybe you won't. I have still got 
an ace up my sleeve.

(Mike scowls as they stand ready for a fight)

Randall: Now...I command you to destroy them!

(He snaps his finger, but nothing happens. He shifts his eyes and looks 
around)

Randall: Eh?

(He turns away from them and snaps twice again, but again gets no response)

Randall: Hey. Come on!

(He scuffles along the floor to a piece of machinery in the corner)

Randall: Move... Move, you stupid--

(He tries to pull on one of the metal spikes of the machine, but it doesn't 
budge)

Mike: Looks like your ace is a joker.

(Randall groans)

Randall: What a pile of junk!

(He kicks the machine and slithers away, seething)

Sora: Wha-- Hey!

(Sora moves to follow him, but Sulley pulls him back)

Sulley: Just leave him. Don't think he can cause us any more trouble.

(He moves an arm to look down at Boo)

Boo: Kitty!

Sulley: Besides, we gotta focus on getting Boo home.

(He pets her and she giggles)

Sora: You're right.

(He dispels his Keyblade)

Sulley: Boo's door has to be somewhere in the vault. If we head outside and 
go through the power station, we can get to the door vault that way.

(They walk to the shutter and it opens)

Sulley: Follow me!

(As they enter the hallway, the door closes and a figure in a black hood 
enters through a corridor of darkness. The figure holds out a hand to the 
machine and oil pools out of it. Randall peeks out from around the corner 
as the oil builds on the edges of the machine, climbing up the sides and 
into every crevice. An Unversed symbol appears on its metal hood. The 
figure directs the wave of oil and machine in front of him and a large 
mouth bursts from the Unversed, causing Randall to grin. Upon reaching 
the Power Plant, they see that it has been set ablaze by Unversed)

Mike: Oh no...

(A helicopter flies overhead and they hear a voice over the radio)

CDA Agent: Disregard Code 835. 72-16 in progress. We have visual on the 
unidentified life-forms. Suspected cause of the conflagration. Code 72-16, 
over.

Sulley: We gotta get to Boo's door.

Sora: Yeah.

Mike: The whole factory--it's a total mess!

Sulley: I know, Mikey. But right now, we just have to keep moving.

(They make their way through the Power Plant and see the Unversed wreaking 
havoc as the helicopter flies in from above, lowering a rope)

CDA Agent: Ready to descend.

(A four-armed monster in a bright yellow suit containing a large tank 
drops to the ground, followed by other CDA Agents with varying appendages. 
He approaches Sora and company)

CDA Agent: Stand aside. We'll get this fire put out, pronto.

(One of the agents behind him points to his left, giving a direction to 
the other, who is knocked off his feet by an explosion. A Spiked Turtletoad 
marches through from its direction, causing the agents to back away. The 
first agent takes out his radio)

CDA Agent: Code 72-16. Unidentified life-form sighted.

(Sora runs ahead of him and summons his Keyblade)

Sora: These guys are OUR specialty!

(The agent moves to the side as the group begins battling the Unversed. 
After taking out the vicious Spiked Turtletoad, several Flame Core 
Heartless appear)

CDA Agent: We have spotted additional unidentified life-forms.

(They continue defeating Heartless and Unversed while also using Water 
spells on the surrounding fire. Once the enemies are taken out, the group 
helps fight the fires with the giant water hoses brought by the CDA. Soon, 
the threat is neutralized)

Sulley: Thank you! You did great.

(The agent salutes him)

CDA Agent: Yes, sir. We'll be on our way.

Sora: Time to go.

Mike: Yeah.

(The group follow the hallways through the Power Plant, reaching another 
outside area where the helicopter flies past them)

CDA Agent: Requesting backup. We need help containing the fire!

(More of the plant is on fire. Heartless appear to block their way to the 
Tank Yard, where the agents are fighting the fire. The helicopter flies 
over the Tank Yard, shining down its searchlight)

CDA Agent: Deal with those life-forms!

(They fight the Heartless and extinguish the fires)

Mike: This way.

(A boom catches their attention as a large blue tank starts crackling with 
electricity. Sulley grabs Boo and the group runs as quick as they can away 
from the tank. It explodes, knocking them all off their feet. Mike's 
breaths come fast and quick as the pipes above burst into flames and 
explode likewise. Another blow to their right causes another explosion, 
dislodging a gigantic pipe above them from its rivets. They run as it 
starts to fall to the ground, sending up a cloud of dust. The passageway 
they were about to use is now filled with broken piping)

Mike: Oh, great. This time we're really stuck.

(Goofy whimpers)

Sora: Sulley, have you got any ideas?

(Boo hops down from his hand)

Sulley: Just gimme a second.

(Boo runs toward something as Sulley thinks. The other watch her as she 
returns)

Boo: Kitty!

(At their confusion, she points ahead at the fallen pipe and giggles)

Sulley: If I'm right about that pipe...

(He makes a fist)

Sulley: Yep, it's perfect. Boo, thank you!

(He pats her on the head and she giggles again)

Sulley: We gotta follow that pipe.

(He starts walking)

Mike: What?! Wait a sec. I thought we were going straight to the door 
vault. The only place that pipe leads is to the cooling tank!

(Mike, walking beside him, blocks his way)

Mike: You sure you don't have a better idea?

(Sulley picks him up by the head with one hand and sets him down to his left)

Sulley: Don't worry, Mike. Just trust me.

(They climb up the busted pipe and into the cooling tank, defeating the 
Unversed that appear inside it. Sulley rushes to a set of doors)

Boo: Kitty!

(Boo follows behind)

Sulley: I'm pretty sure Maintenance hasn't finished patching it up.

(He releases the door from its hinges and sets it aside, pointing)

Sulley: This way.

(Boo giggles and they run inside. Mike looks at his surroundings)

Mike: Wait a second... It's the door vault!

Sulley (smiling): Yep. What'd I tell ya?

(Mike puts his hands on his hips)

Mike: Sure, nice job, Sull. Seriously, if I didn't know any better...I'd 
say you actually ran the place.

(He gives his friend a sly smile)

Sulley: Thanks, Mikey. All right, it's not much farther.

(They traverse the Vault Passage and enter another hallway. The floor is 
covered in a black substance)

Donald: Hey! What's this black goop?

Goofy: Gawrsh, it looks like some kinda trail.

(They follow the trail of sludge into the Door Vault)

Sulley: Everybody look for Boo's door.

(They hear a snicker as a certain purple fiend slithers in)

Sulley: Randall...

Mike: Didn't you learn your lesson with that pile-of-junk fiasco?

(Randall scoffs)

Randall: Oh, I learned a lot.

(He walks aside, pointing out the very same pile of junk behind him. Its 
existence there startles them, but Mike quickly waves it off and moves 
closer. The Unversed symbol appears on its hood, which scares Boo, who 
hides behind Sulley)

Sulley: Wait, Mike. Something's different!

(Sulley picks up Boo and leads her to safety as Sora, Donald and Goofy 
run up to Mike)

Mike: Oh, please. It's just more junk.

(Randall cackles from a high ledge, distracting Mike from the ooze seeping 
out behind his back. He turns around to see an enormous Lump of Horror 
rising up from the machine. Mike shivers and backs away, Sora and company 
running to his rescue)

Sora: An Unversed!

(Mike lands on his butt as the blobby creature opens its mouth wide, 
scream containers bursting from the goo. Sulley grabs Mike by the head and 
lifts him up)

Sulley: Mike, time to reach down and let the scary out.

(Mike smiles, then smacks his own face, Sulley letting him down to the floor)

Mike: Oh, I'm ready, Sulley. I'm ready!

Randall: Finally... This is exactly what I need to take over the company. 
But first, I am getting rid of YOU.

(He looks down at Mike and Sulley)

Randall: Attack!

(The Lump of Horror plants itself into the floor, spreading itself across 
swipes of ooze where Tar Hands burst from the ground, tossing fireballs at 
the party. They take out the Tar Hands and dodge out of the way as the 
great lump barrels towards them. It sinks into the floor for a moment 
before exploding in a swell of oil, sending it all across the floor and up 
the walls. The main body of the Unversed raises itself up in the center 
of the room, sprouting wings on its jack-o-lantern face, as a hundred Tar 
Hands emerge from the walls and floor. The hands attempt to claw at them 
but are quickly subdued. As Sora approaches the Lump of Horror, it strikes 
with a gust of wind from its great wings, sending him back into the Tar 
Hands clutches. As the group destroy the hands, the Unversed absorbs the 
oil back into its body and emits steam from the canisters of scream 
stuck inside it, also sending a cluster of fireballs in their direction. 
Knocking the fireballs back at it causes the Lump of Horror to lose 
control of its form, dripping oil everywhere. It falls to the floor in 
a silent puddle, leaving a pile of machinery and scream canisters, which 
Randall scuttles over to, whimpering)

Randall (screaming): Whyyy?!

(Randall begins kicking the debris as Mike looks over to a door which was 
previously restored from wood chips. He waves for Sulley's attention and 
quickly does a series of charades to get his point across without speaking. 
Door. Randall. Pointing. Strangle? Obviously, Sulley doesn't understand. 
Mike grunts in frustration, then makes a quiet roar)

Sulley: Ah!

(He gives Mike a double thumbs-up and Mike rolls his eyes in relief, as 
Sulley runs forward)

Donald: Where are you going--

(Goofy grabs Donald to silence him as Randall turns toward Sulley in 
surprise. Sulley bellows loudly in Randall's face. Not long after, they 
show Randall the door. Mike turns the knob and opens it)

Mike: All right, and in ya go.

(Randall grits his teeth and Boo roars at him from Sulley's arms)

Sulley: There's no place for you here anymore, Randall. Now we're in the 
business of making children laugh.

(He looks down at Boo, smiling, and she giggles. Randall scowls back at them)

Randall (yelling): You think it's funny?

(He points with two of his arms and Mike puts a hand on his shoulder)

Mike: Hilarious! The more that you whine, the funnier it gets.

(Mike smiles haughtily and Randall growls in anger, before accepting defeat. 
He pushes Mike away and walks toward the door)

Sulley: Enjoy your extended vacation.

(Randall seethes)

Randall: You clowns are gonna be sorry when I find my way back and I 
finally take over this place!

(Mike follows him to the door and Randall steps inside. Mike overhears)

Trailer Son: Mama, that gator's in the house again!

Trailer Mom: Are you kidding?! Oh, this time, he's in for it. C'mere!

(Mike grins widely as they start beating up Randall from beyond the door)

Randall: Ugh! Oof! Ahhh!

(Mike recoils with a grimace)

Trailer Mom: Get back here!

(Randall screams and Mike chuckles)

Mike: So long! Smell ya later.

(He closes the door with a smile and Sulley walks up to the door)

Sulley: And now we just need to do one last thing.

(He reaches an arm back to smash the door)

Sora: Hang on! I have a way to lock him out.

(Sora walks forward and summons the Keyblade, aiming it at the door. A 
Keyhole appears on the door and the Keyblade glows, sending a beam toward 
the Keyhole. A bright light shines and they hear a clicking sound as the 
Keyhole disappears. A warm glow envelops the locked door and it rises into 
the air, vanishing)

Donald: And that takes care of that.

Goofy: Uh-huh.

(Sora gives a sheepish chuckle. Later, they finally find Boo's door and 
jump up to it, Mike and Sulley hanging from the rails)

Sulley: Okay, Boo. Time to go home. You must be tuckered out, but we'll 
play together real soon.

(The rail buckles and begins to slide the door along, with Sora, Donald and 
Goofy following on their own red door. They each give their own excited 
shouts)

Mike: What NOW?!

(The doors arrive at the Laugh Floor, and the group jump off as they lock 
in their terminals. A hooded figure steps toward them, sending Sora on the 
defensive)

Sora: Who are YOU?

???????: Gotta say, that strange facade had me fooled at first, brother.

(The figure takes off his hood, revealing a dark reflective helmet)

Sora: Wait a sec...

(He gasps)

Sora: Oh yeah! You were at the cathedral! And hey! Who are YOU to call 
anyone strange?

Goofy: Say, do we know this guy?

Donald: Uhhh...

???????: We haven't ever met in the flesh. I am Vanitas.

(Goofy and Donald act in surprise)

Sora: This is the part where you spout some mumbo jumbo and disappear, right?

(Vanitas walks through one of the workstations)

Vanitas: This whole world...was powered by scream. They converted the 
screams of human children into energy.

(He picks up one of the scream canisters)

Vanitas: And this very company was what made it all happen. It's as rich 
a source of negative emotion as we'll ever find.

Mike (angrily): For the last time, we already stopped doing that!

Vanitas: Did you? Then how do you explain all these canisters of surplus 
scream?

(He holds the canister up)

Vanitas: This facility was everything I could hope for. And I was lucky 
enough to find a pawn whose heart was darkened by thoughts of revenge.

(He juggles the canister in the air)

Mike: You mean Randall.

Sulley: All Randall ever cared about was winning. And this guy took 
advantage of that weakness.

Vanitas: My heart is made of just one thing. And the Unversed collected 
enough screams and sadness from those children to reconstruct it.

Mike: Yeah, and the whole time they were trashing our company in the 
process!

(Sulley holds Mike back from rushing at Vanitas, but Mike struggles against 
the grip on his head)

Vanitas: But, even with all this negative emotion, my heart is still 
incomplete. I need something else.

(He drops the canister. It clangs to the ground before screaming off into 
the air)

Sora: Whoa!

(Sulley dodges away, taking Mike and Boo with him. They watch as the 
canister flies around the expansive room, bouncing off the walls until 
it runs out of scream and crashes to the floor. Mike and Sulley scowl 
as it rolls to Sora's feet)

Vanitas: The half of me that sleeps on...inside of your heart.

(Sora turns around and gasps as Vanitas holds his Keyblade just inches 
from him. A voice bursts from Sora's chest)

Sora/Ven: Vanitas!

(Sora is taken aback at his own outburst)

Vanitas: Ventus... What a strange place to slither off to...

(He creeps closer to Sora, holding out his hand)

Vanitas: ...you insignificant speck.

(Sora knocks his hand away)

Sora: What are you talking about?

(Mike, Sulley and Boo sneak carefully through the workstations out of 
sight of Vanitas)

Vanitas: Oh, you wouldn't remember. When you were little...you formed a 
special bond, with a boy named Ventus who joined with your heart.

Donald: Ven!

Goofy: Is he sayin' that one of the missing Keyblade wielders is inside 
Sora's heart?

Sora: How is that possible?

(A dark mist swirls around them)

Vanitas: Now, you will return Ventus to me.

(Vanitas swings his Keyblade, releasing a dark wind and Sora feels a tug on 
his heart. He catches himself upon falling to the floor as Donald and Goofy 
shield him from the front)

Sora: Donald...Goofy...

(Goofy struggles, holding back the dark wind with his shield)

Goofy: The King told us about this. Ventus wasn't able to defeat Vanitas. 
They struck each other down, and then the King said that Ventus's heart 
never returned to him!

Donald: You're not gonna do that to Sora! No way!

(The wind is blasted away)

Vanitas: Stay out of this.

(With a wave of his arm, he swipes Donald and Goofy away in a streak of 
darkness. With Sora left defenseless, they gasp)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(Vanitas walks closer as Sora stands and summons his Keyblade. Vanitas 
knocks it away in seconds with his own and aims it at Sora's chest. The 
image of Ventus is superimposed over Sora)

Vanitas: Join your heart...with mine!

(Vanitas releases another dark wind just as Sulley appears behind him)

Sulley: Made you look!

(He roars ferociously and Boo covers her eyes, while Mike covers her ears. 
Vanitas drops his Keyblade as Sulley grabs and lifts him up. He struggles 
against Sulley's firm grip)

Vanitas: Let me go!

(Another set of doors slide into the room, brought by Mike)

Mike: Over here, Sulley!

(Sulley runs over, tossing Vanitas inside the door)

Sulley: Close it! Quick!

(Mike slams the door and Sulley grabs it as Mike runs to the next terminal 
and opens a second door. Sulley tosses the door inside the second door, 
and the process repeats with a third, and then a fourth door. Finally, the 
fourth door is shredded into sawdust with glee. Sulley and Mike high-five 
and Boo dances)

Sulley: Boo!

Mike: Hey!

(The two then high-five Boo)

Sora: That was awesome!

Donald: Thank you!

Goofy: We owe ya.

Sulley: No, WE should be thanking YOU. We never woulda managed to get Boo 
this far if you hadn't come along to help.

Mike: And finally, we found her door.

(Boo giggles and Sora walks over to her)

Sora: Boo, I know how excited you were to come play with Mike and Sulley. 
Sorry we dragged you into this.

Donald: Watch it! You're gonna scare her with that face!

Sora: Hey, you are WAY scarier.

Goofy: Gawrsh, I think you're both scary.

(The group laughs at Sora and Donald's expense)

Sulley: Okay, Boo. Time to go.

Boo: Kitty...

Mike: We'll catch up soon, kid.

Boo: Mike Wazowski!

(Mike turns, seeing Donald behind him)

Mike: No, that's Donald, Boo.

Boo: Mike Wazowski.

(She runs up to Mike and hugs him. Surprised, he smiles and pets her on 
the head)

Mike: Better. I'll see ya, kid.

(He waves as Sulley leads her to her flowery door)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Boo!

(They reveal a trio of silly faces from under their hands)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: So looong!

(Boo laughs and waves goodbye. Later, the trio returns to the lobby with 
Mike and Sulley)

Sora: Sorry for all the headaches we caused.

Sulley: Don't mention it. And actually, it was kinda nice havin' a little 
adventure for old times' sake.

(Mike nods)

Mike: Yeah, the flying and the falling--and hey, let's not do that paint 
thing again--but nothin' like running for our lives to get the heart pumping!

(Sora chuckles)

Donald: I had a great time.

Sora: Donald! All you did was complain!

Donald: I did not.

Goofy: Any chance that we can drop by again?

Mike: The door's always open.

Sulley: And maybe Boo can join us!

(He extends a hand and Sora takes it)

Sora: Yeah.

(Donald shakes Mike's hand while Sulley and Goofy nod)

Sora: Bye!

(They back off to the entrance, waving)

Donald: Good-byeee!

Mike: For the record, I still get the most laughs!

Sulley: Happy exterminating!

(Sora chuckles and shrugs at Donald and Goofy)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Thank you!

(The group returns to the gummi ship. Sora taps his foot and a finger 
impatiently to the concern of Donald and Goofy. Sora stands up on his 
chair, turning back to them)

Sora: We should go to the realm of darkness!

Donald: No way!

Goofy: You can't go there until you get the power of waking!

Sora: But come on, we have to do something! If we don't act, the 
Organization's gonna win!

(Donald and Goofy exchange worried expressions and Jiminy jumps onto Sora's 
shoulder)

Jiminy: Sora, do you even know how to get to the realm of darkness?

(Sora's realization garners a sigh and he takes out his gummiphone)

Sora: Well, Riku and the King do.

Donald: They won't tell you.

Goofy: Nope, not until you complete your own mission.

(He looks back at them sadly, and slumps, defeated, back into his chair, 
letting out an angsty shout and staring at the ceiling. Suddenly, his 
gummiphone begins to ring)

Sora: Huh?

Donald & Goofy (excited): The King?

Sora (excited): Riku?

(He answers the phone and neither Riku nor the King appear)

Ienzo: Is this a bad time?

(They sigh)

Sora: Ienzo.

(Ienzo pauses at this unorthodox response)

Ienzo: So, I have some news about Ansem's Code and the replica we need 
for Roxas's heart.

(Jiminy hops up again to see the screen)

Jiminy: Oh!

Sora: And...?

Ienzo: First, the replica. Even is still missing, but we found some of 
his research. I'll see what I can learn from it.

Jiminy (bowing): You've got our thanks.

Ienzo: As for Ansem the Wise's data, we've discovered a very interesting 
passage. I'll read you exactly what he wrote. "I have discovered three 
unique hearts inside of Sora's. One is Roxas. The second has been with 
Sora for nearly as long. And a third has resided in Sora's heart for even 
longer--most of his life, in fact. This is a truly astonishing discovery. 
While these hearts have now melded with Sora--grown silent and indistinct--
Sora retains the memories of all three. The memories have been compartment-
alized--each placed in its own 'box,' so to speak. I surmise the hearts 
can be awoken, provided that each of them is returned to the box that 
contains the correct memories. Unite the heart with its memories, and 
provide it a suitable body within which it may flourish, and I believe 
any or all three of these people can be made real again."

Sora: Roxas and TWO MORE?

Jiminy: Who else?

(Sora thinks and Jiminy hops down)

Sora: Oh. Thanks, Ienzo.

Ienzo: Certainly. Take care.

(The call ends)

Donald: Three different hearts...

(Sora puts the phone away)

Goofy: One of them's Roxas. The other one must be Ventus.

Donald: You're gonna believe what Vanitas said?

Goofy: Well, uh...it's kinda all we got to go on.

(They think for a second)

Goofy: Sora, do you know who the third one might be?

Sora (shaking his head): Uh-uh.

Donald (teasing): 'Cause Sora can't count.

Sora: Hey! That's not related.

(They begin to laugh)

Sora: Donald...

(The gummi ship sails on. Meanwhile, on the edge of a dark beach, a young 
woman in blue sits with a cloaked man, his blonde beard just visible 
beneath his hood)

Ansem the Wise: Tell me, will you stay here?

Aqua: I can't shake the feeling that these waters touch another shore 
I've visited.

Ansem the Wise: The Destiny Islands.

Aqua (surprised): You've heard of them?

Ansem the Wise: Yes. They are quite lovely--a far cry from this wasteland.

(She crosses her arms over her legs, staring out at the light far over 
the water)

Aqua: I'm staying. Someone will come for me.

Ansem the Wise: These waters are the in-between of dark and light, its 
shores the margins of day and night. They brought you and I together, so 
why not also you and another?

(She nods)

Aqua: Yes.

(Some time later, Aqua senses an approaching presence)

Aqua (turning back): Who's there?

(Ansem the Wise follows suit, seeing the arrival of his usurper, Ansem, 
Seeker of Darkness)

Ansem the Wise (angrily): You...

(They stand to face him, ready for conflict)

Ansem: Master...I must have a word with you.

(Ansem the Wise doffs his hood, glaring at him through orange eyes)

Ansem the Wise: "Master"? So now you mock me.

(Ansem walks nearer to them)

Ansem: Do you recall those experiments of the heart you bade me cease? 
Among the test subjects was a girl. She had lost her memory, just as I 
had. But...you can reconstruct memories. You did with Sora. I believe you 
have seen the girl's memories.

Ansem the Wise: What is your question?

Ansem: Where did you put the girl?

Ansem the Wise: What girl?

Ansem: Very well. If you won't tell me here...

(He reaches for Ansem the Wise, but Aqua knocks his hand away, standing 
between the two of them)

Aqua: I think you should go.

(Ansem looks Aqua over and raises his eyebrow)

Ansem: A lost guardian of light?

(He scoffs)

Ansem: You wait here...for the King and his fool.

(Ansem crosses his arms with a smile, and the earth shakes as a black 
creature with glowing yellow eyes emerges from the ground behind him. The 
Dark Figure reaches back with its muscular arms and punches Aqua away. She 
lands on her feet on the sand)

Ansem the Wise: Where's your Keyblade?

Aqua: Don't need it!

(She runs forward with a leaping kick to the Dark Figure's bandaged face. 
She jumps off its arm, but it grabs her by the leg before she can get away. 
It lifts her up to look her in the eyes as she struggles. Ansem the Wise 
runs up, waving his arms)

Ansem the Wise: No more! I'll go.

(Ansem chuckles evilly)

Ansem: You are wise.

(Aqua breaks free, spinning downward to land a kick on Ansem, but he blocks 
with his arm. She leaps off the arm and lands back near the water)

Ansem the Wise: Poor thing. I mustn't leave you with nothing.

(Energy begins to swirl between the Dark Figure's hands as a massive orb 
of darkness emerges. At the apex, the orb bursts from the Figure's chest, 
striking Aqua at high speed, sending her screaming into the murky waters. 
Ansem the Wise rushes to the water and falls to his knees helplessly. Aqua 
sinks deep into the water, darkness spreading over her heart)

Aqua: What...is this feeling?

(The darkness envelops her body as she drifts deeper into the abyss. 
Meanwhile on the Gummi Ship, Sora's phone rings. Sora answers it, seeing 
Dale on the screen)

Dale: Hiya, Sora.

Sora: Hey, Dale. What's up?

Dale: Chip just got a message from Merlin.

(He yells off-screen)

Dale: Chip! I got him!

(No response)

Dale (waving): Hey, Chipper!

(Chip hops onto the screen)

Chip: Hi, Sora!

Sora: Hi, Chip. Does Merlin need us for something?

Chip: Yep, I think it's got something to do with some kind of book. He 
said he'll have a cup of tea while he waits for ya.

Dale: A cup of tea where?

Chip: Oh no! He said tea, but he didn't say where.

Dale: Do you mean he left before you could find out?

Chip: He's a tough wizard to pin down.

(Chip crosses his arms while Dale sighs)

Chip: Anyway, message delivered. Bye!

(Dale waves and the call ends)

Sora: Where could he be having tea?

Donald: I don't know.

(They pause for a moment to think)

Goofy: Say, if you were gonna have a cup of tea, wouldn't you wanna have 
it at the best restaurant you could find?

Sora: Ohh... Of course!

Donald: Little Chef's bistro.

Goofy: Yeah! Let's go drop by Twilight Town, and we can see if Merlin's 
there.

(The Gummi Ship takes off toward Twilight Town. They enter the Tram 
Common, where Merlin is sipping tea at Le Grand Bistrot, his large carpet 
bag at his feet)

Merlin: Ah, greetings, gentlemen. What brings you all the way out here? 
Besides the finest tea this side of Big Ben, of course.

(He chuckles)

Sora: Huh? But...Merlin, I thought that you asked us to stop by.

Merlin: Gracious, did I?

Sora (nodding): Mm-hmm.

Goofy: Didn't ya leave a message for us with Chip and Dale?

Donald: About a book?

(The wizard raises a finger)

Merlin: Ah! Yes, the book. That's right.

(He taps his wand against the carpet bag and it opens. Out floats a 
familiar children's book labeled "Winnie the Pooh")

Merlin: Behold.

(Sora grabs onto the book)

Sora: Hey, this is...

(They inspect the cover. The titular bear sitting alone on a log beneath 
the stars)

Donald: Sora's not on it.

Goofy: Did somethin' happen?

Merlin: Well, that's what you need to find out, lad.

(Sora contemplates before handing Donald the book)

Sora: Okay, I'll see you in a bit.

(Sora aims his Keyblade at the book)

Goofy: Take care.

Merlin: Yes, and good luck.

(The blade glows and with a flash, Sora becomes particles of light that 
fly into the storybook. In the familiar landscape of Rabbit's Howse, 
Winnie the Pooh sits near the front door with his best friend Piglet, 
a paw to his temple)

Pooh: Oh, bother. Think, think, think... Think, think, think...

Sora: Pooh Bear!

(Piglet looks over as Sora enters)

Sora: You okay?

Pooh: Oh! Hello there, Sora.

(Pooh giggles and stands up)

Pooh: You're home.

Sora: Uh...huh? Good to see you, Pooh. And you, too, Piglet.

Piglet (cheerfully): Hello.

Sora: You're not in trouble? But I thought something odd must be going on.

Pooh: Hmm, let me see... I don't remember anything oddish, but perhaps 
I've forgotten. Think, think, think...

Rabbit: Oh, we've got trouble all right!

Pooh: Think, think, think... Oh, bother.

(Rabbit walks up)

Piglet: Would that be the Rabbit sort of trouble?

(Rabbit crosses his arms and glares at Piglet)

Piglet (shaking): S-s-s-sorry, please continue.

(Sora chuckles)

Roo: Sora!

(Sora looks over and sees a large lavender elephant walking towards 
them, with Roo aboard its back)

Sora: Wow! Who's this?

(Roo leaps over his head and slides down his trunk)

Roo: It's okay. He's my friend.

(Sora approaches and leans down)

Sora: Hi, I'm Sora.

Lumpy: And I'm Lumpy! It's nice to meet you!

(The Heffalump stomps the ground happily and Gopher bursts from the soil)

Gopher: Sufferin' sassafras! Stomp around a little louder, why don't ya?

Lumpy: Oh! Gopher, I'm sorry.

Piglet: I kind of like it when the ground gets bouncy.

(Gopher turns toward Piglet)

Gopher: Well, I suppose if something has to bounce...

(He turns to look behind Sora)

Gopher: Speaking of...

(A bounce. Then another bounce. Then another, and another, until...)

Sora: Hmm?

(Sora turns around and gets tackled by the one and only Tigger)

Tigger: Back for some more bouncin', Sora?

(Sora smiles wide)

Sora: Tigger!

Tigger: C'mon, let's go! You too, Roo!

(He bounces on his striped tail and Roo follows)

Roo: Yippee!

(Roo starts laughing)

Lumpy: Me too! Me too! I wanna bounce!

(Lumpy and Roo bounce around in circles as Piglet and Gopher feel the 
effects on the ground)

Pooh: Think, think, think...

Tigger: Oh yes, it is time for bouncin'! Say no more! All would-be 
bouncers are welcome.

Pooh: Oh, I remember now. Rabbit's trouble is harvest related.

Rabbit: Well, thank YOU for remembering my plight, Pooh. Better late than 
never.

(He addresses the bouncing buddies)

Rabbit: EXCUSE ME!

(They ignore Rabbit and keep bouncing)

Rabbit: Would anyone else care to remember why we're here?

(Rabbit walks toward them and they stop to think)

Pooh: As I recall, we came to help you with your garden, Rabbit. After 
which, perhaps, you'll invite us in for a smackeral or two of honey?

Rabbit: Correct.

(He shakes his head, whirling around)

Rabbit: No. No! I mean, we'll see about that, Pooh. Now, the garden, if 
you please?

(Sora walks over)

Rabbit: You can help, too, Sora.

Sora: What? Me too?

(Together, they help Rabbit pick vegetables. A delighted Rabbit holds a 
bounty of bright orange carrots in his arms)

Rabbit: What a harvest!

Piglet: Thanks to Sora's help.

(Rabbit puts down the carrots)

Rabbit: Yes, quite right. Thank you, Sora!

(Tigger's back at it)

Tigger: Well, how's about a little more bouncin'?

Rabbit: Oh no, no no no! There's no bouncing in farmwork!

Roo: Aww, no bouncin' at all?

Tigger: Huh?

Lumpy: I want to bounce.

Gopher (holding his head): Whippersnappers and their bouncing...

(Piglet giggles)

Pooh: Excuse me, Rabbit. The carrots are very nice, but might you have 
some honey to go with them?

Rabbit: Now's not the time, Pooh. If I give you any honey here, I'll just 
end up with a bear stuck in my front door, AGAIN.

Sora (looking around): Well, looks like your problem's solved. Guess I'll 
be on my way.

(He starts to leave)

Rabbit: Solved? Oh, it's far from solved. We still need to harvest the fruit!

(Sora sighs softly)

Pooh: Won't you stay, Sora, for the sake of honey?

Sora: Uh...okay!

(Sora helps the group pick fruit in the orchard. Rabbit surveys the giant 
pile of colorful fruit)

Rabbit: Yes! Yes! Look at all this marvelous fruit!

Lumpy: Oh, it's lovely.

Roo: Lumpy loves, loves, LOVES fruit.

(Roo giggles)

Pooh: You know, Rabbit, I find that fruit always tastes better with a 
little honey.

Piglet: You're right, Pooh. It certainly does.

Tigger (bouncing): Hoo-hoo! Then, I'll keep lookin' for fruit up at 
bouncin' height!

Gopher: And I'll search closer to the soil.

(Gopher descends into his hole)

Rabbit: Sora...

(Sora bends down and Rabbit whispers in his ear)

Rabbit: ...could you help me with my flower patch? I've got a surprise for 
Pooh.

Sora (quietly): A surprise, for Pooh Bear?

Pooh: Yes, Sora?

Sora: Ohh. It's nothing, Pooh.

(Sora helps Rabbit pick flowers, unearthing the stash of honey he keeps 
there. Afterward, Rabbit presents Pooh with a hunny pot)

Rabbit: Here, Pooh. A pot full of honey. It's your reward for being such a 
big help. Eat all you want.

Pooh: Oh, thank you. Rabbit!

(Pooh sits right then and there for a snack)

Piglet: You planted all these flowers just for Pooh?

Roo: Really? Why?

Gopher: It's simple, sonny. Flowers mean nectar. Nectar means honeybees. And 
honeybees...mean honey.

Lumpy: Oh, and the flowers are so lovely. I like the pretty colors.

(They look over just as a breeze wafts along, sending various flower petals 
into the air. Tigger bounces up to touch them)

Tigger: Look at 'em all. They're bouncin' even higher than me!

(They marvel at the sight)

Pooh: Sora, I believe the one I should thank for all that yummy, delicious 
honey is you.

(Sora squats to Pooh's level)

Sora: Don't mention it, Pooh. Besides, we all helped.

Pooh: Um, Sora?

Sora: Hm?

(Pooh points to his chest)

Pooh: You used to be right here. Why is it that you went away?

Sora: Away? Oh, THAT's what you meant by "you're home."

Pooh: Yes. You see, when I get a rumbly in my tumbly, it's very hard to 
think of anything but honey. So I was worried that I might have forgotten 
you away.

Sora: Silly bear, I'd never.

Pooh: Oh, good, because I want us to be together forever.

Sora: Pooh. We are together. There isn't a second that we're not. (thinking 
to himself) Except I can feel it. Our connection's weaker... Why is that?

Pooh: What's wrong, Sora?

(Sora snaps out of his daze)

Sora: Oh, it's nothing. What matters is I'll be here from now on.

(He points to Pooh's heart and the bear smiles happily)

Sora: No going away.

Pooh: Thank you, Sora.

(They laugh cheerfully, watching the petals dance through the air. The 
storybook closes and Sora has joined Winnie the Pooh on the log, now under 
a bright blue sky. Sora appears back in Twilight Town)

Merlin: Splendid. All is as it should be.

Goofy: But how come Sora's picture disappeared in the first place?

(Sora peers downward sadly)

Donald: Sora?

Sora: Something's happened to me that made me vanish from Pooh's heart.

(He turns to the wizard)

Sora: Merlin, I don't ever want to lose my friends.

Merlin: Well, now.

Sora: Huh?

Merlin: There's no need to fret, lad. Whatever's lost can be found again. 
There are always new paths between hearts for us to discover and traverse. 
But you already know that.

(He shows Sora the changed book cover, bringing a smile to his face)

Sora: Yeah!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy leave Twilight Town and sail the Gummi Ship to a 
kingdom covered in snow and ice. Upon their arrival, they are attacked by 
a group of Soldier Heartless. Goofy knocks one back with his shield and 
Donald sends out a Fire spell, destroying two of them. Sora takes out the 
remaining one with his Keyblade. He feels the wind blow through his hooded 
shirt, garnering a shiver)

Sora: It's cold! Donald, gimme a coat!

(He tucks his arms in, freezing and Donald gives him a stern look)

Donald: The magic doesn't work that way.

Goofy: Guess he's too used to the beach!

Sora: Hey, islander, what can I say?

(He rubs his shoulders and looks over to his right at the fjord...)

Sora (pointing): Look! Even the sea's turning to...ice...

(...which is slowly freezing over)

Sora: Donald, this isn't YOUR magic, is it?

Donald (shaking his head): Uh-uh.

Goofy: Do ya think it's the Heartless?

Sora: Might be. Let's go.

(They run forward to the edge of the fjord, watching the ice creep over 
the rippling water)

Sora: Wow!

(Something catches his attention. A young woman with a blue dress and 
purple cape runs along the top of the water, freezing the surface in her 
wake. The expression on her face is one of desperation. They react with 
a start once the ice reaches the shore)

Sora: That girl... She looked so sad. I wonder what happened. Maybe the 
Heartless? We should talk to her.

(Donald and Goofy nod and they run toward the base of the North Mountain. 
They near a cliffside and see snow fall from it, soon followed by a horde 
of reindeer-like Winterhorn Heartless. They take out the Heartless and 
continue up the mountain. They reach the end of the Treescape with a sheer 
cliff)

Donald: Oh... A dead end.

Goofy: Naw, Sora can run up this.

Sora: Yeah, no problem.

(They continue climbing the mountain, reaching an open spot in the Gorge 
where you can see over the kingdom)

Goofy: Gawrsh, look how high up we are!

Donald: Do I have to? What if we fall?

(They finally catch up to the young woman, who walks slowly across the snow)

Sora: Hey, hold up!

(She gasps, turning around quickly, fear emblazoned on her face)

????: Why are you here? Where did you come from?

Sora: Hi. I'm Sora, and I--

(He looks over at Donald, who gives him a forbidding look)

Sora: Uh...I'm from...let's just say someplace...a little warmer.

(Donald approves of this response)

Donald: I'm Donald.

Goofy: And I'm Goofy.

????: Are you visiting Arendelle? For the coronation?

Sora: Huh? Um... uh...

(He looks to Donald and Goofy for an answer. They both nod)

Sora: You got us!

(Sora laughs nervously and Goofy waves)

Sora: So, what's your name?

????: Elsa... Queen Elsa of Arendelle.

(They appear surprised)

Sora: What? The queen?!

(They stand at attention)

Elsa: You shouldn't be out here. Please go back to the village.

(She turns away from them and begins walking)

Sora: Why? Your Majesty, you look like you could use a friend. Don't you 
want to talk?

(She grapples with the anguish on her face)

Elsa (respectfully): Please leave. I need to be alone. I don't want to 
hurt anyone.

(At a certain distance, she stops)

Sora: Oh... Is it that bad? You must've been through a lot.

Donald: We know what that's like, don't we?
Goofy: Sure, adventuring's fun, but it definitely has its ups and downs. 
When the going gets tough, us friends have to stick together!

Sora: Exactly! Although, Donald, you DO lose your temper a lot, so...I can 
relate to wanting some alone time.

Donald: What? I don't do that!

Elsa: Enough!

(Frustrated, Elsa whirls around, her hand glowing as a multitude of spikes 
emerge from the ground between them. Terror returns to her face at this 
outburst, her second of this unfortunate night)

Sora: Elsa... Did you...

(Heartless appear behind her and she gasps)

Goofy: The Heartless!

(She backs away from them as Sora rushes forward with his Keyblade)

Sora: Don't worry. We got 'em. Take cover!

(She runs safely back as they take on the horde of snow-faring Heartless. 
As Sora deals the final blow to the Rock Troll, Elsa approaches them)

Sora: Elsa, are you okay?

Elsa: I...I'm sorry I was so upset. Thank you for your help.

(A Winterhorn Heartless drops down from above and leaps at the group)

Elsa: Look out!

(Elsa holds up her hands, shooting a beam of ice at the Heartless, taking 
it out)

Sora: That's amazing. You can control ice.

(She holds her one bare hand with her blue-gloved hand)

Elsa: Control it? No, all I ever do...is hurt people.

Goofy: It's okay. Those were just the Heartless.

Elsa: You said that word before. What are they?

Sora: Monsters that are after people's hearts. Wherever they go, there's 
trouble.

Elsa: They're after people's hearts?

Sora: Yes, they're dangerous! You should head home before it gets any worse.

Elsa: This is my home now. I can't go back.

(She looks down at her hand)

Elsa: I don't want to hurt anyone.

Sora: What?

Elsa: Arendelle is safer with me staying up here.

(She walks away from them)

Sora: Not safer for you!

(He tries to follow her but a large ice wall appears to block him. Elsa 
looks back at the wall and then breaks into a run)

Elsa: Please, go away!

(Sora places his hands against the wall of ice)

Sora: Elsa...

Goofy: Aw, don't worry, she'll be okay. Seems like she's pretty strong.

Donald: You gotta let her go. She wants to be alone.

Sora: Yeah, I hear you...but I just wanted to know why she was so sad.

???????: And how is it any of your business? Read the room, kiddo.

(They turn around to see a woman in a black coat with blonde hair and 
yellow eyes)

Sora: Who are you? That's...the Organization coat. You new?

(She raises an eyebrow in annoyance)

???????: Excuse me? Oh yeah, you forgot. The name's Larxene. This time, 
remember. And we'll take care of Elsa, so don't you worry.

(He looks her over and turns to Donald)

Sora: Do you--

Donald: Nope.

Goofy: Well, she seems to think she knows us, so maybe we should play along.

Sora: Not unless her name's "Terra."

Larxene: Excuse me! I'm right here?

(They turn their attention back to Larxene)

Sora: Why are you after Elsa?

Larxene: No one's gonna hurt her? But we're not about to put up with YOUR 
meddling. Stay here and behave yourselves.

(She holds out her hand, electricity crackling as a set of ice crystals 
float around her fingers. She sends out a bolt of lightning at the ice wall, 
which shatters. She raises her arm. The remnants of the ice wall, glowing 
blue from the lightning coursing through it, start to rise into the air, 
spinning into a vortex of frozen electricity. The whirlwind stops, and 
boulders of ice shoot into the ground around the trio)

Sora: Wait. The ice!

Goofy: It's going to wall us in!

Larxene: Ice is so not my style.

Sora: Larxene!

(He runs towards her, but is stopped by a final boulder on the pile of 
frozen blocks. Inside, they inspect their surroundings)

Goofy: Anybody see a way out?

Donald: No, not me.

Sora: Well, we can't stay in here.

Goofy: Elsa's in REAL trouble now.

Sora: Yeah. Larxene promised not to hurt her, but I trust those guys as 
far as I can throw 'em.

Donald (nodding): They've gotta be up to no good!

Sora: Clearly!

(They begin to explore the Labyrinth of Ice)

Donald: Start looking.

Goofy: Yeah, we'll freeze if we don't find a way out.

(They traverse the unsettling landscape, fighting both Heartless and 
Nobodies alike, discovering a room with a peculiar pillar)

Donald: There's something funny about that pillar.

(Sora spins around the pillar and the room starts to shift)

Donald: It's moving!

(The room spins, opening a passageway)

Goofy: Hey, look! We can get through now!

(They reach the Lower Tier of the labyrinth and find another room with 
pillars)

Donald: More pillars!

Goofy: That spin trick you did should work again.

(Sora rotates the pillars, causing the shelf above to slide over, revealing 
a new passageway leading to a vertical shaft)

Donald: Sora, you can climb this!

Goofy: There might be something up there.

(Sora ascends the shaft and reaches the other side of the Middle Tier. 
They continue through the Labyrinth of Ice eliminating Heartless and 
Nobodies and rotating pillars to unbar the way. The final pillar unlocks 
an elevator that takes them to the Upper Tier, revealing the shape of the 
maze to be a snowflake)

Sora: Well, that seemed to lock everything into place.

Donald: That better be the end of it.

(They reach the center of the maze, where a portal sits in waiting)

Goofy: This must be the exit.

Donald: About time.

(They rush through the portal back out to the Gorge and look around for Elsa)

Sora: See her?

Goofy: I think she mighta gone up in that direction.

(He points further up the mountain)

Donald: Yep.

Sora: Okay, c'mon!

(They reach another cliffside)

Donald: More CLIMBING?

Goofy: Yep. And tough climbing, too.

Sora: We can do it. C'mon!

(They ascend to the Mountain Ridge, where a strong icy wind pelts them 
with snow)

Elsa (singing): The snow glows white on the mountain tonight, not a 
footprint to be seen. A kingdom of isolation, and it looks like I'm the 
queen. The wind is howling like this swirling storm inside. Couldn't keep 
it in, heaven knows I've tried. 

(They stop, hearing a voice)

Sora: What?

Elsa (singing): Don't let them in. Don't let them see.

Sora: That's Elsa's voice!

(They start running up the mountain)

Elsa (singing): Be the good girl you always have to be. Conceal, don't 
feel. Don't let them know. Well, now they know.

(Atop the mountain, Elsa releases her glove)

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go!

(She conjures snowflakes from her fingers)

Elsa (singing): Can't hold it back anymore.

(With a spiral of wind, she creates a snowman)

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go! Turn away and slam the door.

(She sends up sparks of magical ice that fall down like rain at her command)

Elsa (singing): I don't care what they're going to say. Let the storm 
rage on.

(She grabs the clasp on her cape...)

Elsa (singing): The cold never bothered me anyway.

(...and lets it fly. It passes over the three of them)

Sora: This way!

(Sora runs ahead, and they follow)

Elsa (singing): It's funny how some distance makes everything seem small.

(She looks out over the mountain)

Elsa (singing): And the fears that once controlled me can't get to me at all.

(She started running up the mountain, elated)

Elsa (singing): It's time to see what I can do, to test the limits and 
break through.

(She pushes her hands forward, creating a jagged set of stairs)

Elsa (singing): No right, no wrong, no rules for me. I'm free!

(She takes one step on the stairs, turning the jagged ice crystals into 
a surface smooth as glass)

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go!

(She runs up the staircase, extending it as she goes, just as Sora and 
company catch up)

Elsa (singing): I am one with the wind and sky.

Sora: Look at that!

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go!

(She reaches the top with a flurry of magic)

Elsa (singing): You'll never see me cry.

(She rushes forward and slams her shoe into the ground, creating a large 
snowflake-shaped platform)

Elsa (singing): Here I stand and here I'll stay.

(The dendrites grow freely, creating a continuously intricate snowflake)

Elsa (singing): Let the storm rage on.

(She bites her lip, raising her arms, lifting the platform with pillars 
of ice, creating large towers against the mountainside. Sora, Donald and 
Goofy stare in amazement)

Elsa (singing): My power flurries through the air into the ground.

(She adds decoration to the walls and floor)

Elsa (singing): My soul is spiraling in frozen fractals all around.

(The magic traces up the walls, adding detail to the archways, reaching 
up to form a ceiling)

Elsa (singing): And one thought crystallizes like an icy blast.

(A chandelier bursts from the ceiling, growing down like a multi-pointed 
stalactite)

Elsa (singing): I'm never going back. The past is in the past.

(She removes her crown and tosses it away)

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go!

(She unties her hair, letting her long braid trail down over her shoulder)

Elsa (singing): And I'll rise like the break of dawn.

(Magic trails along her dress)

Elsa (singing): Let it go! Let it go!

(Her dress changes to a sparkling gown of light blue with a long train)

Elsa (singing): That perfect girl is gone.

(Her reflection shining on the smooth floor, she walks forward confidently)

Elsa (singing): Here I stand in the light of day.

(She walks out onto the balcony as the sun rises into a pink sky, glittering 
every tiny facet of her gown)

Elsa (singing): Let the storm rage on!

(She raises her arms, finally free)

Elsa (singing): The cold never bothered me anyway.

(She spins around, whipping the train in front of her as the doors slam 
behind. Sora, Donald and Goofy stand at the base of her Ice Palace)

Sora: Wow. I don't know what we just saw but...wow. That...was Elsa?

Donald: She looked different.

Goofy: And a lot happier, too.

Sora: Let's say hi.

(They walk closer and a corridor of darkness appears, revealing Larxene's 
smirking face)

Larxene: PLEASE don't tell me that you're spying on her now.

Sora: Larxene!

(The react defensively, but quickly Sora relaxes)

Sora: Don't turn this around on us. YOU'RE following her.

Larxene: Ooh. Look at YOU get all sassy. Okay, I'll admit Elsa is a person 
of interest to us. Maybe she's one of the seven pure lights we need--the 
New Seven Hearts. Gotta make sure though. Fortunately, we're in the best 
position to tell. Can't pick out that "special glimmer"...unless you're 
standing in the shadows.

(She looks up at the palace)

Larxene: And maybe...Elsa DOESN'T have it. I mean, just look how icy her 
palace is--made of magic she forced herself to keep hidden until now. What 
if it's dark magic?

Sora: Elsa would never rely on the darkness!

Larxene: Actually, it's still too early to call. Depends on how SHE sees 
it. If she believes her magic is darkness, that's what it will become. 
Accepting her power, whatever it is, is the only way she can set her heart 
free. So what will Elsa accept? Light or darkness? I know I wanna know!

(She smiles snidely)

Sora: Well, good for you, but guess what? I won't let her fall to darkness!

Larxene: It's her choice to make, not yours. You know, I'm starting to 
understand why she gave you the cold shoulder.

(She combines ice and lightning again to create a blasting wind. Electricity 
crackles along the ground as they struggle against it)

Sora: Larxene!

Larxene: You wanna help her? Then stop trying to be her hero! Let her figure 
things out her own way!

(Bolts of lightning burst from her fingertips, forcing the three of them to 
lose their grip on the snow and fly off down the mountain. Recovering from 
the fall, Sora gets to his knees seeing Donald and Goofy buried in the snow)

Sora: Donald! Goofy! Are you okay?

(Donald stands on his feet, pulling against the heavy pile of snow covering 
his head. He breaks out of the snow, bouncing back from an overabundance of 
force, a light dusting of snow on his hat and bill. He shakes himself off, 
his eyes wobbling from dizziness)

Donald: Phew. I'm okay...

(Goofy signals with his arms from beneath the snow)

Goofy: All good!

(They fish Goofy out of the ground)

Sora: I think we should probably go check on Elsa.

Goofy: And make sure Larxene was wrong about her magic.

Sora: Yeah.

Donald: But don't you tell her what Larxene said.

(He wags a finger at Sora)

Sora: Huh? Why not?

Goofy: Well, to keep the order.

Donald: Yeah. Order.

Sora: Oh... Okay.

(They start to walk, when Goofy's ear perks up)

Goofy: Wait, fellas. Do ya hear that?

(They stop and listen)

Donald: Look!

(An enormous avalanche tumbles down the mountain toward them, encasing tree 
and rock alike)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Avalaaaaaanche!

(Goofy summons his shield)

Goofy: Quick, climb aboard!

Sora: Right!

(Donald and Sora jump aboard the shield and Goofy gets it going, just as 
the snow reaches them)

Goofy: Here we go!

(Goofy jumps on and they start careening down the mountain. From within the 
avalanche, three Frost Serpent Heartless appear. Their wings spin 
effortlessly through the snow as they leer their prey with glowing yellow 
eyes)

Goofy: It's closin' in!

Sora: I got this!

(One of the Frost Serpents swims through the snow after them as another 
takes off into the air)

Goofy: Incoming! Watch out!

(The flying Heartless aims an ice beam at them, but they jump to dodge the 
attack)

Donald: Dodge it!

(Soon all three Frost Serpents fly in the air, shooting identical beams)

Donald: It's right behind us!

(The blasting wind brings a chill over Sora as they eventually careen over 
the mountain edge, spilling from the shield. Further down, the shield 
lands on the snow and they lose their pursuers. Donald and Goofy land back 
on the shield, sledding down the mountain as Sora flips over in the air 
and joins them. Reaching the Snowfield, the three Frost Serpents burst from 
the ground as the shield comes to a stop)

Sora: Look who's back!

(After a tricky battle against air and ice, Sora, Donald and Goofy emerge 
victorious)

Donald: Phew...

(A shadow passes over them, catching their attention. They look skyward, 
seeing more Frost Serpents fly into the snow of the mountain, causing a 
second avalanche. The trio attempts to escape, but the snow overtakes them 
too quickly spilling them over the edge. Later, they hear a voice in their 
unconscious stupor)

????: Wow! Look at all the pretty colors. There's blue, and green--ooh, I 
love green! And look, black.

(Sora feels a tug)

????: Just like my buttons. Hmm?

(Sora wakes up with a snowball stuck in his spiky hair. In his woozy state, 
he thinks he sees a talking, walking snowman. Well, less walking, more 
hopping. The snowman hops over to Sora, just inches from his face)

????: Silly spiky grass. Give me back my foot.

(He pulls the snowball from Sora's hair and reattaches it to his body with 
his twig-like arms. He waddles off between the trees)

Sora: Was that...a snowman?

(Sora stands up slowly, the snow falling from his jacket. He looks ahead, 
but sees no one)

Sora: Huh? Uh...did you see that snowman?

(Donald and Goofy recover from the endeavor)

Goofy: Snowman?

Sora: Yeah. And here's the funny thing: he was walking and talking.

(Donald and Goofy exchange glances)

Donald: Everybody knows snowmen can't walk. You must've imagined it.

Sora: Huh... I thought he was real.

Goofy: Well, maybe we'll see him again. But if we don't get goin', we'll 
never reach Elsa's palace.

Sora: Oh, right! I almost forgot! C'mon!

(They enter the Valley of Ice, surrounded by trees with large frozen 
droplets lining their branches. Soon, they see two people walking with a 
reindeer and a...)

???? (giggling): I can't wait to meet Elsa. I bet she's the nicest, 
warmest, best person ever.

(...snowman!)

Donald: Wow!

Sora: See? I told you! A walking, talking snowman.

(Sora laughs)

Goofy: Well, whaddaya know? You were right!

Sora: I wanna look!

(Sora runs up to the snowman)

Sora: Wow! You really ARE alive! What's making you walk?

(He reaches out to touch the snowman, but he inches backwards. The 
commotion causes the other three strangers to turn around)

????: Um, well, I guess...my feet.

(The three walk over to them and the girl speaks up)

????: Hello. Olaf, are these your friends?

Olaf: Nope! Never met 'em. Don't know anyone blue, green, or who's 
oddly spiky.

Sora: "Spiky"? My hair?

(Olaf giggles)

Sora: Wait, why don't I get a color too? My name is Sora.

Donald: And I'm Donald Duck!

Olaf: Oh.

Goofy: And I'd be Goofy the Green!

????: I'm Anna.

(She addresses the man as he gives her a skeptical look)

Anna: And I know they're strangers, but...they seem pretty nice to me.

(The man sighs)

????????: I'm Kristoff, and this is Sven.

(He motions toward the reindeer who nods)

Goofy: Nice to meet ya.

Sora: So, where are you guys all headed?

Kristoff: We're going to try and put an end to this crazy winter.

Anna: And to do that, we need to find my sister, Elsa.

Sora: Elsa's...your sister?

Goofy: What a coincidence. We're going to see her too.

(She gasps)

Anna: You know Elsa?

Sora: Yeah, we ran into her up the mountain. Um... Do you mind telling 
us what's going on around here? We're worried. We think your sister might 
be in some trouble.

Anna: Trouble? Are you sure?

(She looks into his eyes)

Anna: All right. I know we just met, but...Sora, was it? I get the 
feeling that you're someone to trust.

Kristoff: I'm right there with ya.

Anna: I just hope you like long stories.

Sora: Sure.

Kristoff: Ya know, I should go find some moss for Sven. He's looking a 
little hungry. C'mon, Sven.

(Kristoff and Sven start to leave)

Olaf: Hey, w-w-w-wait, what's going on? Tell me. Is something happening?

(Kristoff bends down to pick up the snowman)

Kristoff: C'mon, Olaf. You're with me.

Olaf: Sure, Sven. Reindeer Sven too?

Kristoff: The reindeer IS Sven.

Olaf: Oh, how fun!

(Olaf giggles as they leave. Anna and Sora sit on a nearby rock)

Anna: When we were little, my sister and I used to be really close.

(Over a decade ago in Arendelle, Anna skips through the halls of the 
palace as Elsa enters her bedroom door. Anna tries to get to her but 
Elsa closes the door)

Anna: But then, one day, for some reason, Elsa just shut me out.

(Later that same year, Anna notices the snow falling outside the window 
and rushes to Elsa's closed door, knocking)

Young Anna (singing): Do you wanna build a snowman? Come on, let's go 
and play. I never see you anymore. Come out the door. It's like you've 
gone away.

Anna: Years passed and we barely ever saw each other. Then, finally, it 
was time for her coronation.

Young Anna (singing): We used to be best buddies and now we're not. I wish 
you would tell me why.

Anna: Let's just say I was more than a little excited. I thought we'd 
finally have a chance to talk.

(Young Anna peers through the keyhole of Elsa's door, then sings into it)

Young Anna (singing): Do you wanna build a snowman? It doesn't have to be 
a snowman.

Anna: But at the party, I did something that made her mad. We got into an 
argument, and I lost my temper.

Young Elsa: Go away, Anna.

Anna: I was just so frustrated!

Young Anna (singing): Okay, bye...

(Young Anna sadly leaves)

Anna: And then, well...that's when she used her magic to push me away. It 
was all my fault.

(The flashback ends)

Anna (singing): Please, I know you're in there. People are asking where 
you've been. They say, "have courage" and I'm trying to. I'm right out 
here for you. Just let me in. We only have each other. It's just you and 
me. What are we gonna do? Do you wanna build a snowman?

(She stops, sadly)

Anna: I shouldn't have upset her the way I did. Elsa ran away because she 
was frightened. I have to bring her home.

Sora: I'm sure she knows how much you love her.

(He remembers the look on Elsa's face when she was fleeing across the fjord)

Sora (thinking) : And I think...maybe that's why she looked so sad.

(He remembers Riku's sacrifice at the door to darkness and his journey after 
Sora woke from his year-long sleep)

Sora (thinking): It's just like when Riku disappeared. He thought he had 
to push me away, to protect me. Maybe Elsa's the same. (to Anna) If anyone 
can help her, it's you.

Anna: Huh?

(He smiles at her)

Anna: Thanks.

Kristoff: Hey, guys! I need some help!

(Kristoff runs toward them)

Sora: What's the problem?

Kristoff: This.

(He holds up a stick)

Donald: A stick problem?

Kristoff: It's not a stick. Well, it IS a stick, but it--

(He bends it and it straightens back up)

Kristoff: It's Olaf's arm. (sigh) He's fallen apart again.

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Fallen apart?!

Donald: Uh, how come you're not upset?

Anna: Oh, it's no big deal. He's a snowman. We'll just...put him back 
together.

Sora: Really?!

Donald: You can do that?

Goofy: I gotta see this! A-hyuck!

Kristoff: The pieces can't be too far from here. Could you guys help us 
look for 'em?

Sora: 'Course!

(They start to search for Olaf)

Goofy: It is kinda hard to spot him in all this snow.

Donald: Everything looks like Olaf.

Goofy: He can't have gone TOO far.

Olaf: Heeey! I'm over this way!

Sora: Huh?

Donald: I heard it too.

Goofy: Yep, that's Olaf's voice.

Olaf: Would I call this cozy or snug? Mmm, I'm gonna go with snug.

(Sora finds an oversized snowball)

Olaf: I can hear you! You're getting closer!

Donald: His voice is getting louder.

(Sora jumps aboard the snowball, riding along until it crashes into a rock 
and bursts open, revealing Olaf's head)

Olaf: Hi, Sora!

Sora: Hey, Olaf. There you are!

Olaf: I was starting to think nobody'd ever come along and find me.

(Sora picks up Olaf's head)

Sora: Well, I'm glad we did.

(They continue searching for the rest of Olaf)

Sora: Are these trees made of ice?

Goofy: Maybe. Look at the little snow-blossoms growing on 'em.

(They find a frozen waterfall)

Goofy: Why don't we look up above the waterfall?

(They climb the water fall and find an oddly-shaped snowball with a 
black rock in it)

Sora: This...MIGHT be Olaf?

Donald: Might be...

Goofy: There's only one way to find out.

(They keep looking)

Goofy: I think I mighta seen Olaf's legs leggin' it.

Donald: Where did he go?

(They return to the frozen pond in the center of the valley)

Donald: Look! Legs!

(The small set of Olaf's legs turn tail and run away on the ice. Sora 
dashes forward and grabs them, its feet wiggling in the air)

Sora: I caught them!

Donald: Yay!

Goofy: Great job, Sora!

Sora: Think that's all of him?

Donald: Yup!

Goofy: Anna'll know what to do next.

(They put Olaf together, but something is wrong)

Olaf: Wait, why does everybody look all wobbly?

Anna: It's not us, Olaf. You're about to tip over!

Olaf: Huh? Wha-- Oh no.

(Olaf's head falls off the oddly-shaped snowball)

Donald: Aww...

Sora: Yeah, I kinda figured that was wrong.

(Just past the waterfall, they find a hugely-oversized snowball with a 
large black rock embedded in it)

Sora: Is THIS him?

Goofy: Well, it's the right shape...

Donald: But it's huge.

(They put Olaf together a second time, but something is definitely wrong)

Olaf: Anna, question... When did you get so small and tiny?

Anna: Um, actually, Olaf, it's more that you're really big now.

Olaf: You're right! What a great view!

Goofy: Hmm... I think we did it wrong.

Olaf: Aw, but I like being tall.

Sora: Keep looking...

(On the other side of the waterfall, they slide down the slippery hill and 
find a small nook, where they find a tiny snowball with a single button of 
coal)

Sora: Hey, this is Olaf's body.

Donald: It is!

Goofy: Button and all!

(They return to the group and Anna puts Olaf back together)

Anna: And that should...do it.

(Olaf's body is correct, but strangely less colorful)

Goofy: You sure something's not missin'?

Kristoff: Nah. Looks right.

Olaf: Wow, I feel so much better.

(He touches his face)

Olaf: Wait! Where's my cute new nose! The one Anna gave me!

Anna: Uh, Sora... Do YOU have his nose?

Sora: I don't think so.

Donald: Nope, didn't see it.

(Olaf gasps sadly and Kristoff eyes Sven, sighing. He leans down to him 
sternly)

Kristoff: Sven...

(The reindeer smiles coyly and Kristoff opens his mouth, commanding. Sven 
obliges, revealing the carrot on his tongue. Kristoff grabs the carrot, 
pursing his lips, and shrugs at a disapproving Anna)

Kristoff (as Sven): "Someone had to pick it up!"

(Sven smirks)

Kristoff: You're right, buddy. Thanks for finding it...and not actually 
eating it. (as Sven) "Aw, you're welcome."

(They return Olaf's nose)

Olaf: My nose, it's back! Oh, I love having a nose!

Sora: Hey, Kristoff, how'd all this happen, anyway?

Kristoff: You know, I'm not sure. These weird animals--well, they were more 
like monsters--they just crashed into Olaf.

Goofy: I knew it.

Donald: The Heartless again!

Sora: Yeah.

Kristoff: The "Heart-less"? Hmm... And I thought the wolves around here 
were bad.

Anna: Kristoff, look!

(A group of Heartless appear over the pond)

Kristoff: They're back!

(Olaf waves his arms frantically)

Olaf: No... I've already fallen apart today.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy summon their weapons)

Sora: We know how to handle them! Anna, Kristoff, keep going!

Kristoff: Okay!

Anna: Wait? What?

(Kristoff leads her away from the battle. The three adventurers defeat the 
horde of Winterhorns, Flutterings, and Satyrs)

Sora: We better catch up!

Donald & Goofy: Yeah!

(They travel out of the Valley of Ice to the Frozen Wall, where an icy wind 
starts to pick up)

Donald (shivering): I'm getting cold.

Sora: Just keep moving. You'll warm up!

Goofy: Gee, nothin' ever gets you down, huh, Sora?

(Sora rides on a snowball and takes out a few Heartless)

Sora: All right! I love snow!

Donald: So much for "islander" Sora.

(They continue up the mountain reaching the Mountain Ridge from the other 
side, where snowdrifts containing horizontal icicles stick out dangerously 
in their path)

Sora: We're back! Finally.

Donald: That palace is incredible!

Goofy: Yeah. I wonder if Anna and the others made it there yet.

(At Elsa's Ice Palace, Anna speaks to her sister, pleading for her to 
return to Arendelle)

Anna: You kind of set off an eternal winter...everywhere.

Elsa (concerned): Everywhere?

Anna: Well, it's okay. You can just unfreeze it.

Elsa: No, I can't. I don't know how.

Anna: Sure you can. I know you can.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy approach the base of the staircase leading to the 
palace, where Sven has stuck his tongue to the banister. The reindeer 
attempts to pull it away with not much luck)

Sora: Anna and the others must've gone inside.

(Inside the palace, a great wind swirls as Elsa's conflicting emotions 
get the better of her. Anna shields her eyes at the stinging snow, but 
stands unrelenting to help her sister)

Elsa (screaming): I CAN'T!

(A giant burst of power erupts from the queen, striking Anna in the heart, 
causing her to lose her balance. Elsa whirls around, terrified at the 
sight of what she had just done. Outside, Sora feels a pain in his heart 
and winces, catching the attention of Donald and Goofy)

Donald: Sora?

Goofy: Are ya hurt?

Sora: No, I'm fine. But...I think something terrible must have happened.

(He looks back up to the palace, and the others follow his gaze)

Sora: I hope our friends are okay.

(The doors slam open and a giant snow monster appears in the doorway)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: What?

(The monster walks out with Olaf, Anna, Kristoff in his clutches)

Anna: Stop! Put us down!

(Anna beats against the monster's icy fingers)

Marshmallow: Go away!

(The monster tosses Anna and Kristoff, who take a bumpy slide down the 
stairs, past the trio)

Olaf: Heads up!

(Olaf's head flies into the snow-covered rock behind Anna and Kristoff)

Olaf: Watch out for my butt!

(Anna and Kristoff duck as Olaf's middle and legs fly in as well)

Anna (yelling): Hey! It is not nice to throw people!

(She gathers a snowball in an attempt to toss it at Marshmallow, but 
Kristoff stops her)

Kristoff: Whoa-whoa-whoa, feisty-pants.

(He grabs her)

Anna: Let me go!

Kristoff: Okay, relax. Just calm down. Calm down.

Anna: Okay! All right! I'm okay.

Kristoff: Just let the snowman be.

(He lets go of her)

Anna: I'm calm.

Kristoff: Great.

(She tosses the snowball less than calmly)

Kristoff: Huh? Oh, come on!

(It hits Marshmallow in the shoulder (barely a scratch) and he roars at 
them, his eyes glowing and spikes protruding from his legs and arms)

Kristoff: Aw, see? Now you made him mad.

Olaf: I'll distract him. You guys go!

(He waves them off and they run, while Olaf's torso and legs do the same)

Olaf: No, no. Not you guys!

(His face falls off the rock and into the snow)

Olaf (muffled): This just got a whole lot harder.

(Sora jumps in front)

Sora: We can buy you some time!

(Marshmallow stomps over to them and roars in their faces, spraying icy 
breath, causing the three to run away. Olaf's body comes out from hiding 
and rejoins with his head)

Olaf: Wait for me!

(Marshmallow pursues Donald and Sora, who looks around)

Sora: Huh? Where's Goofy?

(He spots him at a tree that's bent over from the heavy snow)

Goofy (calling): Hey, Sora! I got an idea!

Donald: Goofy, what are you doing?

Sora: Oh! That's perfect!

(Sora leads Marshmallow in the direction of the tree)

Donald: Huh? Hey!

(Goofy rubs his hands together and grabs onto the tree, lifting it up 
just as Sora latches onto him. They pull back the snow-laden tree as 
Marshmallow approaches)

Sora: Get ready... Okay, now!

(They release the tree and it snaps back into Marshmallow's face, knocking 
him over. Sora and Goofy get up and high-five)

Sora: Oh, yeah!

(Donald reaches them and summons his wand)

Donald: He's not done...

(Marshmallow gets up and Sora and Goofy join Donald)

Sora: Bring it, snowball!

(They take on the snow monster at the end of the ridge. He roars, hundreds 
of spikes emerging across his body, and tries to claw at the three of 
them. He corners them at the edge of the mountain and slams his fist into 
the ground)

Sora: Wh...what?

(The outcropping shatters and they tumble down the cliff once again. At 
the bottom, they rest before getting back up again)

Sora: Good thing snow's so soft. We could do this a HUNDRED times.

(Donald stands up)

Donald: No! Let's not.

Goofy: A-hyuck! Ya sure you don't wanna go again?

Sora: Nooo thank youuu!

(Sora stands)

Sora: Do you think everybody else made it?

Goofy: I don't think the snow monster got 'em.

Donald: They probably went back to the palace.

Sora: Makes sense. For us, too. We still need to talk to Elsa.

Goofy: Second time's the charm!

Sora: Yeah, back to the ice palace.

(As they return to the Snowfield once again, they see an auburn-haired 
man carrying Elsa over his shoulder. He is tall and well dressed, a 
sword attached to his hip)

Sora: Hey...that's Elsa. But who's that guy?

Goofy: It could be somebody from Arendelle who came up here to help her.

(Sora looks closer)

Sora: Don't think so. That doesn't look like help to me.

(Donald takes a careful look)

Donald: Oh no!

(A dark aura eminates from the man's body)

Goofy: Darkness?

Sora: Let's move!

(They lose sight of the man and find a pile of fallen down trees. Suddenly, 
the snow monster bursts from behind the trees and stomps out, growling and 
struggling to walk on his leg)

Sora: Him again?!

(They run over and summon their weapons, preparing for a rematch)

Sora: Hey! You'd better not have hurt our friends!

(The monster walks past them with barely a glance)

Sora: Huh?

Marshmallow: Elsaaa!

(They put their weapons away and run after him)

Sora: Hey, wait up! Are you...looking for Elsa, too?

(They run alongside his giant strides, but he stops and glares at them)

Sora: Whoa! Eeeasy! Do you wanna save her from the bad guy? We're on the 
same side.

(The monster settles down)

Marshmallow: Elsa...

Goofy: I guess all he ever wanted to do was keep Elsa safe.

Sora: Hey. We should team up, big guy.

Donald: Team up?!

Sora: C'mon. We wanna help her, too. Why not?

(Marshmallow watches them talk)

Sora: So, whaddaya say?

(Marshmallow nods and Sora walks closer)

Donald: Sora!

Goofy (to Donald): One great thing about Sora--he can always make friends 
with anybody.

(Donald crosses his arms)

Donald: Yippee...

Sora: Donald! Goofy! C'mon.

Donald & Goofy: Wait for us!

(They catch up and continue through the Snowfield. As they get nearer to 
Arendelle, they hear a voice up ahead)

Kristoff: Stop it. Put me down!

Sora: That's Kristoff.

(He turns to Marshmallow)

Sora: Do me a favor and wait here. If you come alone, Kristoff might 
freak out.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy run ahead, where Sven tosses Kristoff to the ground)

Kristoff (standing up): No, Sven! We're not going back. She's with her 
true love.

Sora: Kristoff!

(He sees them run in)

Kristoff: Sora.

Sora: You all right?

Kristoff: Yeah, I'm fine. I'm glad you guys are safe.

(Donald sees they're alone)

Donald: Hey!

Sora: Where'd Anna go?

(Kristoff sighs)

Kristoff: She's back at home.

Sora: Something happen?

(Sven gives a sad whine)

Kristoff: Anna was struck in the heart by Elsa's ice magic. If the ice 
isn't removed, she'll freeze forever. Only an act of true love can thaw a 
frozen heart. So I took her back to Arendelle and her true love, Hans.

Sora: But...what about you?

Kristoff: What ABOUT me?

Sora (awkwardly): Uh, I sorta assumed you guys were...

Kristoff: Nooo! I just keep her from getting lost.

Sora: Really? Oh, but you seem so...

Goofy: Perfect together!

Donald: Yeah, like me and Daisy!

(Kristoff shrugs, his shoulders slumped, and the wind picks up)

Kristoff: What?

(They look down to the castle town, where a swirl of storm clouds have 
gathered)

Kristoff: Anna.

(He runs off toward town with Sven in tow. The ground shakes and 
Marshmallow catches up to the three of them. He points toward the town)

Marshmallow: Elsa...

Sora: Is that where Elsa is?

(Marshmallow lets out a cascading roar)

Sora: Elsa and Anna might both need our help. Let's go!

(Donald and Goofy nod to each other and follow Sora into a run. They 
travel through the Foothills as the wind bares down upon them)

Sora: Storm's getting worse.

Donald: I'm freezing...

Goofy: Yeah, and the wind's just makin' it colder!

Donald: We got to get out of this storm!

Goofy: There must be some place we can use as shelter.

(Walking through the Foothills, they take cover behind rocks between the 
massive gusts of icy wind as Marshmallow braves the storm ahead of them. 
They catch up and stay behind the huge snow monster)

Goofy: Look! He's protectin' us from the storm!

Donald: We can make it!

(As they near town, the wind calms slightly)

Sora: Okay, guys. The storm's died down.

(The swirling clouds pelt Arendelle with snow)

Goofy: Gawrsh, I hope Anna and Elsa are okay.

Sora: Hurry!

(They run on ahead, where, like the fjord, the storm has frozen solid. 
Snow particles dangle in place in the still air. Anna walks along the 
ice, her hair now completely turned white. She is alone, shivering from 
head to toe. She sees Kristoff in the distance)

Anna: Kristoff?

(He sees her)

Kristoff: Anna!

(He runs her way as she hobbles in his direction. Anna hears the sound of 
a sword unsheathing and turns to see Hans with his weapon out stepping 
slowly toward the back of Elsa, who is on her knees)

Anna: Elsa?

(She sees Kristoff running towards her...and makes her decision. She turns 
away from Kristoff, who stops, just as Sora, Donald and Goofy arrive)

Sora: Elsa, Anna...

(Hans brings the sword up over his head to begin the swing as Elsa sobs, 
oblivious with grief. He brings the sword down, just as Anna rushes in to 
stop him...)

Anna: Nooo!

(...and she freezes solid. The sword makes contact and shatters, a pulse 
of magic knocks Hans off his feet as a final breath exhales from Anna)

Sora: Anna...

(The unconscious body of Hans erupts with darkness, enveloping Sora, 
Donald and Goofy)

Sora: What?!

(They struggle to move as they are dragged down into the pool of darkness. 
Sora opens his eyes and they find themselves in a wide landscape with a 
giant glowing orb of darkness in the center. Particles dance around it 
and it changes form, growing long tail. Claws surface, stomping the 
ground, and two glowing red eyes appear as a giant wolf's head emerges 
bearing the symbol of the Heartless. The Skll howls, leaping into the 
air and hovering)

Goofy: Do ya really think this will help Anna?

Sora: I don't know...but we'd better try something!

(Marshmallow catches up to them)

Donald: Let's get it.

(The Skll begins by tackling them head on and running around the field. 
Sora strikes, but it knocks him back with a giant claw. With a wailing 
howl, it sails high into the clouds spinning itself into a giant ball of 
darkness. It grows larger and larger, getting spherical, undulating 
within the clouds. Darkness rains from the black sun as several wolf 
heads stream downwards toward the party. Casting back the shadows, the 
dark orb slowly encroaches on the ground, threatening to crash into 
the earth. Marshmallow rushes forward and grabs the orb, holding it away 
from the ground)

Sora: Together!

(Sora leaps up to the dark sun, spinning his Keyblade on its surface in 
an attempt to dispell the darkness)

Sora: Come on!

(He spins his Keyblade faster, struggling against the weight of the orb 
that's only purpose is to crush them. Suddenly, the dark breaks beneath 
his fingers, giving way to light as cracks form on the orb's surface. The
