orange tendrils snake their way through the giant dark sphere, light 
shining outward from every crevice. The orb shatters into ice and the 
Skll falls to the ground. After a few more minutes of fighting, the Skll 
leaps into the air for a second chance, creating another black sun, however 
this last-ditch effort cannot sustain the fusion and it explodes brightly, 
expelling its energy in a giant blast. Marshmallow steps in front of Sora, 
Donald and Goofy, shielding them as the blast hits. He roars, struggling 
against the mighty wind, until his knees buckle and he's swept over them. 
He cries out, unable to catch anything to grab, as the wind sweeps the 
trio off their feet behind him. Feeling a cold surface against his chin, 
Sora awakes back on the frozen fjord. He along with Donald and Goofy 
get to their feet, seeing the sight before them. Sora starts to run, but 
something stops him. Elsa is weeping, her arms draped around the frozen 
form of Anna as Olaf, Kristoff and Sven look on. The sorrow in the air 
is palpable. Suddenly, the area around Anna's heart begins to steam and 
then melt, the magic making its way across her shoulders and down her 
arms and the cape billowing around her. Olaf gasps and Sven nudges 
Kristoff, who was looking away. Kristoff's eyes widen and Sora, Donald 
and Goofy wait with bated breath. The melting spreads through Anna's 
toes and fingertips and she finally takes a breath, her braid falling 
over her shoulder. The trio rush forward excitedly, but are surrounded 
by a whirlwind of darkness)

Sora: What?

(The whirlwind encases them in a dome and a flash spreads out from it, 
casting the world out of time. Sora peers through the dark wind, where 
Arendelle outside has stopped moving. Larxene appears before them)

Larxene: So, love has filled BOTH their hearts with light.

(They take a defensive stance)

Sora: Larxene!

Larxene: Two in one world... Definitely didn't see THAT coming.

Sora (angrily): First Marluxia, now you. What is this all about?!

Larxene: Oh, I see, so you bumped into Marluxia. (annoyed) Then why am 
I explaining this again? I told you before: The New Seven Hearts. If you 
mess up and don't find your seven guardians of light, we're gonna need 
another group to fall back on.

Sora: Leave innocent people out of it!

Larxene: Ohh, look at this tough guy. Such a big boy now. Well, maybe 
you should do your job, and find the other guardians of light.

Sora: Please, like you've found your thirteen. The King said you're one 
seeker of darkness short.

Larxene: Oh no, we're set.

(Donald and Goofy jump)

Sora: Huh?

(Larxene giggles through a wide grin and vanishes along with the dark dome)

Sora (thinking): They have all thirteen? Then if we don't find our seven, 
they'll go after Elsa and Anna.

(Elsa looks up, noticing her sister is alive. She smiles, giving her a 
big hug. Sora frowns, despite the happy reunion)

Goofy: It'll be okay. They're strong.

Donald: And now, it's our turn!

(He looks back at them)

Sora: You're right. They have each other.

Elsa: Anna...

Anna: Oh, Elsa.

Elsa: You sacrificed yourself for me?

Anna: I love you.

(Olaf gasps, lifting his head off his body)

Olaf: "An act of true love will thaw a frozen heart."

(Elsa and Anna hold hands)

Elsa: Love...will thaw. (to Anna) Love...

Anna: Elsa?

(Elsa looks down at her hands)

Elsa: Of course. Love!

(She spreads her arms downward and the ice from the fjord spreads out in a 
snowflake shape, magically taking off into the air. Kristoff marvels at 
this sight as Sven tries to catch a floating snowflake on his tongue. The 
magic spreads beneath Sora, Donald and Goofy who jump for joy)

Sora: Yes!

(As the lake thaws, a ship beneath the ice rises to the surface under 
their feet. The frozen magic flies throughout the down, breaking through 
the snow on the rooftops and the water in the fountains. As Elsa raises 
her arms, the floating ice coalesces into a giant snowflake in the air, 
and she blasts it apart with a wave. Everyone is overjoyed to see the sun, 
and Anna places her hand on Elsa's shoulder. Sora and company leave 
Arendelle and travel to Yen Sid's tower, where the sorcerer has also 
summoned King Mickey and Riku. They turn as the door opens)

Sora: Sorry we're late.

Mickey: It's okay. You got here as fast as you could.

(They fill everyone in on what they've learned so far)

Sora: The Organization claims to HAVE their thirteen darknesses.

Mickey: Do we believe it's true?

Sora: Umm...I don't know, but there's something else they keep mentioning. 
They're after a "New Seven Hearts," which seems to be code for "let's go 
bother more princesses."

Yen Sid: Well, as the original princesses of hearts' time for protecting 
the pure light has ended, they have passed the light to others. Our enemy 
must certainly be cognizant of this. If the "New Seven Hearts" is what 
they wish to call them, so be it.

Sora: But Kairi hasn't passed on her power. Is she one of the new seven?

Mickey: She must be. But still, she chose to wield a Keyblade and fight 
with us as one of the guardians of light.

Sora: Yeah...

Donald: We haven't found Terra yet.

Goofy: Hey, at least we've tracked down Ventus. Vanitas told us that he's 
inside Sora's heart.

Jiminy: And so did Ansem the Wise in his data, so it almost certainly must 
be true.

(Donald and Goofy nod)

Mickey: That's great! Now we can rescue Ven.

Riku: Maybe, except Aqua's the only one who knows where he's hidden. We 
still have to find her first.

(Sora feels a tugging in his chest)

Sora: I'll go.

Donald & Goofy: What?!

Mickey: Is that wise?

Yen Sid: You need the power of waking, Sora. Do you have it?

Sora: Uh...no? Probably not.

Yen Sid (sternly): Without that power, you are not ready to face the realm 
of darkness.

Sora: C'mon...

(Riku laughs)

Sora: What's so funny?

Riku: Sorry. Master Yen Sid knows you a little too well. He said you'd try 
to stage a half-baked rescue.

(Donald and Goofy start to laugh, followed by the King)

Sora: Yeah! Laugh it up!

Riku: Sora, I know you're volunterring because you're worried--about me and 
Mickey.

Sora: Yeah...

(Riku places a hand on his shoulder)

Riku: Well, thanks. But, the power of waking's important. You can come to 
the rescue once you've got that. Sound fair?

Sora: Yeah. All right. But be safe. No reckless stunts.

Riku (nodding): Yes, sir.

(Donald and Goofy move aside and Jiminy Cricket jumps down onto the duck's 
hat to whisper softly to each other)

Donald: Sora's the reckless one.

Jiminy: No, not exactly. He just doesn't think.

Goofy: If only he listened to Master Yen Sid the way he listens to Riku. 
That would be a good start.

Sora (miffed): I'm listening now.

(Everyone but Sora chuckles)

Yen Sid: Very good. Sora will continue his journey to build his powers, 
while Mickey and Riku will focus on the search for Aqua.

(They stand at attention)

Sora, Donald, Goofy, Riku & Mickey: Yes, sir!

(In the Badlands on the outskirts of the Keyblade Graveyard, Marluxia and 
Larxene stand atop thirteen pillars of earth)

Marluxia: So, why are you back?

Larxene: Nice way to greet your old partner in crime.

(Marluxia gives a small laugh at the title)

Larxene: So, why do you think the old geezer took us back? He must know 
we backstabbed the Organization when Xemnas was running it.

Marluxia: Xehanort doesn't care about you or me. To him, we're nothing but 
empty husks. The old Organization was the same. Xehanort needs thirteen 
vessels to hold his essence.

Larxene: Husks? Not me. You up for another coup?

(She gives him a coy smile)

?????: Oh, please. You couldn't do it last time. You gotta play it smart, 
like me.

(They look over to another pillar, where a man with blond hair is holding 
a large sitar)

Larxene: What?! You're not smart!

Demyx: Well, you heard what Marly said. I don't have to be smart.

(He smirks)

Larxene: Or capable, or likeable, or attractive. A cereal bowl would make 
a better vessel.

(Demyx tunes his strings)

Demyx: Whoa now, you are WAY out of line. I am extremely imposing...when I 
want to be. Which is, admittedly, almost never.

Larxene: Why haven't you gone to any worlds? Are you slacking?

Demyx: 'Course not. I got benched.

Larxene: Huh?

Marluxia: Sax brought Vexen on board. They must be planning to use replicas.

Larxene: Those windup toys?

Demyx: Oh, no. The replicas are way more real than you remember. I mean, one 
stole my spot!

(Larxene bursts into laughter)

Larxene: OF COURSE it stole your spot. You're dumb as a brick.

Demyx: Har-dee-har.

Marluxia: Vexen's latest replicas are no mere puppets. The Riku replica we 
used in Castle Oblivion was just a prototype. The next replica, the one 
crafted from Sora's memories, was real enough to join our ranks. And Vexen 
claims the new ones will be human in every way. If he ever finishes them.

Larxene: Oh... The thing is...I kinda told Sora and his nitwits that we're 
ready. My bad.

??????: Let them believe as much.

(Xemnas appears on another pillar)

Larxene: Ugh. Xemnas.

Xemnas: If they think that we have all thirteen darknesses, then they will 
panic. And panic leads to a lack of preparation.

Demyx: Yeah, totally.

(Larxene points towards Demyx)

Larxene: Why is this thing a member again?

Demyx: Hey now! Pointing is rude.

Xemnas: The first six members of the original Organization were all 
apprentices to Ansem the Wise, and the seventh and eighth members joined 
thereafter. The thirteenth member was Roxas, a Keyblade wielder. So. What 
about you? How do you suppose I chose numbers nine through twelve?

Larxene: Because our hearts are ber powerful.

Xemnas: Wrong. You have been brought together for another purpose.

??????: What? So that we can rot away on the bottom rung?

(A man with short blond hair and multiple earrings appears on the pillar 
adjacent to Demyx)

Larxene (sighing): You're in too? What is this, Organization Rehash?

Luxord: I happen to play an important role. No one "benched" me.

Demyx: You were listening? So not cool.

Luxord: One must hold one's cards as long as necessary.

Larxene: What "important role"? That stupid box that Xigbar claims is real, 
but won't tell us a thing about?

Luxord: You'll just have to ask Xigbar that.

(He plays with his cards in his hand)

Luxord: Now then, Xemnas, what is this "purpose"? You didn't invite us 
back for old times' sake.

Xemnas: You four are going to reveal your greatest secret: the ancient 
Keyblade legacy that slumbers within you.

(They each react with surprise and skepticism as Xemnas gives a breathy 
laugh. Meanwhile, Sora, Donald and Goofy return to Le Grand Bistrot in 
Twilight Town to give Little Chef more ingredients from their travels. 
Scrooge walks into the kitchen where Little Chef is perched on Sora's head)

Scrooge (ecstatic): Me business is boomin! Splendid! Just splendid! You two 
have outdone yourselves. The critics are going cuckoo and the register, 
"ka-ching". I canna wait to see what it is you cook up next.

(He takes out a present)

Scrooge: Nor can the customers.

(He offers the present and Sora takes it, laughing)

Sora: We try! Right, Little Chef?

(He lifts a finger to the rat, who high-fives it confidently. Later, Sora 
sets sail for a world of ships and sea-faring pirates. A sea shanty plays 
to open our tale:

"Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me
The Kraken leapt from the ocean brine
Look out, me hearties yo ho
And to the Locker the sparrow confined
Look out, me hearties yo ho
Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me
A goddess thought she'd a sparrow save
Look out, me hearties yo ho
And brought a blackguard back from the grave
Look out, me hearties yo ho
Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me
The Flying Dutchman is on the hunt
Look out, me hearties yo ho
To punish a sparrow for his affront
Look out, me hearties yo ho
Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me
Within the chest his secret sleeps
Look out, me hearties yo ho
The heart of Davy Jones still beats
Look out, me hearties yo ho
Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me"

Sora, Donald and Goofy arrive in the night under a cloudless sky)

Sora (singing): Yo ho, yo ho, a pirates life for me

(Sora hums to the song as Donald and Goofy row, each dressed in pirate garb)

Donald: Why are you so happy?

Sora: 'Cause we get to be pirates again!

Goofy: Yep, you always did like this world.

Sora: How could anyone not? Still...it's a real shame we don't have a 
bigger ship.

(They sail upon a fairly small raft lit by a single lantern. The fog 
looms around them)

Donald: Got any idea where we're going?

Sora: Where else? The edge of the world!

(He points ahead confidently)

Goofy (saluting): Captain Sora!

(Sora puts on his best pirate voice)

Sora: What ails ya, Mister Goofy?

Goofy: The edge of the world!

(He points forward)

Sora: Aye!

Goofy: We're runnin' outta sea, sir!

Sora: Aye! We're runnin' outta sea.

(He chuckles, then glancing at Donald, realizes what Goofy said)

Sora & Donald: Running OUT?!

(Up ahead, the ocean water rushes forward and down into an abyss, dragging 
the raft with the current. The raft rocks, knocking Goofy over while Sora 
clutches the mast)

Sora: Hard to starboard!

(Goofy and Donald try rowing with reckless abandon as the edge grows nearer)

Goofy: But there's no time, Captain!

(The raft reaches the edge and careens over the waterfall, sending Sora, 
Donald and Goofy screaming over the world's end. In the midst of Davy 
Jones' Locker, the trio awake and sit up, surrounded on all sides by 
endless dry sand. The three sigh together)

Sora: Where'd we end up THIS TIME?

(Eventually, they get up and walk across the empty dunes, only finding 
more sand ahead of them, no matter how long they trudge)

Goofy: We've been walkin' forever.

Donald: I'm exhausted...

Sora: Some pirates. We won't get anywhere without a ship.

(He looks up through the heat in the air, making out an image of a pirate 
ship sailing over the desert)

Sora: A ship...

(He stops, causing Goofy, and then Donald, to crash into him)

Donald: Sora... This is dry land.

(The duck shrieks as he also sees the ship)

Goofy: Oh boy!

(Strangely enough, the ship comes clearer into view, drifting through the 
sand as if by magic)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: It IS a ship!

(They run to catch up to the forward vessel, being pulled by an incalculable 
amount of odd white crabs. From behind, a familiar man gains on them and 
then passes by, raising an arm in greeting)

????: Hail, Sora!

Sora: Huh? (excited) Jack Sparrow!

(Jack stops momentarily to face them)

Jack Sparrow: CAPTAIN Jack Sparrow.

Goofy: Sure is!

(Donald giggles)

Sora: Hey, Jack. Where are we?

(He looks back at Jack, who's already begun running again)

Jack Sparrow: Belay that. Ship absconding!

Sora: Huh?

Jack Sparrow: Help me catch the Pearl before she gets away!

Sora (saluting): Aye, aye, Captain!

(They race to catch up with the Black Pearl, but are delayed by attacking 
Heartless)

Donald: Heartless?

Goofy: We better get rid of 'em quick.

(The Pearl turns, sending cannonfire in their direction)

Sora: Who's shooting at us?

Jack Sparrow: Cease fire! Cease fire!

(They avoid the cannonballs and take out the Earth Core Heartless, using 
the slowed momentum of the Pearl to their advantage. Reaching the still 
moving ship, a group of Anchor Raider Heartless appear, swinging the 
anchors at the end of their right hands like propellers)

Sora: That's who's doing this.

Jack Sparrow: No one said you could use my ship!

(Together with Captain Jack, they take out the Anchor Raiders and take 
back the Pearl. Jack Sparrow watches from atop the mast as the ship crests 
the final sand dune and reaches the sea's edge of Davy Jones' Locker. Sora, 
Donald and Goofy stand at the bow, as more familiar faces stand aghast at 
the sight from the beach. Elizabeth Swann and her betrothed Will Turner are 
joined by the previously deceased Hector Barbossa and others in their crew. 
A mysterious woman with dreadlocks named Tia Dalma pets the crab in her 
hand, chuckling to herself. Will watches in amazement as the Black Pearl 
settles into the water with a loud splash. As Jack and the trio disembark 
from the Pearl as it reaches the sea, a smiles comes to the faces of both 
Elizabeth and Joshamee Gibbs, Jack's first mate)

Gibbs: Jack!

Jack Sparrow (commandingly): Mister Gibbs.

Gibbs: Aye, Cap'n.

Jack Sparrow: I thought so. I expect you're able to account for your 
actions, then.

Gibbs (confused): Sir?

Jack Sparrow: There's been a perpetual and virulent lack of discipline upon 
my vessel--why?

Gibbs: Sir, you're... You're in Davy Jones' Locker, Cap'n.

(Jack's face twitches)

Sora: Davy Jones' Locker?

Jack Sparrow: I know that. I know where I am. And don't think I don't.

(He turns to Sora)

Jack Sparrow: I'm in Davy Jones' Locker. Assuredly.

Barbossa: Jack Sparrow.

(Sora gasps)

Sora: Barbossa!

(Barbossa smiles at them cheekily as the wind blows through the feather 
in his wide-brimmed hat. Jack saunters forward towards him)

Jack Sparrow: Ah, Hector! It's been too long. Hasn't it?

Barbossa: Aye, Isla de Muerta, remember? You shot me.

Jack Sparrow: No, I didn't.

(Will and Elizabeth walk up to Sora and friends)

Will: Sora. We meet again.

Elizabeth: It's lovely to see you all.

Sora: Oh! Will. Elizabeth. Is...something about you different?

(They notice her more pirate-y clothing)

Goofy: Yeah, you look all swashbuckly.

Elizabeth: Well, I've seen some adventures. But I never thought I'd find 
YOU here.

Sora: Speaking of... Where exactly IS "here"? What's all this about a locker?

Will: Davy Jones' Locker. Jack neglected to repay a certain debt to Jones. 
So Jones sent the Kracken to devour Jack, and that's how he ended up here.

Sora: Then...Davy Jones' Locker... (frightened) You're saying that we've 
gone beyond...

Goofy (sadly): Beyond the grave?

(Donald whimpers)

Elizabeth: And we're here to wrest Jack from his fate.

(Jack notices the mysterious woman with them)

Jack Sparrow: Tia Dalma, out and about, eh?

(She smiles at him)

Jack Sparrow: You add an agreeable sense of the macabre to any delirium.

(She chuckles softly)

Will: He thinks we're a hallucination.

Jack Sparrow: Heh... Complete with these three masqueraders.

(He motions toward Sora, Donald and Goofy)

Elizabeth: Jack, this is real. We're here. We've come to rescue you!

(He looks at her, cycling through his emotions)

Jack Sparrow: Have you, now? That's very kind of you. But it would seem that 
as I possess a ship and you don't, you're the ones in need of rescuing. And 
I'm not sure as I'm in the mood.

(He walks up to Elizabeth, narrowing his eyes, and Will moves forward)

Will: Jack, Cutler Beckett has the heart of Davy Jones. He controls the 
Flying Dutchman.

Elizabeth: He's taking over the seas.

Tia Dalma: And him must be stopped. The Brethren Court is called.

(Jack turns to her)

Jack Sparrow: Leave you people alone for just a minute and look what 
happens. Everything's gone to pot!

(He throws his hands up in the air. Sora turns to Donald and Goofy, 
crossing his arms)

Sora: I'm lost. What's going on?

Goofy: Well, umm...sounds to me like this Beckett fella they mentioned is 
tryin' to conquer the ocean.

Sora: Oh.

Donald (scowling): The sea belongs to everyone!

Sora: Yeah! No conquerers.

Donald: Yeah!

(They nod)

Gibbs: Listen, Jack. The world needs you back somethin' fierce.

Will: And you need a crew.

Jack Sparrow: Why should I sail with any of you? Four of you have tried to 
annihilate me.

Sora (waving): Jack, WE'RE on your side.

Jack Sparrow: Aye, so you are, mates. I never could have caught the Pearl 
without you. Sora, Donald, Goofy, you're hired.

Sora: Yes!

Jack Sparrow: Now, as for the rest of you...

(He walks up to Tia Dalma and copies her infectious smile)

Jack Sparrow: Tia Dalma, you're in. Gibbs, you can come.

(Gibbs gives a satisfied chortle)

Jack Sparrow: Weigh anchor, all hands! Prepare to make sail!

(The crew starts toward the Pearl as Jack takes out his compass, the 
needle spinning continuously. Unsatisfied, he closes it. A captain without 
a heading)

Barbossa: Jack... 

(He looks over, seeing a grinning Barbossa holding up the ancient charts)

Barbossa: Which way you goin', Jack?

(Hector taps on the maps with his long fingers forcing Jack to hold back a 
sneer. Later, once everyone is aboard, Jack lets Sora try his hand at the 
wheel)

Jack Sparrow: Right then, Mister Sora. The helm is yours, provided...you 
pass muster.

(He places a hand on Sora's shoulder)

Sora: Huh?

(Jack leans in closer, pointing ahead)

Jack Sparrow: See that island there with the two peaks? Prove you can reach 
that, and the open sea is yours.

Sora: Oh!

(He gives an excited laugh)

Sora: Aye, aye!

(Later, after sailing for a while, the ship has nearly come to a stop. 
Sora, Donald and Goofy sit on deck at the base of the mast)

Sora: So, we DO have a destination, right?

Goofy: I can't tell anymore.

Donald: Jack is just making it up.

(Jack stands at a pair of barrels, idly playing with the rings of the map 
charts. Tia Dalma walks up to them and smiles)

Tia Dalma: Cast your fate with Jack Sparrow, and you soon be sharing in the 
wrath of Davy Jones.

Sora: The guy Will mentioned? Who does he think he is, anyway? And what did 
Jack ever do to him?

Tia Dalma (coyly suspicious): Truly? You don't know who Davy Jones be? And 
you say you be men of the sea?

(The three tense up and Sora tries to cover)

Sora: Let's put it this way--we're from ANOTHER sea.

(Donald and Goofy nod in agreement)

Tia Dalma: Are you now? Jack and Davy Jones' fate be intertwined. Jones, 
him raised Jack's precious Pearl from the depths and make Jack captain for 
thirteen years. In exchange, Jack promise to give Jones him soul as payment. 
But thirteen years pass, and Jack fail to return.

(Will concerningly looks toward Elizabeth, who herself is frowning, her 
back turned to him)

Tia Dalma: So Jones, him send the Kraken to devour Jack, taking him and 
the Pearl back to the depths. But... if Jones learn that Witty Jack cheat 
that fate, him wanna punish Jack even worse. And Jack's friends, too.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy whimper)

Donald: Are you, um, talking about us?

Goofy: Ya mean that the Kraken's gonna eat us?

Sora: Aw, let the Kraken have a crack. I ain't scared!

(She leans over him)

Tia Dalma: Hmm... Not scared at all? That be rare. Most men, them run for 
land at the mention of the Kraken. Not you.

(She stands, turning in Jack's direction)

Tia Dalma: But Jack be scared. He want to be free of his debt to Davy Jones. 
That's why him need the box.

Sora, Donald and Goofy: Box?!

(Sora glances at Donald in mutual understanding)

Tia Dalma: It be a chest...where Davy Jones lock away the part of him that 
hurt. The pain it cause him was too much to live with...but not enough to 
cause him to die.

Sora: And...what part of him is that?

(She chuckles, placing a hand over her chest)

Tia Dalma: Him heart.

(Meanwhile on the deck of a separate vessel, Vexen stands with Luxord)

Vexen: Oh, how does he do it? A creature absent a heart and yet somehow 
able to keep existing... Not even my finest replica can claim that 
achievement. The secret must be in that box. I have to know what mysteries 
it contains.

Luxord: I believe our orders were to find the box and seize it. No more. 
Put a leash on that runaway curiosity.

Vexen: Always so shortsighted. Why would the Organization seek me out 
just as soon as I was recompleted--if not to affirm my intellectual prowess 
and invest in my research? Every stride I make is a stride for all of us.

Luxord: Oh really? And what exactly are we striding towards?

(Vexen narrows an eye)

Vexen: Luxord, do I detect...a hint of treachery in your words?

Luxord: What? Don't be absurd. But to be clear, I serve the Organization. 
I don't share your need to please Xemnas. He's good at wrapping you around 
his little finger--always has been.

Vexen: All I desire is the freedom to continue my research. Ansem the Wise 
refused to nurture my talents. So I cast my lot with Xemnas--with Xehanort, 
rather. Simple as that.

Luxord: I see. And you don't care how he uses your research?

Vexen: Not in the slightest. All that concerns me is that I complete the 
perfect human vessel.

Luxord: That's all well and good. But I know this world better than you. 
Kindly stay out of the way.

Vexen: Oh, of course. Considering those pests have shown up, I'd hardly 
get anything done.

Luxord: I already know what to do with the "pests." Then you can resume 
your stuffy studies.

Vexen: Ah, that's my boy. I'll be watching from the shadows, then.

(He disappears in a corridor of darkness. Back aboard the Black Pearl, 
Sora along with the ship and the crew have been entirely submerged in the 
water. They hold their breath as the sun sets with a flash of green. 
Suddenly, the water surges downward and the Black Pearl emerges from the 
sea, the briny water splashing off its sails. The crew inhales the sea 
air and regains their bearings. Sora stands, waving water off his wet clothes)

Sora: Thanks, Jack. You could've warned us.

Goofy: Yeah, everything went topsy-turvy and upsy-downsy!

Sora: Well, at least we're back in the land of the living.

Donald: Thank goodness!

(Jack stands up and adjusts his hat)

Jack Sparrow: Never fear. All according to plan.

Barbossa: But that be no reason to rest easy.

(He looks out to sea, Will following his lead)

Will: A ship!

(They gaze at another pirate ship sailing in their direction)

Elizabeth: I've never seen one like that.

(A horde of Vaporflies sails out ahead of it)

Sora: Heartless!

(Tia Dalma smirks at his understanding of the situation as a Raging Vulture 
Heartless soars above the ship. It roars, sending a cascade of energy from 
its two cannon wings)

Gibbs: Look out!

(The first strike hits the water, causing a giant splash and rocking the 
Black Pearl, knocking the crew off balance and spraying them with mist)

Jack Sparrow: Barbossa, have you allied with those fiends again?

Barbossa: Don't impugn me honor. Why would I conspire with them?

Jack Sparrow: But you DID conspire with them.

Elizabeth: Could you discuss it later?

(Tia Dalma whispers something in Sora's ear)

Sora: Huh?

(She laughs softly, smiling as he looks back at her before walking away)

Will: Get ready!

(The Raging Vulture flies overhead)

Goofy: Hmm... I sure do wish we could get a little closer.

Donald: What? Walk on air? We can't do that!

(Vaporfly Heartless zoom above them, leaving trails of colored smoke in 
their wake)

Sora: We can!

(Sora runs forward before they can stop him)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(He jumps off the ship's deck and onto a blue smoke trail, riding it up 
into the sky)

Sora (yelling back): Donald and Goofy, protect the ship! I'll handle the 
Heartless.

(He reaches the Vaporfly and jumps aboard. Utilizing the Vaporfly's 
torpedoes and flight, Sora weakens the Raging Vulture before leaping aboard 
the Heartless itself. As he grabs hold of one of the Vulture's back spikes, 
the Heartless flaps its wings, flying higher into the sky. Once it settles 
down, Sora leaps across its back from spike to spike. The bird's long neck 
turns to face him as he reaches its head and screams in his face, almost 
knocking him off)

Sora: Taaake...THIS!

(Sora leaps at the face of the Vulture, serving up a killing blow. A 
cracking sound reverberates and the Heartless starts to glow, a giant Heart 
rising out of its body as its form dissipates)

Sora: All right!

(As the Vaporflies vanish in succession, Sora is stranded in the air)

Sora: Wha-- Wait! Oh noooooo!

(He falls, landing straight down into the water. Not too long after...)

Donald: Sora?

Goofy: Sora?

(He opens his eyes, seeing the faces of Donald and Goofy staring down at him)

Donald & Goofy: Sora!

(He lies on a sandy beach with the sound of the waves in his ears)

Sora (weakly): Donald? Goofy?

(They nod and he slowly sits up)

Sora: Where are the others?

Goofy: After you fell, we came looking for ya. I guess they musta kept goin'.

Donald (sternly): That's desertion.

Sora: Oh... And I was so happy that we got to see them again.

Jack: That eager to sail under Captain Jack Sparrow?

(They turn to see Jack approach from behind)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: Jack!

(A white crab falls out from behind his leg and scuttles away. Meanwhile, 
aboard another ship, the Endeavour, the real Jack Sparrow has been pulled 
aboard and into the Captain's Cabin, where he finds Lord Cutler Beckett)

Beckett: Perhaps you'll consider an arrangement. One which requires nothing 
from you but information.

(He holds out a small glass of sherry, which Jack takes)

Jack Sparrow: Regarding the Brethren Court, no doubt.

(Beckett raises his own glass up to drink, which Jack takes also)

Jack Sparrow: In exchange for fair compensation...

(Jack drinks the first glass)

Jack Sparrow: Square my debt with Jones...

(and the second)

Jack Sparrow: Guarantee my freedom...

(Beckett pops the cork on the bottle of sherry and pours another drink)

Beckett: Of course. It's just good business.

(Jack picks up a small human statue)

Jack Sparrow: Were I in a divulgatory mood, what then might I divulge?

Beckett: Everything. Where are they meeting? What are their plans?

(Back on the Huddled Isles, Sora, Donald and Goofy are with Jack)

Jack: Shall we?

(He turns away, leading them further into the island)

Sora: Shall we what?

Jack: Some pirate! Won't get anywhere without a ship.

(Donald and Goofy exchange puzzled looks)

Jack: So, let's go get one.

(Sora can barely contain his excitement)

Sora: Yes!

(Sora chuckles happily and starts to follow Jack, Donald and Goofy after him)

Goofy: Sora and Jack sure are cut from the same cloth.

Donald: They even talk alike!

(Sora stops, reflecting on what Tia Dalma has whispered to him earlier)

Tia Dalma: Use that key to free me, Sora, and you have my most certain 
promise--all the power on the sea you ever wish for be yours.

Sora: Free her how?

Donald: Sora?

Goofy: What's wrong?

Sora: Huh?

(He turns around)

Sora: Oh, nothing, really. I'm good.

(They explore the island, swimming into one of the many underwater caverns)

Goofy: Look! Something's glowin'.

(They see two strange glowing rods emerging from the seabed)

Donald: And there's a chest!

(A chest is nestled directly between the rods)

Goofy: That seems suspiciously convenient.

Sora: I'll check it out.

(He swims closer)

Donald: Sora, this could be dangerous.

(Sora smirks)

Sora: But Donald! No pirate worth his salt ignores treasure.

(Sora swims to the sea floor and taps on the treasure chest. Suddenly 
the ground beneath him quakes, sending up dirt in the water and clouding 
his vision, as two gigantic blue jaws clamp over him and the chest. 
Breaking out of the ground, the Lightning Angler ejects Sora from his 
mouth and attacks them. After a strike with electricity from the Heartless's 
many glowing spikes, the trio manage to dislodge the treasure chest from 
within its throat. Its eye scans its surroundings, trying to make a break 
for it, but crashes into the cave wall. The Heart floats out of its body 
as the rocky wall opens into a further cave containing jellyfish. Exploring 
the inner cave, they reach a tunnel that becomes shallow until they wade 
into a huge open-air cavern. Inside, they find an abandoned pirate ship 
with orange sails)

Sora: Oh, cool.

(They run forward, Sora leaping into the air)

Sora: Woo-hoo! It's our very own ship!

(He laughs)

Jack: Are you certain about that?

(Jack appears from up on deck)

Sora: Jack?

Jack: Finder's keepers.

Goofy: How'd he get here so fast?

Jack: Mine. Savvy?

(Donald stamps his foot)

Donald: No savvy!

Sora: Jack, you already have the Black Pearl.

Jack: Aye, to which this ship holds no candle. But, take what you can, mate.

(He walks forward, but stops)

Jack: Now then, my ship has a captain, but it does appear I'm in need of 
a crew.

(He turns around in their direction)

Jack: Suppose you'll have to do. Don't dawdle. Climb aboard!

(He waves them on)

Sora: Ummm...

(They enter the Leviathan and Sora takes the helm)

Jack: Ready now, helmsman?

Sora: Ready enough, Cap'n, but...aren't we kinda...trapped?

Jack: Now, Sora, I know you've made passage through straits far more dire 
than this. Just follow your heart's command.

(He nods, grabbing the help with both hands and taking a deep breath. Ahead, 
the cave wall collapses into open air, the bright sun shining through and 
allowing the seawater to unmoor the ship from the sandbar)

Sora: Make way!

(The ship sails out of the cave, free to sail the Caribbean ocean. Once 
they find their bearings, they sail into a fog, where a giant ship silently 
sails near them. Its sails are emblazoned with the Nobody insignia)

Sora: That ship...

(Donald and Goofy summon their weapons)

Donald: It's the Heartless.

(Goofy sees a hooded figure on its deck)

Goofy: But look. This time there's somebody aboard.

Sora: Isn't that...

Jack: Not the merry company I'd hoped for.

(The hooded figure removes his hood to reveal...)

Luxord: Parley!

Sora: A black coat.

Jack: Of course...

(Luxord boards the Leviathan)

Sora: You back in the Organization?

Luxord: Yes. Surprising, isn't it, that they'd do me the honor? Never count 
your cards until they've all been dealt.

Sora: Jack, don't you give this creep the time of day.

Donald: Yeah!

Luxord: Come now, are you really so unsophisticated that you'd decline a 
gentlemanly conversation?

Sora: What'd you say?!

Jack: Sora. Stand down. It's the Code. Mustn't strike a pirate aboard ship...
when said pirate offers to confabulate.

Luxord: Ah yes. And how could I love games and contests without honoring the 
rules? Because only by winning fairly does victory have any savor at all.

Jack: But...of course the Code is actually more guidelines than rules. Speak 
your piece.

Luxord: I am looking...for a box. A chest, perhaps.

(Jack's face twitches)

Luxord: You know the one?

Jack: Yes. M-maybe. No! I know of A box. But said box is not a box you want 
to trifle with, mate. Trust me.

Luxord: Really? A wager, then.

Jack: And of what nature would this wager be?

Luxord: What say we have a little race to that charming port town which you 
hold so dear?

Jack: Port Royal?

Luxord: Yes. Whoever reaches it first is the victor. And the stakes: you 
tell me all about that chest.

Jack: Against what?

Luxord: I will get you whatever it is you want.

(Jack mulls over this)

Jack: Done!

Sora: Jack!

Luxord: Then we have an accord.

(Luxord teleports from the Leviathan back to his own ship)

Luxord: Now, let us begin!

Jack: All hands! Prepare to make sail!

(Jack starts walking toward the stairs)

Sora: But Jack!

Jack: Drop canvas!

(Sora runs after him)

Sora: Hey... Jack!

(Jack rushes up the stairs)

Jack: With a will, lads!

Sora: Jack, listen!

Jack (whirling around): What?!

Sora: You can't let him get his hands on that box. Do you really know 
whatever it is that he's looking for?

Jack: Let's just say...there's a potential possibility he wants the chest 
containing Davy Jones' heart. But I haven't the foggiest notion why he'd 
covet the blighted thing.

Goofy: Is it a BLACK box?

Jack: It is more black than blue... So, yes!

Sora (to Donald and Goofy): Hmm... Do you think it's the one?

Donald: Could be.

Goofy: And winnin' the race would keep it out of Organization XIII's hands.

Sora: Hey... You're right!

Jack: What are you three muttering on about?

Sora: Basically, we need to win this race.

Jack: Precisely. No purchase, no pay. You might have the makings of a pirate 
after all.

Sora: Yeah!

(Sora rushes to the helm and the race begins)

Goofy: First one to Port Royal wins!

Jack: And I say we make it interesting. Let's try out those cannons.

(They sail east, weaving between small islands, and fighting off Heartless 
ships until they have Port Royal in their sights)

Jack: That's it. Don't let up now!

Goofy: Go, go go!

(They near the waters of the port)

Donald: Getting close!

Jack: Lookouts, report!

Goofy: Starboard side, all clear!

Donald: Port, too!

Sora: We got this one in the bag.

(From behind the fog looms heavy and other ships appear around Luxord's 
vessel, gaining on them)

Luxord: The game isn't over until it's over.

(Luxord raises an arm)

Luxord: Fire!

(From both sides, the ships aim their cannons at the Leviathan, rocking 
the boat)

Jack: They're closing in! Come about! Make ready to return fire!

(Sora nods)

Sora: Aye, aye!

(Sora spins the wheel with a large thrust and the ship begins to turn as 
a multitude of cannonballs splash in the water around them, near misses. 
It's a full-on naval battle as they take down the sister ships in Luxord's 
fleet. Soon they focus their efforts on taking down Luxord's ship. When 
the mast topples over, the battle is nearly won)

Jack: Prepare to board!

(They launch their arrow-shaped anchor into the ship and use the chain to 
board)

Luxord: Another game it is, then.

(Luxord snaps his fingers summoning a group of Heartless and Nobodies, and 
retreats into the ship. Once the battle is over, Luxord reappears, clapping)

Luxord: Magnificent! I salute you all, gentlemen.

Sora (scowling): You're up to something.

Donald: Admit it!

Luxord: Perish the thought. I know when I've been outdone.

Jack: You were outdone before you even started, mate. But I admire your 
conciliatory way of conceding defeat.

(Luxord quickly brushes away the polite insult)

Luxord: Yes... Now, I believe I owe you your prize. But I neglected to 
ask what it is that you want. Perhaps...you'll enlighten me?

Jack: Aye, that's easy. I want the chest that's aboard the Dutchman.

Goofy: No, Jack, don't tell him!

(There is an awkward pause)

Luxord: Really?

(Jack has half-way realized his mistake)

Jack: Not good?

(Sora realizes)

Sora: Oh, Jaaack...

(Sora, Donald and Goofy summon their weapons)

Jack: Well...I didn't tell him WHICH Dutchman.

(Jack draws his sword and Donald glares at Luxord)

Donald: You tricked him!

Luxord: Actually, I outwitted him.

Sora: You knew he'd tell you where it was!

Luxord (chuckling): I've always been far more interested in the long game. 
Now, let's see where it takes us. That is, if you stay apace.

(Luxord disappears into a corridor of darkness. Sora hears a buzzing off 
to his right)

Sora: Huh?

(A group of Vaporfly Heartless swoop in and knock the party back onto the 
Leviathan. Sora gets up, rushing to the edge of the deck, and sees that 
Luxord's ship has vanished)

Sora: After him!

(He starts to run for the helm)

Jack: Nay. There's no point.

Sora (stopping): Why not?

Jack: The ship's listing near to scuppers from that cannon fire. She'll be 
needing repairs. Best make berth at Port Royal.

Sora: Whaaat?

(They dock at Port Royal and walk up the marina)

Jack: Look for crabs. They'll set her right.

Sora: Crabs? Why crabs?

Jack: Never mind the particulars, mate. The white crabs. Savvy?

Sora: Aye, aye.

(They search Port Royal from top to bottom for the elusive white crabs. 
After gathering a sufficient amount, they return to the Leviathan)

Jack: Aye, that's all of 'em. Now, to my final task. Be back in a trice.

(Jack leaves momentarily and brings the ship back to shipshape)

Jack: There, mates. Fit to sail any sea. Now, Sora, one final inquiry: is 
there any particular reason you wanted this ship?

(Sora's eyes widen at the question and he thinks on it)

Sora: Yeah, to explore the seas, free as the wind.

Jack: Good answer. You ARE a pirate... Captain Sora.

(Sora smiles for a moment)

Sora: But, Jack...why do you keep saying "final," like you're leaving?

Jack: Ah... It's because THIS me has run his course, mate.

(Three white crabs fall from his body and one scuttles away, catching 
Donald's attention)

Sora: "This" you?

Jack: Aye, the surrogate me that the goddess of the sea sent here to help 
you lot. Of course, any me is still me. I may be duplicatable, but I'm 
always incomparable. The sea, she smiles upon us, Sora--and let's leave it 
at that, shall we? For now, the REAL me has a crucial engagement...at 
Shipwreck Cove, where the Pirate Brethren will meet Beckett and his lot in 
battle to win back our freedom.

Sora: Then let us help.

(Donald and Goofy nod)

Jack: No, it's for pirates to resolve. But not you, Sora.

(Jack begins to glow)

Jack: You're as free as the winds now, and far you'll go.

(Jack explodes into a burst of light, leaving behind a pile of white crabs. 
They settle on the dock and splash down into the water. The trio watch them 
go)

Goofy: So, Jack was showin' us the way.

Donald: Even if he did get tricked.

Sora: Jack... He said it was the pirates' battle to fight.

(He smiles brightly)

Sora: But a fight for pirates...

(He gets Donald and Goofy to join him)

Sora, Donald & Goofy: ...is a fight for us!

(The three of them punch the sky)

Sora: C'mon! Let's find the real Jack!

(Before meeting in battle, on a sparkling white strip of sand, Captain 
Jack Sparrow, Elizabeth, and Barbossa walk away from a longboat beached on 
one side, toward a second longboat on the other side. The threesome draw 
near to the three others who have docked: Cutler Beckett, Davy Jones and 
Will Turner. Jonas, as per his curse by the goddess Calypso, stands in a 
bucket of water. They regard each other in silence; this is an attempt at 
parley)

Beckett: You made a deal with me, Jack, to deliver the pirates. And here 
they are. Don't be bashful. Step up. Claim your reward.

(Elizabeth and Barbossa look to their left at Jack, who looks to his left, 
too. He makes no effort to corroborate Beckett's words)

Davy Jones: Sparrow. Your debt to me is still to be satisfied. One hundred 
years in servitude aboard the Dutchman. As a start.

Jack Sparrow: That debt was paid, mate.

Davy Jones: You escaped.

Elizabeth: I propose an exchange.

(Jack turns to Elizabeth and Beckett perks up)

Elizabeth: Will leaves with us...and you can take Jack.

(Barbossa and Sparrow are taken aback by this offer)

Will: Done.

Jack Sparrow: Undone.

Beckett: Done.

Barbossa (to Elizabeth): Jack's one of the nine Pirate Lords. You have no 
right.

Elizabeth (dismissively): King.

(Elizabeth turns away from him to Jack, the reason for her being declared 
Pirate King of the Brethren Court. He smirks and doffs his hat)

Jack Sparrow: As you command, your nibs.

Barbossa: Scurvy blackguard!

(Barbossa draws his sword and slices at Jack, just missing him and tearing 
off the circlet coin that hung from his hair. It falls to the sand and the 
two men regard each other)

Jack Sparrow: Easy there, mate. You wouldn't want to damage the leverage, 
now would you?

(Jack moves to cross and Barbossa picks up the coin with a smirk)

Beckett: Now...

(Will and Jack complete the cross, keeping eyes on each other. Reaching 
Beckett, the lord motions Jack to stand beside Jones. He does so nervously, 
donning his hat, and Jones breathes menacingly in his face. Beckett steps 
forward and Jack saunters to the side making space between him and Jones)

Beckett: Advise your Brethren. You can fight, and all of you will die. Or 
you can not fight, in which case only most of you will die.

(Elizabeth moves closer)

Elizabeth: We will fight. And YOU will die.

(Elizabeth walks away, followed by Will and Barbossa. Meanwhile, Sora, 
Donald and Goofy return to the High Seas and look off to the north, where 
large clouds have begun to gather)

Donald: Look at those clouds!

Goofy: That must be Shipwreck Cove, the place that Jack told us about.

(They sail into the Northern Waters, the wind blowing through Sora's pirate 
garb)

Donald: The water looks turbulent in that direction.

(Nearly to their destination, the fog looms heavy and out sails Luxord's ship)

Sora: Luxord!

Luxord: Ahh, you do know how to make good time. Yes, one must simply marvel 
at your celerity. But, such compulsive behavior is eventually going to 
bring you nothing but sorrow.

(He snaps his fingers and more ships appear around him as his disappears)

Sora: Lost him again.

(Goofy blocks the sun with his hand, seeing the fleet of ships before them)

Goofy: How are we gonna go after him?

Donald: First, get those Heartless!

Sora: Right!

(Sora steers the ship to the right, aiming the starboard cannons in the 
fleet's direction. Keeping the wind in their sails, they target the 
Heartless ships, managing to sink several of them. Once out of range, Sora 
turns again, but the maneuver slows their speed such that they take on 
some cannonfire, sending splinters of wood into the air. Getting the boat 
back on track, they are surrounded, with ships on either side planning to 
cut them off or ram into them. They ready both the port and starboard 
cannons as the wind direction changes, speeding them along. Seeing their 
chance to neutralize the threat if they can pass through to Shipwreck 
Cove faster than the fleet can catch them, they open fire on the enemy, 
sending bursts of wood and sail crashing to the depths of the sea. The 
fog lightens once safety is assured)

Sora: He's plotting to swipe the chest in the heat of battle.

Goofy: To Shipwreck Cove!

Donald: Fast!

(Sora nods. Sailing into Shipwreck Cove, amongst the incredible amount of 
pirate ships Sora spots the Black Pearl as a torrent of crabs flow over 
the sides into the water. Calypso has been freed. Will looks up as the 
Leviathan pulls alongside)

Sora: Guys! Are you okay?

Will: Sora... You're a welcome sight!

(Sora, Donald and Goofy board the Pearl)

Elizabeth: We've all been quite worried about you.

(The sight of a few straggling crabs on the deck catches Sora's eye)

Sora: Isn't that...?

Elizabeth: Sora?

Sora: Where's Jack? And Tia Dalma?

Elizabeth: I'm afraid you've missed a few things while you've been gone.

Will: Jack... He's...he's been taken by Cutler Beckett.

Elizabeth: Yes, and Beckett commands Davy Jones and the Flying Dutchman.

Will: Barbossa thought we could defeat them if we released Calypso, the 
goddess of the sea, who was really Tia Dalma, bound in human form.

(A crab scuttles up to Will's shoe, but quickly turns away from the 
obstruction)

Will: But it didn't work.

Barbossa: Aye, a fickle goddess Calypso be.

Goofy: So what now?

Barbossa: Nothin'. Our final hope has failed us.

(Sora remembers Tia Dalma's words once again)

Tia Dalma: Use that key to free me, Sora, and you have my most certain 
promise--all the power on the sea you ever wish for be yours.

Sora (thinking): So...Tia Dalma was Calypso. She's the one who was helping us.

(He looks down at the crabs)

Sora (thinking): And you know what? I think...that she might just be able 
to help us again.

(He turns to Will and Elizabeth)

Sora: You can't give up now. We can all fight, together.

(Donald and Goofy nod)

Sora: The sea belongs to everyone!

(The hopeful determination coming from Sora is infectious, even catching 
Barbossa's interest)

Donald: I said that. Don't copy my expressions!

Sora: Huh? You did?

(Donald nods vehemently)

Goofy: Sometimes it just goes in one ear and right out the other.

Sora: Wait... Really?

Donald: Yes!

(Elizabeth looks toward the sky, where the wind has picked up. Mr. Gibbs 
follows her gaze, as does Barbossa)

Elizabeth: It's not over. There's still hope for us.

(She turns, walking across the deck past the crew)

Elizabeth: You will listen to me. (shouting) Listen!

(She ascends to the edge of the deck, grabbing hold of the rigging)

Elizabeth: The Brethren will still be looking here to us, to the Black 
Pearl, to lead. And they will see free men and freedom! Our enemy will 
see the flash of our cannons and hear the ring of our swords, and they 
will see the courage of our hearts as we succeed and they fail. Gentlemen... 
Hoist the colours!

Will: Hoist the colours!

Sora: Hoise the colours!

(The rest of the crew release shouts of tenacity)

Goofy: Hooray!

Donald: Oh boy!

(The clouds above begin to rotate and sheets of rain begin to fall. 
Lightning strikes down at the sea as a giant whirpool begins to turn slowly. 
The two formations converge, the Black Pearl outpacing the pirate fleet 
and the Flying Dutchman outpacing the Armada. Between them the sea continues 
to swirl. The two warring ships sail into the maelstrom and ready their 
cannons, the Leviathan following the Pearl. Cannonfire thunders as the two 
ships battle across the abyss. In awe of this spectacle, Sora steers the 
Leviathan as the rain pelts down on him. Luxord appears on the quarterdeck 
and Sora whirls around)

Sora: I knew it was you!

(Luxord walks to the edge of the ship, looking down at Jones's vessel)

Luxord: So that's the Flying Dutchman.

Sora: The chest Jack told you about has the heart of Davy Jones in it. 
There's no way it's the chest that you're looking for!

(Luxord gives a haughty chuckle)

Luxord: No one knows what's in the chest we're looking for. If it's a black 
box, then we are to collect it, simple as that.

Sora: You don't know what's in it? Then why do you need it? How will you 
know you've found it?

Luxord: Got me. Regrettably, the higher-ups haven't deigned to tell us. But 
they did say the box contains "hope."

Sora: Huh?

Luxord: That's all you'll get from me.

(He looks over at the Black Pearl, still firing on the Dutchman)

Luxord: Hmm, it's far to chaotic to find the box like this. Perhaps I'll 
remove that ship from the picture.

(He snaps his fingers and the boat lurches upward as thick, slithering 
tentacles rise out of the water surrounding the Black Pearl. The crew dives 
out of the way as they crash down onto the deck. Barbossa holds tight to 
the helm as the ship is lifted high into the air by the Kraken. Sora's eyes 
grow wide)

Luxord: Now, this should afford me time to look.

(Luxord vanishes in a corridor of darkness)

Sora: THEY'RE looking for hope?

Donald: Hey! 

Goofy: Will and the others need us!

Sora: Yeah, I know!

(Sora maneuvers the Leviathan alongside the Kraken in an attempt to free 
the Black Pearl from its clutches. The Flying Dutchman uses this 
opportunity to fire on the Leviathan, expecting the Pearl to be crushed 
by the sea monster. Meanwhile, Jack has secretly escaped the brig on the 
Flying Dutchman and gotten his hands on the chest. He stops as Luxord 
appears before him)

Luxord: So, you got what you want. Perhaps you're the better player among 
us. However, I must demand you give THAT to me.

Jack Sparrow: Pardon? You must be mistaken, mate. I'll not be giving you 
anything.

Luxord: Then I invoke the right of parle--

(Jack walks right up to him, wagging a finger in his face)

Jack Sparrow: Uhp, no! No parley.

(He presses further, causing Luxord to step back)

Jack Sparrow: Look around. We're a little busy.

(He nearly pins Luxord to the overboard railing and holds up the chest)

Jack Sparrow: And besides, I've already got all that I want, mate.

(He breathes directly in Luxord's face. The stench is unbearable and causes 
Luxord to fall from the ship into the water. Jack cups a hand to his mouth 
and breathes again, slightly coughing himself)

Jack Sparrow: Yup. Still works.

(He walks further down the deck and comes face to face with--Davy Jones. 
Jack reels back in surprise)

Davy Jones: Jack Sparrow... Are you lost? Prisoners don't belong on deck. 
Your station is in the brig!

(Jones swings his arm, or tentacle rather, and Jack starts to run as Sora, 
Donald and Goofy have come aboard the Dutchman)

Sora: We're here!

(They jump down to the deck between Jack and Davy Jones, and summon their 
weapons. Jack turns to see them and laughs, unsheathing his sword)

Jack Sparrow: Tables have turned, mate.

(Lightning flashes)

Davy Jones: Hardly. Just a few more maggots to join my crew!

(They attack the captain of the Dutchman getting in a few successful hits 
before the cursed pirate sinks into his ship)

Davy Jones: Over here!

(He reemerges from the crow's nest above, cackling, as the tentacles of the 
Kraken rise up around the ship, swiping at Sora and the others. One tentacle 
spirals around Donald and squeezes him)

Davy Jones: Hahah! Fish food!

(Sora rushes up the stairs and strikes down the squirming appendage, 
releasing Donald from its grasp. Davy Jones returns to the deck as the 
Kraken retreats, but is knocked back by Jack Sparrow)

Jack Sparrow: Care to surrender?

(Davy Jones growls at him, rushing forward with his sword. Jack jumps 
back, knocking away Jones's blows, until the swords cross at a standstill)

Davy Jones: The chest. Hand it over!

Sora: Jack!

(Sora tries rushing at them)

Davy Jones: Stay out of this, boy!

(A tentacle crashes down to the deck in front of Sora, stopping him in his 
tracks, and a second one emerges from behind, trapping the three inside. The 
two ships are drawn closer in an ever-tightening circle as Jack and Davy 
Jones spar. The fight takes them to the yard atop the mainsail where they 
exchange sword blows. The giant masts of the two ships tilt toward each 
other before slamming together. Jack loses his balance and the chest falls, 
just as Will swings to the deck from the Black Pearl. He bends and picks up 
the chest, running across the deck as a tentacle emerges from the floor. It 
slithers beside him and knocks him over, spilling the chest from his hands 
to the rain-soaked floor. Davy Jones jumps down to the deck, walking towards 
the chest, when Jack drops drown in front of him. They strike each other 
with their swords and Jack moves so the ship's capstan is between them. Jack 
and Jones try to fake the other out in which direction to go around the 
capstan before Jones realizes the game's folly. Jones walks THROUGH the 
capstan, alarming Jack. He leaps from the capstan slashing at Jack, who 
knocks the sword down, before swinging back at Jones with his own. In a 
quick movement, Jones grabs Jack's sword with the large claw that is his 
left hand. Jack tries to push back, but Davy Jones cleaves his sword in two 
and punches Jack hard in the face with the same claw. Jack lands hard on 
the deck as Elizabeth swings in between Jones and the chest)

Davy Jones: Harridan! You'll see no mercy from me.

Elizabeth: That's why I brought this!

(She draws her sword as Will awakens. He looks over, seeing Elizabeth 
knocked away against the stairs, dropping her sword. As Jones moves in for 
the kill, he is run through with a sword by Will)

Jones: Missed. Did you forget? I am a heartless wretch!

(Jones looks back at him before swinging around and kicking him in the face 
with his peg leg. Elizabeth brushes her wet hair out of her eyes as Will 
squirms on the deck of the Dutchman, weaponless. His eyes shift toward 
Elizabeth. Davy Jones looks from Will to Elizabeth)

Davy Jones: Ah. Love. A dreadful bond. And yet, so easily severed.

(Jones lurches across the deck toward Will)

Sora: That's not true!

(Jones looks over to see Sora, Donald and Goofy)

Sora: I may still have a lot to learn about love, but I know what it means 
to share my heart with others. And it will take more than you to break a 
bond like that.

(Sora's words taste bitter in Jones's mouth)

Davy Jones: What does a whelp like you know about the heart?

(Jack arrives)

Jack Sparrow: The whelp has seen far more of the world than you know.

Davy Jones: Ha! What of it?

(Jones raises his sword to Will's neck)

Davy Jones: Tell me, William Turner: do you fear death?

Jack Sparrow: Do you?

(Jones turns, seeing Jack with the chest open, his broken sword aimed at 
Jones's still-beating heart. Above, Vexen watches the scene unfold)

Vexen: How disappointing. So this is all they meant when they said "heart." 
We've been chasing the wrong box this whole time.

(He angrily whisks away)

Jack Sparrow: Heady tonic, holding life and death in the palm of one's hand.

Davy Jones: You're a cruel man, Jack Sparrow.

Jack Sparrow: Cruel is a matter of perspective.

Davy Jones: Is it?

(Without hesitation, Jones stabs Will Turner and cackles. Sora screams, 
leaping at him along with Donald and Goofy as Jack looks at Will, mortally 
wounded. Sora punches Jones in the face as Elizabeth races toward Will)

Elizabeth: Will? Will? Look at me. Look at me!

(Jones knocks Donald and Goofy off of him before grabbing at Sora and doing 
the same)

Davy Jones: You will not forestall my judgment!

(As he moves to strike Sora, he feels a sudden shooting pain and cries out 
in anguish. He blinks, looking back toward Will. Jones's heart has been 
stabbed. By Jack's shortened sword. And Will's hand is on the sword hilt. 
Davy Jones stumbles back, his mortality returning, and he falls over the 
rail, plummeting down into the sea, at one with Calypso at last. Barbossa 
is at the wheel of the Pearl)

Barbossa: She's taking us down! Make quick, or it's the Locker for us all!

(The ships spin. The point of no return. On the Dutchman, Elizabeth weeps 
over Will's body)

Sora: Jack, can't we save him?

Jack Sparrow: Part of the ship, part of the crew. The Dutchman must have a 
captain.

(Jack grabs Elizabeth, pulling her away from Will)

Jack Sparrow: Elizabeth, say good-bye.

Elizabeth: No! I won't leave you!

(She struggles briefly, but the grief is overwhelming. They escape to the 
Black Pearl once the ship wrenches free from the Dutchman and Will and the 
ship vanish into the whirlpool. The maelstrom ends as they regroup with the 
crew aboard the Pearl)

Gibbs: Thank goodness, Jack. The armada's still out there. The Endeavour's 
coming up hard to starboard. And I think it's time we embrace that oldest 
and noblest of pirate traditions.

(His hands mimic the act of running away)

Jack Sparrow: Never actually been one for tradition.

(Mr. Gibbs and Elizabeth watch as Jack moves toward the wheel)

Jack Sparrow: In we go!

(On the Endeavour, Beckett sees the Black Pearl, sails luffing, helpless. 
Below him on the gun deck, the cannon ports open and the cannons emerge)

Beckett: It's nothing personal, Jack. It's just good business.

(The armada reforms behind him and Beckett sails in for the kill. Suddenly, 
the Flying Dutchman breaks the water's surface, up from the depths, sailing 
alongside the Black Pearl. A clean slate gray, no longer encrusted. On the 
deck, William Turner puts his hands on the helm, a dark, avenging anger in 
his eyes, now in control of the Flying Dutchman)

Will: Ready on the guns.

(Elizabeth smiles)

Jack Sparrow: Full canvas!

Barbossa: Aye! Full canvas!

(Will turns the wheel of the Dutchman as Barbossa does the same with the 
Pearl. On the Endeavour, Beckett's smile fades as the Dutchman and the 
Pearl split, sailing to either side of the Endeavour, trapping it between)

Jack Sparrow: Fire!

Gibbs: Fiiire!

Will: Fire!

Barbossa: Fiiiiiire!

Elizabeth: Fire aaall!

(The Dutchman and the Black Pearl open fire and we see the full fury of 
these two ships for the first time. Cannons blast and blast and blast, the 
crew on the Endeavour screaming in the furious broadside. Beckett stares in 
disbelief as his ship is blown to pieces)

Beckett: It's just...good business.

(A mast falls and the deck gives way, the Endeavour sinking into the 
Caribbean. On the Black Pearl, the crew cheers. Donald and Goofy share a 
fist bump)

Donald: We did it!

(Sora looks back at Elizabeth, who is staring out at the Dutchman)

Gibbs: The Flying Dutchman must have a captain. Just wed, and now she and 
Cap'n Turner must live in different worlds.

(Will's gaze is drawn back to Elizabeth)

Gibbs: One day ashore, ten years at sea. It's a steep price.

Sora: Will...

(Gibbs walks up to Elizabeth)

Gibbs: Your chariot awaits, Your Highness.

(She smiles, walking over to the crew gathered on deck. Barbossa addresses

Barbossa: Mrs. Turner.

(She walks up to Sora, Donald and Goofy)

Donald: Elizabeth...

Goofy: Take care.

(She walks up to Jack Sparrow)

Elizabeth: Jack...

(She smiles)

Elizabeth: Thank you.

(She leaves)

Sora: One day isn't enough time.

Jack Sparrow: There's always enough time for hearts to say what's true. 
Sora, you know better than anyone. It only takes a moment to connect with 
your mates... With your hearties.

Sora: There's always enough time. And I'm going to find them.

(Behind them, the Leviathan's magic wears off and it bursts into thousands 
of white crabs that sink into the ocean. Meanwhile, Axel sits alone in the 
Secret Forest in his usual black coat)

Kairi: Hey, Axel!

(He turns to see Kairi in her new outfit)

Axel: Hey. Liking the look.

(She giggles, showing it off)

Axel: Cut your hair, too.

Kairi: Mm-hmm. So, you gonna try yours on?

Axel: Uhh...I dunno. Maybe later.

Kairi: But you always wear the same thing.

Axel: If it ain't broke, don't fix it. This is how you pick me out of a 
crowd. I make myself easy to remember.

Kairi: How thoughtful.

Axel: Nah, not really...

(He scratches his head and she giggles, sitting down next to him)

Kairi: Our training's almost finished.

Axel: Yeah...

Kairi: Somewhere inside me is Namin. If we can free Roxas, we can free her 
too.

Axel: I guess so.

Kairi: Namin was made when Sora freed me from his heart. So, now that she's 
a part of me again, I figured all was right. But she can't look at this 
forest, feel the wind on her face, none of it. And if she could, it would be 
different for her. Her time was short, but she lived it, and that makes it 
hers. What right did I have to take those feelings and experiences back? 
They don't belong to me. Nothing's as it should be. Not for her OR Roxas.

(Axel takes in her words, agreeing)

Axel: I know.

(He pauses)

Axel: Way back when I was a kid, I met this other weird kid. Somehow we 
became fast friends. Never saw him again--nearly forgot about him, too. 
Then, I met Roxas. Couldn't believe it. The two of 'em were identical. Oh, 
I didn't tell Roxas. Didn't want HIM to go vanishing on me, too.

(He leans back on his hands)

Axel: The kid's name was Ventus. He's one of the lost Keyblade wielders 
we're looking for. Think he's still got ME memorized?

Kairi: Oh yeah. Very memorized.

(She points to her head and he laughs softly)

Axel: Now that we're going back, I'm worried about everything.

Kairi: Well, you don't have to worry alone anymore, Axel.

(He smiles at her. In the Dark World, Mickey and Riku are fighting the Demon 
Tower once again with their repaired Keyblades. The tower strikes at Riku 
twice, but he dodges before it slams into the ground, forcing him to jump 
away. The Shadows scramble across the sand as Riku catches his breath. From 
behind him, the energy rebuilds)

Mickey: Riku, look!

(The Demon Tower wriggles in the air, bending over and twisting into Riku, 
knocking the Keyblade from his arms. It dissipates when it hits the sand)

Mickey (gasping): Riku!

(The swarm of Heartless knocks Mickey off his feet and he also drops his 
Keyblade, consumed by the swarm. Riku lifts himself up)

Riku: Mickey!

(In the Woods of Twilight Town, just outside the Old Mansion, a corridor of 
darkness appears and Ansem, Seeker of Darkness strolls out of it, followed 
by Ansem the Wise. From behind a tree, Hayner, Pence and Olette watch)

Pence (more excited than impatient): It's about time!

(Hayner covers Pence's mouth)

Hayner: Heeey, shut it! C'mon.

(He moves ahead as the two skulk behind him. As both Ansems walk into the 
courtyard, the trio peek out from behind the gate. Ansem the Wise stops 
just before the entrance door, forcing Ansem to turn around)

Ansem: What now?

(Ansem the Wise looks up to the curtained window)

Ansem the Wise: Please. I have created enough victims.

Ansem: Yes, you have. All the children sacrificed in the name of your 
research... So make things right.

Ansem the Wise: I told you I did not take her. Her disappearance was why I 
put a stop to the research.

Ansem: And that makes you honorable? You used Roxas and Namin and threw

and hid her. Now, show me the data you are hiding here.

Ansem the Wise: Roxas and Namin... If there is any reason that I still 
draw breath, it is to atone for what I did to them.

(Olette and Pence gasp)

Pence: He said "Roxas."

Hayner: Yeah.

Olette: That man needs us.

Hayner: Right.

Pence: Yeah.

Ansem the Wise: If you do find the girl, what is it that you expect will 
happen?
Ansem: The child's memory holds a mystery to unravel--one concerning the 
battle we seek between light and darkness. You know something and that...
is why you stopped the experiments.

Ansem the Wise: You are completely deluded, Xehanort.

Ansem: We shall soon see.

(He grabs Ansem the Wise's shoulder and pushes him toward the door before 
Pence pops in)

Pence: Yoo-hoo!

(Ansem stops)

Pence: 'Scuse meee!

(Ansem whirls around at this interruption)

Ansem: Who are you?

Pence: Oh, well, I'm looking for a friend who used to live here.

(His distraction enables Olette to run inside the courtyard)

Ansem: No one lives here. Begone.

Pence (stalling): But sir...

(He starts to approach them)

Ansem: No, no, no! Not one more step. Get out!

(As he walks toward Pence, Olette rushes and grabs Ansem the Wise)

Olette (whispering): This way!

(Ansem spins around, seeing Ansem the Wise escaping as Hayner runs in, 
attempting to jump kick him from behind)

Hayner: Hey, loser!

(The Dark Figure emerges from behind Ansem and catches Hayner in its grip)

Hayner: ...or not!

Pence: Hayner!

(The Dark Figure tosses Hayner at the brick wall of the courtyard but a 
strange white blob curls around him and cushions the blow. He bounces to 
the ground safely. More white blobs fly through the air from behind corners, 
like wispy trails. They surround Ansem and the Dark Figure, revealing

Pence: The squiggly things?

(It uncurls from Hayner as he sits up in disbelief)

Hayner: They...protected me.

(Pence grabs Hayner's arm)

Pence: Hayner! Get a move on!

Hayner: Oh... Okay.

(Pence helps Hayner up and the two run back to the Woods. Ansem focuses his 
attention on the Dusks)

Ansem: I serve the Organization. This is treason.

(He sneers)

Ansem: I see what is happening. Have it your way then.

(Olette and Ansem the Wise escape to the Underground and Hayner and Pence 
catch up)

Olette: Are you guys okay?

(They catch their breath)

Hayner: Yeah, I think.

Pence: Nobody knows the twists and turns of Twilight Town better than us.

Ansem the Wise: You are Roxas's friends.

Hayner: That's right. So you know him, too?

Ansem the Wise: Oh yes. Quite well.

Pence: Pay dirt. Guess it was worth staking out the old mansion after all, 
because this guy here is what I call a lead.

(He reaches into his pocket and takes out the photo of them together with 
Roxas)

Olette: That's the only proof we have that Roxas was our friend.

Hayner: Tell us about him. We wanna know him better.

?????: My dear master. You are safe.

(A cloaked man enters behind them)

Hayner: Who's there?

(They whirl around, seeing the scientist with blond hair)

Ansem the Wise: Even, is that you? So...those Nobodies were your doing.

(The wispy blobs float in behind Vexen and become Dusks again. Their 
appearance unsettles the trio. However, Vexen bows his head)

Vexen: I have been waiting for this. Gave up a normal life in order to plant 
myself in the Organization. And when I heard Xehanort had gone looking for 
you, I realized it was my chance to find you as well. For you see, I, too, 
wish to atone.

(Sora, Donald and Goofy leave the Caribbean and travel to a world of science

Sora: Oh, wow!

Sora: Cool!

Sora: Aww, but I wanna take a look at the big city!

Goofy: Yeah, it does seem pretty exciting.

Goofy: The Heartless!

????: Go Go! You okay?

Sora: What in...

Hiro: Let's go, Baymax!

(Baymax shoots forward with his rocket boots, his wings engaged. The group

scattered between the cars. Sora slides to avoid their rocket fire and

Goofy: Sora! Go from car to car!

Donald: Look above you!

(Sora slides between cars, sniping the Pole Cannons. A great stomping quakes

Donald: Look!

(A yellow car becomes a missile swung by the Metal Troll's mighty axe,

Sora: It tried to crush us!

(It hones in on Sora, roaring at him)

Baymax: You may reduce the risk of injury, by seeking cover.

(Together, they defeat the Metal Troll and regroup in Hiro's Garage. The

"MYSTERIOUS MONSTERS ATTACK!

Crisis struck San Fransokyo today when a 
horde of unidentified creatures attacked 
the populace without warning.
Local superteam Big Hero 6 was nearly 
deep-sixed when they came to the rescue, 
raising questions about just how prepared 
they are to protect the city.
Will another group of crimefighters rise up 
in our hour of need? Or is there no force 
capable of containing this new threat?
In the opinion of this humble reporter, the 
city's days are numbered, so grab your 
wallets, keys, kids, and pets, and get your 
kiesters to the airport before it's too late.")

Go Go: Not cool.

Honey Lemon: People like spectacle, not truth.

Wasabi: Yeah, who needs quality reporting when you can just make stuff up?

Fred: I don't get it. I mean, didn't they see how awesome we were?! Sure,

(They head to the city. Sora rides on Baymax as he flies past a fish-shaped

pitched squeal and they shoot forward with his rocket boots, curving through

Hiro: Okay, guys. Go through the rings and head for the goal.

Honey Lemon: Don't you just LOVE chemistry?

(Sora airsteps off the building, flying through the rings to the windsocks 
hanging in the air as Baymax flies ahead. Sora catches up to Baymax)

Baymax: You are near the goal.

(Proceeding further, Sora reaches for a virtual star high above a building 
and Baymax catches him on the way down. Later, Sora runs down the street

post ahead, surprising her. He jumps from the post to a building and begins 
running up the side, magical blue dust eminating from him. She stops, 
watching him run)

Go Go: Interesting. Gravity--not binding.

(A virtual Tireblade Heartless in flight mode swoops down at Sora and his

Wasabi: Hey, wait. My laser hands...

(He looks down at his energy-covered gauntlets)

Wasabi: ...can be projectiles!

(Honey Lemon hides near a group of virtual Pole Cannon Heartless, thinking 
up a strategy to defeat them, while Sora reaches the edge of the building 
and changes his Keyblade to the Magic Launcher, striking the enemies with 
a charged cannon)

Honey Lemon: Ooh! Change the weapon, change the attack.

(Sora runs ahead into a group of Tireblade Heartless. He jumps to the 
right ascending the building as the Heartless engage their flight mode and 
follow him. Sora aims his Keyblade and releases a Blizzara spell, 
shattering the Tireblades, as Fred watches from below)

Fred: Whoa. A freeze attack!

(He looks down at his claws)

Fred: Fire...and ice. Diametrically opposed...or SO WE THOUGHT!

(He takes off excitedly and Sora hops down)

Hiro: Thanks, Sora. That should be enough data. And I think you sparked 
some new ideas.

Go Go: Yeah! Hiro, I think there's a way to--

(They all start talking at once in Sora's ear. He winces at first, but smiles)

Fred: Hey, are you listening?

(Back in Hiro's Garage, Hiro is enthusiastically typing at his computer, 
creating updates for his pals' gear. Goofy and Honey Lemon create new 
elemental combinations for her chem-balls. Wasabi praises Hiro on his 
new gauntlets and Donald imagines having one of his own. Fred gives 
Hiro difficult specifications for his suit, but Sora comes up with an 
easier solution. The data from Sora is updated for Baymax to use and 
Hiro ejects the data chip from the drive. He walks up to Baymax and 
presses the port on the robot's chest. It opens, displaying Baymax's 
chip slots. Hiro inserts the updated battle chip into Baymax and the 
port closes)

Hiro: That...should do it.

(The video on Hiro's computer suddenly broadcasts a news update)

Action 7 News: We interrupt your scheduled program to deliver this 
breaking news. Moments ago, the city's South District was attacked by 
numerous unidentified creatures.

(They rush to the screen, seeing Heartless marching through the city)

Action 7 News: Witnesses describe losing sight of victims during the 
mayhem. Many also said they saw strange, floating heart symbols in the

home. For those just joining us, only minutes ago the South District was 
attacked by--

(Hiro closes the broadcast and turns to Sora, who nods)

Sora & Hiro: Go time.

(The rest of the group agree. They make it to the South District, where

Donald: Heartless!

Hiro: Sora, above you!

(Sora looks up and his AR Device searches for a target. A large shape is 
moving on the roof of a building)

Hiro: I'm picking up some kind of threat.

Sora: Okay, I'll check it out.

Hiro: Run up the buildings if you have to. Watch out for those enemies on 
the building.

(They fight the Heartless from the ground to the roof, where they're 
surrounded by Mechanitaur Heartless. They take the group out and Sora 
dispels his Keyblade)

Sora: Piece of cake.

Hiro: Wait, Sora! Something big's coming your way.

(There is a large crash in the middle of the city as a titanic Catastro-
chorus Heartless stomps through. It eyes a green car on the road and chases

citizens screaming for their lives. Baymax flies over carrying Sora, Donald 
and Goofy as the giant dinosaur-like Heartless bellows loudly. They spot

Sora: Gotcha! I'll take care of it.

(Baymax's rocket boots engage and he swoops down with a superhero landing,

Hiro: That thing's massive! Stop it, or it's gonna wreck the city!

(The dangerous dino sends huge fireballs from the volcano on its back as

Hiro: The target's moved up onto one of the buildings. You gotta go after

(They take care of the smaller Heartless that pop up to bar their way to

Sora returns to ground level, scanning for more threats as Go Go is being 
chased by a small group of Heartless)

Go Go: Just try and catch me.

(She speeds ahead, charging her magnetic disks from the friction against

persuing her. Smirking, she tosses a disk, which slices through the 
Heartless near the ground before flying back to her arm, and drops back

Honey Lemon (excitedly): I've got an idea!

(She tosses a purple chem-ball at the Heartless which bursts into a purple 
cloud of smoke)

Wasabi: Hey!

(She starts typing in a new combination into her purse)

Wasabi: I can't aim if I can't see!

(Out from her purse comes a red chem-ball and she smiles, tossing it 
into the cloud. It turns into a solid block of purple hexagons, trapping

Honey Lemon: Better?

Wasabi: Much better.

(She smiles at him and he aims his gauntlets to the ground, destroying

Fred: Freeze!

(Fred blows a torrent of icy wind from the mouth of his monster suit, 
freezing the Heartless in place. Then, switching to fire, becomes a human

Fred: Whuh? Oh, I get it...

(He jumps into the air, now spewing out fire and ice together, eliminating 
the Heartless flying above him)

Fred: It's a combo move!

(Up in the sky, Baymax flies in, engaging the rocket boosters on his

in front of Sora, who grits his teeth and takes it down in one strike. The

Sora: Nice, Baymax!

(Baymax raises a fist)

Sora: What?

Baymax: Now, we fist bump.

Sora: Fist bump?

Baymax: To display excitement. Hiro taught it to me.

Sora: So, like...this?

(Sora taps his fist against Baymax's, while Donald does the same with Goofy's)

Baymax: Bah-la-la-la-la-la-la.

(Baymax flutters his fingers upward in the air)

Sora: Bah-la-la-la-la-la-la?

(Sora, Donald, and Goofy do the same with confused looks. Suddenly, a Metal 
Troll drops from the building behind them. The three summons their weapons)

Goofy: Get ready!

(They rush forward)

Sora: Another one?!

Honey Lemon: We're here!

(They turn to see Hiro, Fred, Wasabi, and Honey Lemon ready to fight)

Wasabi: Ugh! Can't we pick on one our own size?

(Go Go rolls in)

Go Go: It looks the right size to me.

Fred: Watch me scorch 'em with my freeze-nado! The only tornado made of 
ice AND fire.

Sora: Prepare to face Keyblade Hero 3!

Hiro: And the crime fighting team of Big Hero 6! Together, we're unstoppable.

(They run forward and clash with the Metal Troll. Later, the group relaxes

bars. Fred jumps around Donald, excited)

Fred: Was that awesome...or was that TOTALLY AWESOME?! Haha! Jumping!

Donald: Yeah, I was pretty good.

Honey Lemon: Your magic is amazing. Do you think I could study it sometime?

Donald: Why not?

Goofy: You just made Donald's day.

(Honey Lemon giggles. They sit and watch the sunset)

Hiro: My brother wanted to help people. Now, we try to do the same.

Sora: Your brother?

Hiro (looking down): Yeah, Tadashi. There was a fire, and now he's gone.

(Go Go shares Hiro's grief)

Hiro: But he always wanted to make a difference. He cared about people. 
That's why he worked so hard to create Baymax.

Sora: I'm sorry.

(Hiro and Sora take bites of their ice cream)

Hiro: He's still here. In Baymax. In all of us.

Sora: Tadashi--he lives on in your hearts.

Hiro: Yeah. Right. He will always be a part of us in some way.

(Sora leans back)

Sora: And when you're not strong enough, he'll make up the difference.

(Morning bells ring and Sora becomes Roxas as Hayner, Pence and Olette eat 
sea-salt ice cream beside him, if only for a moment)

Hiro: Sora. You okay?

Sora: Yeah. Fine.

(Hiro takes another bite as Sora looks down at his hand, coming to his 
senses, and places it over his heart)

Sora: I'm with you.

(Later at night, the friends walk through the city together. Fred stretches

Sora: What?!

Goofy: What's that?

(They see a jellyfish-shaped cluster of blocks floating through the air)

Go Go: Great, they're back.

Wasabi: Oh, we got this.

(Fred closes his hood and jumps ahead)

Fred: Cheee-aaarge!

Hiro: Wait! Uh, guys! That one's not like the others!

(They fail to hear him)

Hiro: It can't be. Microbots?

Sora: Microbots? You know what they are?

Goofy: Well, they're different from Heartless.

Donald: Uh-huh.

Hiro: Microbots are designed to do whatever you think via a neural

(He trails off upon seeing their ever-more confused faces)

Hiro: They're kind of a mini-bot I invented. Some bad stuff happened and

Hiro: Could it be?

Donald: You bet!

Sora: We need you on the sciency stuff.

Hiro: They're not microbots... Be careful!

Sora: It's no fair! Why can't we hurt it?

Wasabi: Now he tells us.

Hiro: Wasabi! What happened?

Sora, Donald & Goofy: We got it!

Sora: Time to go, Baymax!

Baymax: All right.

Hiro: Cool. Good luck!

(In the Central District they reach Honey Lemon's indicator, but don't see

Sora: Honey Lemon!

Honey Lemon: Hey, Sora? I think I'm stuck. See if you can find the residue

(Sora leaps over a high-powered fan, which sends him soaring over the

Wasabi: Finally! Thanks for the save, Sora. I'll see if anyone else needs

Go Go: Sora! C'mon, hurry!

Fred: Yeah!

Hiro: Glad you're okay, Fred. Listen, Sora! The Darkubes have converged

Sora: Nah, it's okay, Hiro. We're on it.

Hiro: Thanks.

Donald: Get a move on!

(The Darkubes resemble fireflies as they float in the air of the South

Go Go: Okay, there's a lot of them.

Goofy: What do ya suppose they'll do?

Wasabi: I don't think we wanna find out.

(Fred hops closer)

Fred: I say we destroy this thing!

Donald: Yeah!

Honey Lemon: But without a strategy, we'd just be wasting our strength.

Sora: If we knew where to strike...

Hiro: Sora! I got it! I'm sending you an AR software update. It'll show you 
where the core is--the Darkubes' weak point. I'm coming to help.

Sora: Huh? That's weird. Is it busted?

(He attempts to press the button on his headset, but it has no effect. 
Looking ahead, he sees a cloaked figure walking in his direction)

Sora: Hiro, who's that on the display?

Goofy: That's not the display. He's really here.

Sora: Huh?

Go Go: The black coat... He's back?

????: Are you done messing around?
